From Passive Observer to Active Critic: Reinforcement Learning Elicits Process Reasoning for Robotic Manipulation
Authors: Yibin Liu, Yaxing Lyu, Daqi Gao, Zhixuan Liang, Weiliang Tang, Shilong Mu, Xiaokang Yang, Yao Mu
First: 2026-03-16T17:53:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:53:28+00:00
Comments: 31 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurate process supervision remains a critical challenge for long-horizon robotic manipulation. A primary bottleneck is that current video MLLMs, trained primarily under a Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) paradigm, function as passive "Observers" that recognize ongoing events rather than evaluating the current state relative to the final task goal. In this paper, we introduce PRIMO R1 (Process Reasoning Induced Monitoring), a 7B framework that transforms video MLLMs into active "Critics". We leverage outcome-based Reinforcement Learning to incentivize explicit Chain-of-Thought generation for progress estimation. Furthermore, our architecture constructs a structured temporal input by explicitly anchoring the video sequence between initial and current state images. Supported by the proposed PRIMO Dataset and Benchmark, extensive experiments across diverse in-domain environments and out-of-domain real-world humanoid scenarios demonstrate that PRIMO R1 achieves state-of-the-art performance. Quantitatively, our 7B model achieves a 50% reduction in the mean absolute error of specialized reasoning baselines, demonstrating significant relative accuracy improvements over 72B-scale general MLLMs. Furthermore, PRIMO R1 exhibits strong zero-shot generalization on difficult failure detection tasks. We establish state-of-the-art performance on RoboFail benchmark with 67.0% accuracy, surpassing closed-source models like OpenAI o1 by 6.0%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从被动观察者到主动评判者：强化学习激发机器人操作的过程推理
精确的过程监督仍是长时程机器人操作的关键挑战。当前主要瓶颈在于，现有视频多模态大语言模型主要在监督微调范式下训练，仅作为被动“观察者”识别进行中的事件，而非评估当前状态相对于最终任务目标的进展。本文提出PRIMO R1（过程推理诱导监控）——一个70亿参数的框架，将视频多模态大语言模型转化为主动“评判者”。我们利用基于结果的强化学习激励显式的思维链生成以进行进度估计。此外，该架构通过将视频序列显式锚定在初始状态与当前状态图像之间，构建了结构化时序输入。基于提出的PRIMO数据集与基准测试，在多样域内环境及域外真实世界人形机器人场景中的大量实验表明，PRIMO R1实现了最先进的性能。量化数据显示，我们的70亿参数模型将专业推理基线的平均绝对误差降低50%，相对720亿参数通用多模态大语言模型实现显著精度提升。PRIMO R1在困难故障检测任务上展现出强大的零样本泛化能力，在RoboFail基准测试中以67.0%准确率创下新纪录，较OpenAI o1等闭源模型提升6.0%。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of current video MLLMs, which act as passive observers in long-horizon robotic manipulation by merely recognizing events rather than actively evaluating progress toward task goals. To overcome this, the authors introduce PRIMO R1, a 7B framework that transforms video MLLMs into active critics using outcome-based reinforcement learning to incentivize explicit Chain-of-Thought reasoning for progress estimation, with a structured temporal input anchoring video between initial and current states. Experimental results show state-of-the-art performance, including a 50% reduction in mean absolute error compared to specialized baselines and strong zero-shot generalization, achieving 67.0% accuracy on the RoboFail benchmark, surpassing larger models like OpenAI o1 by 6.0%.
本文针对当前视频多模态大语言模型在长时程机器人操作中仅作为被动观察者识别事件而非主动评估任务进展的局限性，提出PRIMO R1这一7B框架，通过基于结果的强化学习激励显式的思维链生成以进行进度估计，并采用结构化时序输入将视频锚定在初始与当前状态图像之间。实验结果表明，该模型实现了最先进的性能，包括将专业基线的平均绝对误差降低50%，并在困难故障检测任务上展现出强大的零样本泛化能力，在RoboFail基准测试中以67.0%的准确率超越OpenAI o1等闭源模型6.0%。
Unbiased and Biased Variance-Reduced Forward-Reflected-Backward Splitting Methods for Stochastic Composite Inclusions
Authors: Quoc Tran-Dinh, Nghia Nguyen-Trung
First: 2026-03-16T17:39:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:39:25+00:00
Comments: 34 pages and 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper develops new variance-reduction techniques for the forward-reflected-backward splitting (FRBS) method to solve a class of possibly nonmonotone stochastic composite inclusions. Unlike unbiased estimators such as mini-batching, developing stochastic biased variants faces a fundamental technical challenge and has not been utilized before for inclusions and fixed-point problems. We fill this gap by designing a new framework that can handle both unbiased and biased estimators. Our main idea is to construct stochastic variance-reduced estimators for the forward-reflected direction and use them to perform iterate updates. First, we propose a class of unbiased variance-reduced estimators and show that increasing mini-batch SGD, loopless-SVRG, and SAGA estimators fall within this class. For these unbiased estimators, we establish a $\mathcal{O}(1/k)$ best-iterate convergence rate for the expected squared residual norm, together with almost-sure convergence of the iterate sequence to a solution. Consequently, we prove that the best oracle complexities for the $n$-finite-sum and expectation settings are $\mathcal{O}(n^{2/3}ε^{-2})$ and $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-10/3})$, respectively, when employing loopless-SVRG or SAGA, where $ε$ is a desired accuracy. Second, we introduce a new class of biased variance-reduced estimators for the forward-reflected direction, which includes SARAH, Hybrid SGD, and Hybrid SVRG as special instances. While the convergence rates remain valid for these biased estimators, the resulting oracle complexities are $\mathcal{O}(n^{3/4}ε^{-2})$ and $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-5})$ for the $n$-finite-sum and expectation settings, respectively. Finally, we conduct two numerical experiments on AUC optimization for imbalanced classification and policy evaluation in reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无偏与有偏方差缩减前向反射后向分裂方法求解随机复合包含问题
本文针对求解一类可能非单调的随机复合包含问题，提出了新的方差缩减技术用于前向反射后向分裂方法。与无偏估计器（如小批量采样）不同，开发有偏随机变体面临基础性技术挑战，此前未在包含问题与不动点问题中得到应用。我们通过设计能同时处理无偏与有偏估计器的新框架填补了这一空白。核心思想是构建前向反射方向的随机方差缩减估计器，并用于迭代更新。首先，提出一类无偏方差缩减估计器，证明递增小批量随机梯度下降、无环随机方差缩减梯度及随机增量梯度均属此类。针对这些无偏估计器，建立了期望残差范数平方的$\mathcal{O}(1/k)$最优迭代收敛率，并证明迭代序列几乎必然收敛至解。由此得出：采用无环随机方差缩减梯度或随机增量梯度时，$n$有限和与期望设置的最优Oracle复杂度分别为$\mathcal{O}(n^{2/3}ε^{-2})$与$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-10/3})$，其中$ε$为目标精度。其次，针对前向反射方向提出新的有偏方差缩减估计器类，其特例包括随机递归梯度、混合随机梯度下降及混合随机方差缩减梯度。这些有偏估计器虽保持相同收敛率，但产生的Oracle复杂度在$n$有限和与期望设置下分别为$\mathcal{O}(n^{3/4}ε^{-2})$与$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-5})$。最后，通过不平衡分类的AUC优化与强化学习策略评估两个数值实验验证了理论结果。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of solving stochastic composite inclusions, particularly nonmonotone ones, by developing new variance-reduction techniques for the forward-reflected-backward splitting method. The method introduces a framework that accommodates both unbiased and biased estimators, constructing stochastic variance-reduced estimators for the forward-reflected direction to update iterates. For unbiased estimators like loopless-SVRG and SAGA, it achieves a best-iterate convergence rate of O(1/k) in expected squared residual norm, with oracle complexities of O(n^{2/3}ε^{-2}) for finite-sum settings and O(ε^{-10/3}) for expectation settings. For biased estimators such as SARAH, it maintains convergence but with higher complexities of O(n^{3/4}ε^{-2}) and O(ε^{-5}), and numerical experiments on AUC optimization and reinforcement learning policy evaluation validate the approach.
本文针对求解随机复合包含问题（特别是非单调情形）的挑战，开发了前向反射后向分裂方法的新方差缩减技术。该方法引入了一个能同时处理无偏和有偏估计器的框架，通过构建前向反射方向的随机方差缩减估计器来更新迭代。对于无偏估计器（如循环无偏SVRG和SAGA），实现了期望平方残差范数的最佳迭代收敛速率O(1/k)，在有限和设置下的Oracle复杂度为O(n^{2/3}ε^{-2})，期望设置下为O(ε^{-10/3})。对于有偏估计器（如SARAH），虽保持收敛但复杂度较高，分别为O(n^{3/4}ε^{-2})和O(ε^{-5})，并通过AUC优化和强化学习策略评估的数值实验验证了方法的有效性。
Convergence of Distributionally Robust Q-Learning with Linear Function Approximation
Authors: Saptarshi Mandal, Yashaswini Murthy, R. Srikant
First: 2025-10-02T07:01:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:23:13+00:00
Comments: Preprint. 53 Pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Distributionally robust reinforcement learning (DRRL) focuses on designing policies that achieve good performance under model uncertainties. The goal is to maximize the worst-case long-term discounted reward, where the data for RL comes from a nominal model while the deployed environment can deviate from the nominal model within a prescribed uncertainty set. Existing convergence guarantees for DRRL are limited to tabular MDPs or are dependent on restrictive discount factor assumptions when function approximation is used. We present a convergence result for a robust Q-learning algorithm with linear function approximation without any discount factor restrictions. In this paper, the robustness is measured with respect to the total-variation distance uncertainty set. Our model free algorithm does not require generative access to the MDP and achieves an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/ε^{4})$ sample complexity for an $ε$-accurate value estimate. Our results close a key gap between the empirical success of robust RL algorithms and the non-asymptotic guarantees enjoyed by their non-robust counterparts. The key ideas in the paper also extend in a relatively straightforward fashion to robust Temporal-Difference (TD) learning with function approximation. The robust TD learning algorithm is discussed in the Appendix.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布鲁棒Q学习与线性函数逼近的收敛性
分布鲁棒强化学习（DRRL）专注于设计在模型不确定性下仍能保持良好性能的策略，其目标是在最坏情况下最大化长期折扣奖励。强化学习的数据来源于名义模型，而实际部署环境可能在预设的不确定性集合内偏离该模型。现有DRRL的收敛性保证仅限于表格化MDP，或在使用函数逼近时依赖于严格的折扣因子假设。本文提出了一种无折扣因子限制的线性函数逼近鲁棒Q学习算法的收敛性结果，其中鲁棒性通过全变差距离不确定性集合衡量。这种无模型算法无需生成MDP样本，对于ε精度值估计实现了$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/ε^{4})$的样本复杂度。该研究填补了鲁棒强化学习算法实证成功与非鲁棒方法非渐近保证之间的关键空白。论文核心思想还可直接扩展至带函数逼近的鲁棒时序差分（TD）学习，相关算法在附录中讨论。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the lack of convergence guarantees for distributionally robust reinforcement learning (DRRL) with function approximation, which aims to optimize policies against worst-case model uncertainties. The authors propose a robust Q-learning algorithm using linear function approximation, with robustness defined via a total-variation distance uncertainty set, and prove its convergence without restrictive discount factor assumptions. Their model-free method achieves an Õ(1/ε⁴) sample complexity for an ε-accurate value estimate, bridging the theoretical gap between robust and non-robust RL algorithms, with extensions to robust TD learning also provided.
本文针对使用函数近似的分布鲁棒强化学习（DRRL）缺乏收敛性保证的问题展开研究，该领域旨在优化策略以应对最坏情况下的模型不确定性。作者提出了一种采用线性函数近似的鲁棒Q学习算法，其鲁棒性通过全变差距离不确定性集来定义，并在无限制性折扣因子假设下证明了算法的收敛性。这种无模型方法实现了Õ(1/ε⁴)的样本复杂度以获得ε精确的值估计，从而弥合了鲁棒与非鲁棒强化学习算法之间的理论差距，文中还将其扩展至鲁棒时序差分学习。
Curriculum Reinforcement Learning from Easy to Hard Tasks Improves LLM Reasoning
Authors: Shubham Parashar, Shurui Gui, Xiner Li, Hongyi Ling, Sushil Vemuri, Blake Olson, Eric Li, Yu Zhang, James Caverlee, Dileep Kalathil, Shuiwang Ji
First: 2025-06-07T02:41:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:16:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We aim to improve the reasoning capabilities of language models via reinforcement learning (RL). Recent RL post-trained models like DeepSeek-R1 have demonstrated reasoning abilities on mathematical and coding tasks. However, prior studies suggest that using RL alone to improve reasoning on inherently difficult tasks is less effective. Here, we draw inspiration from curriculum learning and propose to schedule tasks from easy to hard (E2H), allowing LLMs to build reasoning skills gradually. Our method is termed E2H Reasoner. Empirically, we observe that, although easy tasks are important initially, fading them out through appropriate scheduling is essential in preventing overfitting. Theoretically, we establish convergence guarantees for E2H Reasoner within an approximate policy iteration framework. We derive finite-sample complexity bounds and show that when tasks are appropriately decomposed and conditioned, learning through curriculum stages requires fewer total samples than direct learning. Experiments across multiple domains show that E2H Reasoner significantly improves the reasoning ability of small LLMs (1.5B to 3B), which otherwise struggle when trained with vanilla RL alone, highlighting the effectiveness of our method. Our code can be found on https://github.com/divelab/E2H-Reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从易到难任务的课程强化学习提升大语言模型推理能力
我们旨在通过强化学习提升语言模型的推理能力。近期经过强化学习后训练的模型（如DeepSeek-R1）已在数学与编程任务中展现出推理能力。然而，先前研究表明，单独使用强化学习改进固有困难任务的推理效果有限。受课程学习启发，我们提出从易到难的任务调度方法，使大语言模型能逐步构建推理技能，该方法称为E2H推理器。实证研究发现，虽然简单任务在初期至关重要，但通过合理调度逐步淡化这些任务对防止过拟合具有关键作用。理论上，我们在近似策略迭代框架内为E2H推理器建立了收敛保证，推导出有限样本复杂度边界，并证明当任务被恰当分解与条件化时，通过课程阶段学习所需总样本量少于直接学习。跨多领域实验表明，E2H推理器显著提升了中小规模大语言模型（1.5B至3B参数）的推理能力——这些模型若仅使用原始强化学习训练则表现欠佳，从而凸显了本方法的有效性。代码已开源：https://github.com/divelab/E2H-Reasoning。
Summary / 总结
This paper aims to enhance the reasoning capabilities of language models through reinforcement learning (RL), motivated by the observation that applying RL directly to difficult reasoning tasks is often ineffective. The proposed method, E2H Reasoner, introduces a curriculum learning strategy that schedules tasks from easy to hard, allowing models to build skills gradually; it also incorporates a fading mechanism for easy tasks to prevent overfitting. Theoretically, the approach is supported by convergence guarantees and sample complexity bounds showing efficiency gains. Experimentally, it significantly improves the reasoning performance of small LLMs (1.5B-3B parameters) on mathematical and coding tasks, outperforming vanilla RL training.
本文旨在通过强化学习提升语言模型的推理能力，其动机是观察到直接对困难推理任务使用强化学习效果不佳。所提出的方法E2H Reasoner采用课程学习策略，将任务从易到难进行调度，使模型逐步构建技能，并引入了对简单任务的淡化机制以防止过拟合。理论上，该方法在近似策略迭代框架下建立了收敛保证和样本复杂度界限，证明了其效率优势。实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了小型语言模型（15亿至30亿参数）在数学和编码任务上的推理性能，优于单纯的强化学习训练。
DOT: Dynamic Knob Selection and Online Sampling for Automated Database Tuning
Authors: Yifan Wang, Debabrota Basu, Pierre Bourhis, Romain Rouvoy, Patrick Royer
First: 2026-03-16T17:05:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:05:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Database Management Systems (DBMS) are crucial for efficient data management and access control, but their administration remains challenging for Database Administrators (DBAs). Tuning, in particular, is known to be difficult. Modern systems have many tuning parameters, but only a subset significantly impacts performance. Focusing on these influential parameters reduces the search space and optimizes performance. Current methods rely on costly warm-up phases and human expertise to identify important tuning parameters. In this paper, we present DOT, a dynamic knob selection and online sampling DBMS tuning algorithm. DOT uses Recursive Feature Elimination with Cross-Validation (RFECV) to prune low-importance tuning parameters and a Likelihood Ratio Test (LRT) strategy to balance exploration and exploitation. For parameter search, DOT uses a Bayesian Optimization (BO) algorithm to optimize configurations on-the-fly, eliminating the need for warm-up phases or prior knowledge (although existing knowledge can be incorporated). Experiments show that DOT achieves matching or outperforming performance compared to state-of-the-art tuners while substantially reducing tuning overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DOT：面向自动化数据库调优的动态参数选择与在线采样方法
数据库管理系统（DBMS）对高效数据管理与访问控制至关重要，但其管理对数据库管理员（DBA）仍具挑战性，尤其调优环节尤为困难。现代系统包含大量调优参数，但仅部分参数对性能产生显著影响。聚焦关键参数可缩减搜索空间并优化性能。现有方法依赖高成本预热阶段与人工经验识别重要参数。本文提出DOT——一种动态参数选择与在线采样的DBMS调优算法。DOT采用交叉验证递归特征消除（RFECV）剪枝低重要性参数，并运用似然比检验（LRT）策略平衡探索与利用。在参数搜索层面，DOT采用贝叶斯优化（BO）算法实时优化配置，无需预热阶段或先验知识（但可兼容既有知识）。实验表明，DOT在显著降低调优开销的同时，其性能达到或超越现有先进调优器。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of tuning complex database systems with many parameters, where only a subset significantly affects performance, this paper introduces DOT, an automated tuning algorithm. The method dynamically selects important tuning knobs using Recursive Feature Elimination with Cross-Validation (RFECV) and employs a Likelihood Ratio Test (LRT) strategy for exploration-exploitation balance, alongside Bayesian Optimization (BO) for online configuration search without requiring a warm-up phase. Experimental results demonstrate that DOT matches or surpasses state-of-the-art tuners in performance while substantially reducing tuning overhead.
针对数据库系统调优参数众多且仅部分关键参数影响性能的挑战，本文提出了DOT自动调优算法。该方法采用递归特征消除与交叉验证动态选择重要调优参数，利用似然比检验策略平衡探索与利用，并结合贝叶斯优化进行在线配置搜索，无需预热阶段。实验结果表明，DOT在达到或超越现有先进调优器性能的同时，显著降低了调优开销。
Deep Reinforcement Learning for Fano Hypersurfaces
Authors: Marc Truter
First: 2026-03-16T15:42:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:42:12+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 10 figures, 1 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We design a deep reinforcement learning algorithm to explore a high-dimensional integer lattice with sparse rewards, training a feedforward neural network as a dynamic search heuristic to steer exploration toward reward dense regions. We apply this to the discovery of Fano 4-fold hypersurfaces with terminal singularities, objects of central importance in algebraic geometry. Fano varieties with terminal singularities are fundamental building blocks of algebraic varieties, and explicit examples serve as a vital testing ground for the development and generalisation of theory. Despite decades of effort, the combinatorial intractability of the underlying search space has left this classification severely incomplete. Our reinforcement learning approach yields thousands of previously unknown examples, hundreds of which we show are inaccessible to known search methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向Fano超曲面的深度强化学习
我们设计了一种深度强化学习算法，用于探索具有稀疏奖励的高维整数格点，训练前馈神经网络作为动态搜索启发式方法，引导探索朝向奖励密集区域。我们将此方法应用于发现具有终端奇点的Fano四重超曲面——这是代数几何中至关重要的研究对象。具有终端奇点的Fano簇是代数簇的基本构成单元，其具体实例为理论发展与推广提供了关键的验证平台。尽管经过数十年的努力，底层搜索空间的组合复杂性使得该分类工作仍极不完整。我们的强化学习方法产生了数千个先前未知的实例，其中数百个被证明是现有搜索方法无法触及的。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the long-standing and combinatorially intractable challenge of classifying Fano varieties with terminal singularities, which are fundamental objects in algebraic geometry, this paper develops a deep reinforcement learning method to explore high-dimensional integer lattices with sparse rewards. The approach trains a feedforward neural network as a dynamic heuristic to guide exploration toward reward-dense regions, specifically targeting the discovery of Fano 4-fold hypersurfaces. The main experimental result is that this reinforcement learning algorithm successfully generates thousands of previously unknown examples, with hundreds confirmed to be inaccessible to traditional search techniques, thereby significantly advancing the classification effort.
针对代数几何中具有终端奇点的法诺簇这一基础对象的分类难题，该研究设计了一种深度强化学习算法来探索具有稀疏奖励的高维整数格。该方法训练一个前馈神经网络作为动态搜索启发式，引导探索朝向奖励密集区域，专门用于发现四维法诺超曲面。主要实验结果表明，该强化学习方法成功生成了数千个先前未知的实例，其中数百个被证实是传统搜索方法无法获得的，从而显著推进了分类工作的进展。
Listening to the Echo: User-Reaction Aware Policy Optimization via Scalar-Verbal Hybrid Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jing Ye, Xinpei Zhao, Lu Xiang, Yaping Zhang, Chengqing Zong
First: 2026-03-16T15:39:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:39:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While current emotional support dialogue systems typically rely on expert-defined scalar rewards for alignment, these signals suffer from severe information sparsity. They cannot explain why a response failed or how to adapt to dynamic user states, often diverging from the actual goal of facilitating positive emotional shifts. In practice, the most direct and reliable learning signal emerges from the user's continuous reactions during ongoing interaction. We therefore propose Reaction Aware Policy Optimization (RAPO), a framework that optimizes over interaction consequences rather than rubric scores. RAPO treats dialogue as a reaction-driven process and utilizes simulated user responses to generate dense natural-language feedback through three core components: Hindsight Dialogue Selection, which isolates pivotal turns that meaningfully alter user emotional trajectories; Generative Hindsight Feedback, which transforms user reactions into contrastive ranking signals and natural-language critiques; and Scalar-Verbal Hybrid Policy Optimization, which couples scalar reward optimization for global alignment with verbal feedback distillation for fine-grained semantic refinement. Extensive experiments on ESC and Sotopia demonstrate that RAPO significantly outperforms strong reinforcement learning baselines in driving positive interaction outcomes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：倾听回声：基于标量-语言混合强化学习的用户反应感知策略优化
当前情感支持对话系统通常依赖专家定义的标量奖励进行对齐，但这些信号存在严重的信息稀疏性问题。它们无法解释响应失败的原因或如何适应动态用户状态，常偏离促进积极情绪转变的实际目标。实践中，最直接可靠的学习信号来自用户在持续交互中的实时反应。为此，我们提出反应感知策略优化框架，该框架基于交互结果而非评分规则进行优化，将对话视为反应驱动的过程，通过三大核心组件利用模拟用户反应生成稠密的自然语言反馈：后见对话选择——识别显著改变用户情绪轨迹的关键对话轮次；生成式后见反馈——将用户反应转化为对比排序信号与自然语言评述；标量-语言混合策略优化——耦合标量奖励优化实现全局对齐，结合语言反馈蒸馏完成细粒度语义优化。在ESC与Sotopia数据集上的大量实验表明，该框架在促进积极交互结果方面显著优于主流强化学习基线模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of sparse scalar rewards in emotional support dialogue systems, which fail to capture dynamic user states and explain response failures, this paper introduces Reaction Aware Policy Optimization (RAPO), a framework that leverages user reactions as dense learning signals. The method treats dialogue as a reaction-driven process, employing three components: Hindsight Dialogue Selection to identify pivotal emotional turns, Generative Hindsight Feedback to convert reactions into contrastive rankings and natural-language critiques, and Scalar-Verbal Hybrid Policy Optimization to combine scalar rewards with verbal feedback for refinement. Experimental results on ESC and Sotopia datasets show that RAPO significantly outperforms strong reinforcement learning baselines in achieving positive interaction outcomes.
针对情感支持对话系统中标量奖励信号稀疏、无法解释响应失败或适应动态用户状态的问题，本文提出了反应感知策略优化（RAPO）框架，利用用户连续反应作为密集学习信号。该方法将对话视为反应驱动过程，通过三个核心组件实现：后见对话选择以识别改变用户情绪轨迹的关键轮次，生成式后见反馈将用户反应转化为对比排序信号和自然语言批评，以及标量-言语混合策略优化，结合标量奖励的全局对齐与言语反馈的细粒度语义优化。在ESC和Sotopia数据集上的大量实验表明，RAPO在促进积极互动结果方面显著优于强强化学习基线。
MA-VLCM: A Vision Language Critic Model for Value Estimation of Policies in Multi-Agent Team Settings
Authors: Shahil Shaik, Aditya Parameshwaran, Anshul Nayak, Jonathon M. Smereka, Yue Wang
First: 2026-03-16T15:29:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:29:41+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) commonly relies on a centralized critic to estimate the value function. However, learning such a critic from scratch is highly sample-inefficient and often lacks generalization across environments. At the same time, large vision-language-action models (VLAs) trained on internet-scale data exhibit strong multimodal reasoning and zero-shot generalization capabilities, yet directly deploying them for robotic execution remains computationally prohibitive, particularly in heterogeneous multi-robot systems with diverse embodiments and resource constraints. To address these challenges, we propose Multi-Agent Vision-Language-Critic Models (MA-VLCM), a framework that replaces the learned centralized critic in MARL with a pretrained vision-language model fine-tuned to evaluate multi-agent behavior. MA-VLCM acts as a centralized critic conditioned on natural language task descriptions, visual trajectory observations, and structured multi-agent state information. By eliminating critic learning during policy optimization, our approach significantly improves sample efficiency while producing compact execution policies suitable for deployment on resource-constrained robots. Results show good zero-shot return estimation on models with differing VLM backbones on in-distribution and out-of-distribution scenarios in multi-agent team settings
中文标题/摘要
标题：MA-VLCM：面向多智能体团队策略价值评估的视觉语言评论家模型
多智能体强化学习通常依赖集中式评论家进行价值函数估计，但从头学习此类评论家样本效率低下且泛化能力不足。尽管基于互联网数据训练的大型视觉语言动作模型具备强大的多模态推理与零样本泛化能力，但其直接部署于机器人系统仍面临计算成本过高的问题，尤其在异构多机器人系统中。为此，我们提出多智能体视觉语言评论家模型框架，该框架通过微调预训练的视觉语言模型替代传统学习型集中式评论家，使其能够基于自然语言任务描述、视觉轨迹观测与结构化多智能体状态信息评估群体行为。该方法在策略优化过程中省去评论家学习环节，显著提升样本效率，同时生成适用于资源受限机器人的紧凑执行策略。实验表明，采用不同视觉语言模型骨干的MA-VLCM在多智能体团队场景的分布内与分布外任务中均表现出良好的零样本回报估计能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the sample inefficiency and limited generalization of centralized critics in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) and the computational impracticality of directly deploying large vision-language-action models for robotic execution. It proposes MA-VLCM, a framework that replaces the learned critic with a pretrained vision-language model fine-tuned to evaluate multi-agent behavior using natural language task descriptions, visual trajectories, and structured state information. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach significantly improves sample efficiency, enables zero-shot return estimation across in-distribution and out-of-distribution scenarios, and yields compact policies suitable for resource-constrained robots.
本文针对多智能体强化学习中集中式评论家样本效率低、泛化能力有限的问题，以及大型视觉语言动作模型直接部署于机器人执行时计算成本过高的问题，提出了MA-VLCM框架。该方法用预训练的视觉语言模型替代学习型评论家，通过微调使其能基于自然语言任务描述、视觉轨迹观察和结构化多智能体状态信息评估行为。实验结果表明，该方法显著提高了样本效率，在分布内和分布外场景中实现了良好的零样本回报估计，并生成了适合资源受限机器人的紧凑策略。
Amplification Effects in Test-Time Reinforcement Learning: Safety and Reasoning Vulnerabilities
Authors: Vanshaj Khattar, Md Rafi ur Rashid, Moumita Choudhury, Jing Liu, Toshiaki Koike-Akino, Ming Jin, Ye Wang
First: 2026-03-16T15:28:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:28:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Test-time training (TTT) has recently emerged as a promising method to improve the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs), in which the model directly learns from test data without access to labels. However, this reliance on test data also makes TTT methods vulnerable to harmful prompt injections. In this paper, we investigate safety vulnerabilities of TTT methods, where we study a representative self-consistency-based test-time learning method: test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL), a recent TTT method that improves LLM reasoning by rewarding self-consistency using majority vote as a reward signal. We show that harmful prompt injection during TTRL amplifies the model's existing behaviors, i.e., safety amplification when the base model is relatively safe, and harmfulness amplification when it is vulnerable to the injected data. In both cases, there is a decline in reasoning ability, which we refer to as the reasoning tax. We also show that TTT methods such as TTRL can be exploited adversarially using specially designed "HarmInject" prompts to force the model to answer jailbreak and reasoning queries together, resulting in stronger harmfulness amplification. Overall, our results highlight that TTT methods that enhance LLM reasoning by promoting self-consistency can lead to amplification behaviors and reasoning degradation, highlighting the need for safer TTT methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：测试时强化学习中的放大效应：安全性与推理漏洞
测试时训练作为一种提升大语言模型推理能力的新兴方法，允许模型在无标签情况下直接从测试数据中学习，但这也使其易受有害提示注入攻击。本文聚焦于测试时强化学习这一基于自一致性的代表性方法，探讨其安全漏洞。研究发现，有害提示注入会放大模型的既有行为：当基础模型相对安全时，会引发安全性放大；当模型易受注入数据影响时，则导致危害性放大。两种情形均伴随推理能力下降，即“推理税”。研究进一步表明，攻击者可通过特制的“HarmInject”提示，迫使模型同时处理越狱查询与推理任务，加剧危害性放大。这些发现揭示，依赖自一致性的测试时训练方法在提升推理能力的同时，可能引发行为放大与推理退化，凸显了开发更安全测试时训练方法的迫切性。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates safety vulnerabilities in test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL), a method that enhances large language model reasoning by rewarding self-consistency using majority vote. The motivation stems from the risk that such test-time training, which learns directly from unlabeled test data, is vulnerable to harmful prompt injections. The method involves analyzing TTRL's behavior under attack, showing that prompt injections amplify the model's existing tendencies—safety amplification if the base model is safe, and harmfulness amplification if it is vulnerable—while consistently degrading reasoning performance, termed the "reasoning tax." Experimental results demonstrate that adversarial "HarmInject" prompts can force the model to answer both jailbreak and reasoning queries, leading to stronger harmfulness amplification and highlighting the need for safer test-time training approaches.
本文研究了测试时强化学习的安全漏洞，该方法通过多数投票奖励自洽性来增强大语言模型的推理能力。研究动机在于这种直接从未标记测试数据中学习的测试时训练方法容易受到有害提示注入的攻击。方法包括分析TTRL在攻击下的行为，表明提示注入会放大模型的现有倾向——若基础模型安全则产生安全放大，若易受攻击则产生有害放大，同时一致地降低推理性能，称为“推理税”。实验结果证明，对抗性的“HarmInject”提示可以迫使模型同时回答越狱和推理查询，导致更强的有害放大，凸显了开发更安全测试时训练方法的必要性。
CASHomon Sets: Efficient Rashomon Sets Across Multiple Model Classes and their Hyperparameters
Authors: Fiona Katharina Ewald, Martin Binder, Matthias Feurer, Bernd Bischl, Giuseppe Casalicchio
First: 2026-03-16T14:12:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T14:12:05+00:00
Comments: Equal contributions by Fiona Katharina Ewald and Martin Binder
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rashomon sets are model sets within one model class that perform nearly as well as a reference model from the same model class. They reveal the existence of alternative well-performing models, which may support different interpretations. This enables selecting models that match domain knowledge, hidden constraints, or user preferences. However, efficient construction methods currently exist for only a few model classes. Applied machine learning usually searches many model classes, and the best class is unknown beforehand. We therefore study Rashomon sets in the combined algorithm selection and hyperparameter optimization (CASH) setting and call them CASHomon sets. We propose TruVaRImp, a model-based active learning algorithm for level set estimation with an implicit threshold, and provide convergence guarantees. On synthetic and real-world datasets, TruVaRImp reliably identifies CASHomon sets members and matches or outperforms naive sampling, Bayesian optimization, classical and implicit level set estimation methods, and other baselines. Our analyses of predictive multiplicity and feature-importance variability across model classes question the common practice of interpreting data through a single model class.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CASHomon集合：跨多模型类别及其超参数的高效Rashomon集合
Rashomon集合指同一模型类别中性能接近参考模型的模型集合，其揭示了存在其他性能优异的替代模型，这些模型可能支持不同的解释。这使得选择符合领域知识、隐藏约束或用户偏好的模型成为可能。然而，目前仅少数模型类别具备高效的构建方法。应用机器学习通常需搜索多个模型类别，且最佳类别事先未知。因此，我们研究组合算法选择与超参数优化（CASH）设定下的Rashomon集合，并将其称为CASHomon集合。我们提出TruVaRImp——一种基于模型的主动学习算法，用于具有隐式阈值的水平集估计，并提供收敛性保证。在合成和真实数据集上，TruVaRImp能可靠识别CASHomon集合成员，其性能匹配或优于朴素采样、贝叶斯优化、经典与隐式水平集估计方法及其他基线。我们对跨模型类别的预测多重性和特征重要性变异性的分析，对通过单一模型类别解释数据的常见实践提出了质疑。
Summary / 总结
The study is motivated by the need to identify diverse, well-performing models across multiple model classes and hyperparameters, moving beyond the limitations of Rashomon sets confined to a single model class. The authors introduce CASHomon sets within the combined algorithm selection and hyperparameter optimization (CASH) framework and propose TruVaRImp, a model-based active learning algorithm for level set estimation with implicit thresholds, supported by convergence guarantees. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world datasets show that TruVaRImp effectively identifies CASHomon set members, outperforming naive sampling, Bayesian optimization, and other baseline methods, while analyses reveal significant predictive multiplicity and feature-importance variability across model classes, challenging the reliance on single-model interpretations.
该研究的动机在于需要跨多个模型类别和超参数识别多样化的高性能模型，以克服传统Rashomon集合局限于单一模型类别的不足。作者在组合算法选择和超参数优化（CASH）框架下提出了CASHomon集合，并设计了TruVaRImp算法，这是一种基于模型的主动学习方法，用于具有隐式阈值的水平集估计，且提供了收敛性保证。在合成和真实数据集上的实验结果表明，TruVaRImp能可靠地识别CASHomon集合成员，其性能优于朴素采样、贝叶斯优化及其他基线方法；同时，分析揭示了跨模型类别的预测多重性和特征重要性变异性，质疑了依赖单一模型进行数据解释的常见做法。
Evolutionary Transfer Learning for Dragonchess
Authors: Jim O'Connor, Annika Hoag, Sarah Goyette, Gary B. Parker
First: 2026-03-16T13:58:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:58:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dragonchess, a three-dimensional chess variant introduced by Gary Gygax, presents unique strategic and computational challenges that make it an ideal environment for studying the transfer of artificial intelligence (AI) heuristics across domains. In this work, we introduce Dragonchess as a novel testbed for AI research and provide an open-source, Python-based game engine for community use. Our research investigates evolutionary transfer learning by adapting heuristic evaluation functions directly from Stockfish, a leading chess engine, and subsequently optimizing them using Covariance Matrix Adaptation Evolution Strategy (CMA-ES). Initial trials showed that direct heuristic transfers were inadequate due to Dragonchess's distinct multi-layer structure and movement rules. However, evolutionary optimization significantly improved AI agent performance, resulting in superior gameplay demonstrated through empirical evaluation in a 50-round Swiss-style tournament. This research establishes the effectiveness of evolutionary methods in adapting heuristic knowledge to structurally complex, previously unexplored game domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：龙棋进化迁移学习研究
龙棋是由加里·吉盖克斯提出的三维象棋变体，其独特的战略与计算挑战使其成为研究跨领域人工智能启发式迁移的理想环境。本研究将龙棋确立为人工智能研究的新型测试平台，并提供了开源Python游戏引擎供社区使用。我们通过直接移植顶尖国际象棋引擎Stockfish的启发式评估函数，并采用协方差矩阵自适应进化策略进行优化，探索了进化迁移学习方法。初步实验表明，由于龙棋特有的多层结构与移动规则，直接启发式迁移效果有限。但进化优化显著提升了智能体性能，通过在50轮瑞士制锦标赛中的实证评估，验证了优化后智能体具备更优的对弈能力。本研究证实了进化方法在将启发式知识适配至结构复杂、未经探索游戏领域的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to study AI heuristic transfer in complex, unexplored domains, this paper introduces Dragonchess as a novel testbed and provides an open-source engine. The method involves directly transferring heuristic evaluation functions from the Stockfish chess engine and then optimizing them using the Covariance Matrix Adaptation Evolution Strategy (CMA-ES). The main experimental results showed that direct transfer was insufficient for Dragonchess's unique structure, but subsequent evolutionary optimization significantly enhanced AI performance, as empirically validated in a 50-round tournament, establishing the effectiveness of this approach for complex game domains.
本研究旨在探索人工智能启发式知识在复杂、未开发领域的迁移，为此引入了龙棋作为新的测试平台并提供了开源引擎。方法上，它直接从顶级国际象棋引擎Stockfish迁移启发式评估函数，随后使用协方差矩阵自适应进化策略进行优化。主要实验结果表明，直接迁移对于龙棋独特的结构效果不佳，但后续的进化优化显著提升了智能体的性能，这在50轮锦标赛的实证评估中得到验证，从而确立了该方法在适应复杂游戏领域的有效性。
Evaluating the Robustness of Reinforcement Learning based Adaptive Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Dickens Kwesiga, Angshuman Guin, Khaled Abdelghany, Michael Hunter
First: 2026-03-16T13:47:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:47:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has attracted increasing interest for adaptive traffic signal control due to its model-free ability to learn control policies directly from interaction with the traffic environment. However, several challenges remain before RL-based signal control can be considered ready for field deployment. Many existing studies rely on simplified signal timing structures, robustness of trained models under varying traffic demand conditions remains insufficiently evaluated, and runtime efficiency continues to pose challenges when training RL algorithms in traffic microscopic simulation environments. This study formulates an RL-based signal control algorithm capable of representing a full eight-phase ring-barrier configuration consistent with field signal controllers. The algorithm is trained and evaluated under varying traffic demand conditions and benchmarked against state-of-the-practice actuated signal control (ASC). To assess robustness, experiments are conducted across multiple traffic volumes and origin-destination (O-D) demand patterns with varying levels of structural similarity. To improve training efficiency, a distributed asynchronous training architecture is implemented that enables parallel simulation across multiple computing nodes. Results from a case study intersection show that the proposed RL-based signal control significantly outperforms optimized ASC, reducing average delay by 11-32% across movements. A model trained on a single O-D pattern generalizes well to similar unseen demand patterns but degrades under substantially different demand conditions. In contrast, a model trained on diverse O-D patterns demonstrates strong robustness, consistently outperforming ASC even under highly dissimilar unseen demand scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：评估基于强化学习的自适应交通信号控制鲁棒性
强化学习因其无需模型、可直接通过与交通环境交互学习控制策略的能力，在自适应交通信号控制领域受到日益关注。然而，基于强化学习的信号控制在实际部署前仍面临诸多挑战：现有研究多依赖简化的信号配时结构，训练模型在不同交通需求条件下的鲁棒性评估不足，且在交通微观仿真环境中训练强化学习算法的运行效率仍存在瓶颈。本研究提出一种基于强化学习的信号控制算法，能够完整表征与现场信号控制器一致的八相位环栅栏配置。该算法在不同交通需求条件下进行训练与评估，并与当前最优实践的自适应信号控制进行对比。为评估鲁棒性，实验覆盖了多种交通流量和具有不同结构相似度的起讫点需求模式。为提高训练效率，采用分布式异步训练架构，实现多计算节点的并行仿真。案例交叉口结果表明，所提出的强化学习信号控制显著优于优化后的自适应信号控制，各流向平均延误降低11%-32%。在单一O-D模式上训练的模型能较好泛化至相似的未知需求模式，但在差异显著的需求条件下性能下降；而在多样化O-D模式上训练的模型则表现出强鲁棒性，即使在高度差异化的未知需求场景下仍持续优于自适应信号控制。
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the need for robust and efficient reinforcement learning (RL) models for adaptive traffic signal control, motivated by challenges in deployment such as simplified signal structures, unproven robustness under varying traffic, and slow training. The method develops an RL algorithm that models a full eight-phase ring-barrier signal configuration and employs a distributed asynchronous training architecture for efficiency, evaluating robustness across diverse traffic volumes and origin-destination patterns against actuated signal control (ASC). Experimental results from a case study intersection show the RL control reduces average delay by 11-32% compared to ASC, with models trained on diverse demand patterns maintaining strong performance even under unseen, dissimilar conditions, whereas those trained on single patterns degrade when demand differs substantially.
本研究针对强化学习在自适应交通信号控制中部署的挑战，如信号结构简化、多变交通下的鲁棒性不足及训练效率低，旨在开发鲁棒高效的强化学习模型。方法上，提出了一个能模拟完整八相位环栅栏信号配置的强化学习算法，并采用分布式异步训练架构提升效率，在不同交通量和起讫点需求模式下与感应信号控制进行鲁棒性对比测试。案例交叉口实验结果表明，该强化学习控制相比感应信号控制将平均延误降低了11-32%，在多样化需求模式上训练的模型即使面对未见且差异大的场景仍保持强劲性能，而仅在单一模式上训练的模型则在需求差异大时性能下降。
Probe-then-Plan: Environment-Aware Planning for Industrial E-commerce Search
Authors: Mengxiang Chen, Zhouwei Zhai, Jin Li
First: 2026-03-16T13:28:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:28:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern e-commerce search is evolving to resolve complex user intents. While Large Language Models (LLMs) offer strong reasoning, existing LLM-based paradigms face a fundamental blindness-latency dilemma: query rewriting is agnostic to retrieval capabilities and real-time inventory, yielding invalid plans; conversely, deep search agents rely on iterative tool calls and reflection, incurring seconds of latency incompatible with industrial sub-second budgets. To resolve this conflict, we propose Environment-Aware Search Planning (EASP), reformulating search planning as a dynamic reasoning process grounded in environmental reality. EASP introduces a Probe-then-Plan mechanism: a lightweight Retrieval Probe exposes the retrieval snapshot, enabling the Planner to diagnose execution gaps and generate grounded search plans. The methodology comprises three stages: (1) Offline Data Synthesis: A Teacher Agent synthesizes diverse, execution-validated plans by diagnosing the probed environment. (2) Planner Training and Alignment: The Planner is initialized via Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) to internalize diagnostic capabilities, then aligned with business outcomes (conversion rate) via Reinforcement Learning (RL). (3) Adaptive Online Serving: A complexity-aware routing mechanism selectively activates planning for complex queries, ensuring optimal resource allocation. Extensive offline evaluations and online A/B testing on JD.com demonstrate that EASP significantly improves relevant recall and achieves substantial lifts in UCVR and GMV. EASP has been successfully deployed in JD.com's AI-Search system.
中文标题/摘要
标题：探后规划：面向工业电商搜索的环境感知规划
现代电商搜索正朝着解决复杂用户意图的方向演进。尽管大语言模型具备强大的推理能力，但现有基于大语言模型的范式面临根本性的盲区-延迟困境：查询改写无视检索能力与实时库存，导致生成无效计划；反之，深度搜索代理依赖迭代式工具调用与反思，产生数秒延迟，无法满足工业级亚秒级响应要求。为解决这一矛盾，本文提出环境感知搜索规划，将搜索规划重构为基于环境实况的动态推理过程。该方法引入“探后规划”机制：轻量级检索探针获取检索快照，使规划器能够诊断执行差距并生成基于实况的搜索计划。方法论包含三个阶段：（1）离线数据合成：教师代理通过诊断探测环境，合成多样化且经执行验证的计划。（2）规划器训练与对齐：通过监督微调初始化规划器以内化诊断能力，再通过强化学习将其与业务指标（转化率）对齐。（3）自适应在线服务：基于复杂度的路由机制选择性激活复杂查询的规划，确保资源最优分配。在京东进行的广泛离线评估与在线A/B测试表明，该方法显著提升相关召回率，并在UCVR和GMV上实现大幅增长，目前已成功部署于京东AI搜索系统。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the dilemma in industrial e-commerce search where existing LLM-based methods either produce invalid plans due to ignorance of real-time inventory and retrieval capabilities or incur high latency from iterative tool calls, conflicting with sub-second response requirements. It proposes Environment-Aware Search Planning (EASP), which employs a Probe-then-Plan mechanism: a lightweight Retrieval Probe first captures a retrieval snapshot, enabling a Planner to diagnose execution gaps and generate grounded search plans through offline synthesis of validated plans via a Teacher Agent, supervised fine-tuning, and reinforcement learning aligned with business outcomes like conversion rate, coupled with adaptive online routing for complex queries. Experimental results from JD.com show that EASP significantly improves relevant recall and achieves substantial lifts in UCVR and GMV, demonstrating its effectiveness in real-world deployment.
本文针对工业电商搜索中现有基于大语言模型的方法存在的困境：要么因忽略实时库存和检索能力而产生无效计划，要么因迭代工具调用导致高延迟，无法满足亚秒级响应需求。提出了环境感知搜索规划（EASP），采用“探测后规划”机制：通过轻量级检索探测捕获检索快照，使规划器能够诊断执行差距并生成基于环境的搜索计划，该方法包括离线数据合成（由教师代理生成多样化且经验证的计划）、规划器训练与对齐（通过监督微调和强化学习优化业务指标如转化率），以及自适应在线服务（根据查询复杂度选择性激活规划）。在京东的离线评估和在线A/B测试中，EASP显著提升了相关召回率，并在UCVR和GMV上实现了大幅增长，已成功部署于京东的AI搜索系统。
SAGE: Multi-Agent Self-Evolution for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Yulin Peng, Xinxin Zhu, Chenxing Wei, Nianbo Zeng, Leilei Wang, Ying Tiffany He, F. Richard Yu
First: 2026-03-16T13:24:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:24:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves reasoning in large language models (LLMs), but many methods still rely on large human-labeled datasets. While self-play reduces this dependency, it often lacks explicit planning and strong quality control, limiting stability in long-horizon multi-step reasoning. We present SAGE (Self-evolving Agents for Generalized reasoning Evolution), a closed-loop framework where four agents: Challenger, Planner, Solver, and Critic, co-evolve from a shared LLM backbone using only a small seed set. The Challenger continuously generates increasingly difficult tasks; the Planner converts each task into a structured multi-step plan; and the Solver follows the plan to produce an answer, whose correctness is determined by external verifiers. The Critic scores and filters both generated questions and plans to prevent curriculum drift and maintain training signal quality, enabling stable self-training. Across mathematics and code-generation benchmarks, SAGE delivers consistent gains across model scales, improving the Qwen-2.5-7B model by 8.9% on LiveCodeBench and 10.7% on OlympiadBench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SAGE：面向大语言模型推理的多智能体自进化框架
基于可验证奖励的强化学习能提升大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但现有方法仍依赖大规模人工标注数据集。尽管自博弈机制可降低这种依赖，但其常缺乏显式规划和严格的质量控制，限制了长跨度多步推理的稳定性。本文提出SAGE（面向泛化推理进化的自进化智能体框架），这是一个闭环系统：挑战者、规划者、求解者、评判者四个智能体仅基于少量种子数据，从共享的LLM主干网络协同进化。挑战者持续生成难度递增的任务；规划者将任务转化为结构化多步方案；求解者依据方案生成答案，其正确性由外部验证器判定。评判者对生成的问题和方案进行评分筛选，防止课程漂移并维持训练信号质量，从而实现稳定的自训练。在数学与代码生成基准测试中，SAGE在不同规模模型上均取得稳定提升，将Qwen-2.5-7B模型在LiveCodeBench和OlympiadBench上的性能分别提升8.9%和10.7%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind SAGE is to enhance LLM reasoning without heavy reliance on large human-labeled datasets by addressing the limitations of self-play methods, which often lack explicit planning and quality control in multi-step reasoning. The method introduces a closed-loop framework with four co-evolving agents—Challenger, Planner, Solver, and Critic—all derived from a shared LLM backbone using only a small seed set; the Challenger generates progressively harder tasks, the Planner creates structured multi-step plans, the Solver executes these plans to produce answers verified externally, and the Critic filters questions and plans to prevent curriculum drift and ensure training stability. Experimental results show consistent improvements across model scales, with the Qwen-2.5-7B model achieving gains of 8.9% on LiveCodeBench and 10.7% on OlympiadBench in mathematics and code-generation benchmarks.
SAGE的动机是在减少对大规模人工标注数据依赖的同时，提升大语言模型的推理能力，以解决自对弈方法在长视野多步推理中缺乏显式规划和质量控制的问题。该方法提出一个闭环框架，包含四个协同进化的智能体——挑战者、规划者、求解者和评判者，它们均基于共享的LLM主干，仅使用少量种子数据；挑战者持续生成难度递增的任务，规划者将任务转化为结构化多步计划，求解者按计划生成答案并由外部验证器检验正确性，评判者则对生成的问题和计划进行评分过滤，以防止课程漂移并保持训练信号质量。实验结果表明，该方法在不同模型规模上均带来稳定提升，其中Qwen-2.5-7B模型在数学和代码生成基准测试中，于LiveCodeBench上提高了8.9%，在OlympiadBench上提高了10.7%。
Towards Foundation Models for Consensus Rank Aggregation
Authors: Yijun Jin, Simon Klüttermann, Chiara Balestra, Emmanuel Müller
First: 2026-03-16T12:55:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T12:55:54+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aggregating a consensus ranking from multiple input rankings is a fundamental problem with applications in recommendation systems, search engines, job recruitment, and elections. Despite decades of research in consensus ranking aggregation, minimizing the Kemeny distance remains computationally intractable. Specifically, determining an optimal aggregation of rankings with respect to the Kemeny distance is an NP-hard problem, limiting its practical application to relatively small-scale instances. We propose the Kemeny Transformer, a novel Transformer-based algorithm trained via reinforcement learning to efficiently approximate the Kemeny optimal ranking. Experimental results demonstrate that our model outperforms classical majority-heuristic and Markov-chain approaches, achieving substantially faster inference than integer linear programming solvers. Our approach thus offers a practical, scalable alternative for real-world ranking-aggregation tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向共识排序聚合的基础模型研究
从多个输入排序中聚合出共识排序是推荐系统、搜索引擎、招聘选举等领域的基础性问题。尽管共识排序聚合研究已开展数十年，最小化Kemeny距离的计算复杂度问题仍未解决。具体而言，基于Kemeny距离的最优排序聚合属于NP难问题，导致其实际应用仅限于小规模场景。本文提出Kemeny Transformer——一种基于Transformer架构、通过强化学习训练的新型算法，可高效逼近Kemeny最优排序。实验表明，该模型在经典多数启发式和马尔可夫链方法上表现更优，且推理速度显著快于整数线性规划求解器。该方法为现实世界的排序聚合任务提供了可扩展的实用解决方案。

本文针对通过最小化Kemeny距离来聚合共识排名这一计算上难解的NP难问题展开研究，该问题限制了在推荐系统、选举等领域的实际应用。为此，作者提出了Kemeny Transformer，这是一种基于Transformer架构、通过强化学习训练的模型，旨在高效近似最优Kemeny排名。实验结果表明，该方法在性能上超越了传统的多数启发式和马尔可夫链方法，且推理速度显著快于整数线性规划求解器，从而为现实世界的排名聚合任务提供了一个可扩展的实用解决方案。
Admission Control of Quasi-Reversible Queueing Systems: Optimization and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Céline Comte, Pascal Moyal
First: 2025-05-22T08:05:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T12:48:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we introduce a versatile scheme for optimizing the arrival rates of quasi-reversible queueing systems. We first propose an alternative definition of quasi-reversibility that encompasses reversibility and highlights the importance of the definition of customer classes. Then we introduce balanced arrival control policies, which generalize the notion of balanced arrival rates introduced in the context of Whittle networks, to the much broader class of quasi-reversible queueing systems. We prove that supplementing a quasi-reversible queueing system with a balanced arrival-control policy preserves the quasi-reversibility, and we specify the form of the stationary measures. We revisit two canonical examples of quasi-reversible queueing systems, Whittle networks and order-independent queues. Lastly, we focus on the problem of admission control and leverage our results in the frameworks of optimization and reinforcement learning.

标题：准可逆排队系统的准入控制：优化与强化学习
本文提出了一种优化准可逆排队系统到达率的通用框架。首先提出一种涵盖可逆性并强调顾客类别定义重要性的准可逆性替代定义。随后引入平衡到达控制策略，将Whittle网络中提出的平衡到达率概念推广至更广泛的准可逆排队系统类别。我们证明在准可逆排队系统中补充平衡到达控制策略可保持准可逆性，并明确了稳态测度的形式。通过重新审视Whittle网络与顺序无关队列这两个准可逆排队系统的典型范例，最终聚焦于准入控制问题，并将研究成果应用于优化与强化学习框架。

本文旨在优化拟可逆排队系统的到达率，通过强调顾客类定义来扩展可逆系统。方法上引入了平衡到达控制策略，将Whittle网络的概念推广到更广泛的拟可逆系统，证明了该策略能保持拟可逆性并给出了稳态测度形式。实验结果通过Whittle网络和顺序无关队列等典型示例验证了该方法的有效性，展示了其在准入控制优化和强化学习框架中的应用。
Iterative Learning Control-Informed Reinforcement Learning for Batch Process Control
Authors: Runze Lin, Ziqi Zhuo, Junghui Chen, Lei Xie, Hongye Su
First: 2026-03-16T12:17:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T12:17:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A significant limitation of Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) is the stochastic uncertainty in actions generated during exploration-exploitation, which poses substantial safety risks during both training and deployment. In industrial process control, the lack of formal stability and convergence guarantees further inhibits adoption of DRL methods by practitioners. Conversely, Iterative Learning Control (ILC) represents a well-established autonomous control methodology for repetitive systems, particularly in batch process optimization. ILC achieves desired control performance through iterative refinement of control laws, either between consecutive batches or within individual batches, to compensate for both repetitive and non-repetitive disturbances. This study introduces an Iterative Learning Control-Informed Reinforcement Learning (IL-CIRL) framework for training DRL controllers in dual-layer batch-to-batch and within-batch control architectures for batch processes. The proposed method incorporates Kalman filter-based state estimation within the iterative learning structure to guide DRL agents toward control policies that satisfy operational constraints and ensure stability guarantees. This approach enables the systematic design of DRL controllers for batch processes operating under multiple disturbance conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向间歇过程控制的迭代学习控制启发的强化学习方法
深度强化学习（DRL）的一个显著局限在于探索-利用过程中生成动作的随机不确定性，这在训练和部署阶段均会带来重大安全风险。在工业过程控制中，缺乏形式化的稳定性与收敛性保证进一步阻碍了从业者采用DRL方法。相比之下，迭代学习控制（ILC）是一种针对重复系统的成熟自主控制方法，尤其适用于间歇过程优化。ILC通过在连续批次间或单个批次内迭代优化控制律，以补偿重复性与非重复性扰动，从而实现期望的控制性能。本研究提出一种迭代学习控制启发的强化学习（IL-CIRL）框架，用于在间歇过程的双层（批间与批内）控制架构中训练DRL控制器。该方法在迭代学习结构中引入基于卡尔曼滤波的状态估计，以引导DRL智能体学习满足操作约束并确保稳定性保证的控制策略。该框架为在多重扰动条件下运行的间歇过程DRL控制器提供了系统化设计途径。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the safety and stability concerns of Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) in industrial batch process control by integrating it with the established methodology of Iterative Learning Control (ILC). The proposed IL-CIRL framework employs a dual-layer control architecture and incorporates Kalman filter-based state estimation within an iterative learning structure to guide DRL agents. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach enables the systematic design of DRL controllers that satisfy operational constraints and ensure stability guarantees under multiple disturbance conditions.
本文针对深度强化学习在工业批次过程控制中的安全性与稳定性问题，将其与成熟的迭代学习控制方法相结合。所提出的IL-CIRL框架采用双层控制架构，并在迭代学习结构中融入基于卡尔曼滤波的状态估计，以引导深度强化学习智能体。实验结果表明，该方法能够系统化地设计出满足操作约束、确保稳定性保证的深度强化学习控制器，以应对多种扰动条件。
Feature-driven reinforcement learning for photovoltaic in continuous intraday trading
Authors: Arega Getaneh Abate, Xiao-Bing Zhang, Xiufeng Liu, Ruyu Liu
First: 2025-10-15T15:19:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T11:29:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sequential intraday electricity trading allows photovoltaic (PV) operators to reduce imbalance settlement costs as forecasts improve throughout the day. Yet deployable trading policies must jointly handle forecast uncertainty, intraday prices, liquidity, and the asymmetric economics of PV imbalance exposure. This paper proposes a feature-driven reinforcement learning (FDRL) framework for intraday PV trading in the Nordic market. Its main methodological contribution is a corrected reward that evaluates performance relative to a no-trade baseline, removing policy-independent noise that can otherwise push reinforcement learning toward inactive policies in high-price regimes. The framework combines this objective with a predominantly linear policy and a closed-form execution surrogate for efficient, interpretable training. In a strict walk-forward evaluation over 2021-2024 across four Nordic bidding zones (DK1, DK2, SE3, SE4), the method delivers statistically significant profit improvements over the spot-only baseline in every zone. Portfolio experiments show that a pooled cross-zone policy can match zone-specific models, while transfer-learning results indicate a two-cluster market structure and effective deployment in new zones with limited local data. The proposed framework offers an interpretable and computationally practical way to reduce imbalance costs, while the transfer results provide guidance for scaling strategies across bidding zones with different market designs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向光伏连续日内交易的特征驱动强化学习
时序性日内电力交易允许光伏运营商在日内预测精度提升时降低不平衡结算成本。然而，可部署的交易策略必须同时处理预测不确定性、日内价格、流动性以及光伏不平衡风险的非对称经济性。本文提出了一种适用于北欧市场的日内光伏交易特征驱动强化学习框架。其主要方法论贡献是引入一种修正奖励函数，该函数以无交易基准为参照评估策略表现，消除了与策略无关的噪声——这类噪声在高价格区间可能迫使强化学习策略趋于无效。该框架将此目标与主导线性策略及闭式执行代理相结合，实现高效且可解释的训练。在2021-2024年间对北欧四个竞价区（DK1、DK2、SE3、SE4）的严格滚动前进评估表明，该方法在所有区域均实现了较纯现货基准的统计显著利润提升。组合实验显示，跨区域聚合策略可达到区域专用模型水平，而迁移学习结果揭示了市场的双簇结构，并证明在本地数据有限的新区域仍能有效部署。所提框架提供了一种可解释且计算可行的不平衡成本削减方案，迁移结果则为跨不同市场设计的竞价区扩展策略提供了实践指引。

This paper addresses the challenge for photovoltaic operators to reduce imbalance costs through sequential intraday electricity trading, which must account for forecast uncertainty, price dynamics, liquidity, and asymmetric imbalance economics. The authors propose a feature-driven reinforcement learning framework with a corrected reward function that evaluates performance relative to a no-trade baseline to avoid policy inertia, combined with a predominantly linear policy and a closed-form execution surrogate for efficient and interpretable training. In a walk-forward evaluation from 2021 to 2024 across four Nordic bidding zones, the method achieved statistically significant profit improvements over a spot-only baseline, and portfolio experiments demonstrated that a pooled cross-zone policy can match zone-specific models while transfer learning revealed a two-cluster market structure enabling effective deployment in new zones with limited data.
本文针对光伏运营商在连续日内电力交易中降低不平衡成本的挑战，该交易需综合考虑预测不确定性、价格动态、流动性和不对称的不平衡经济性。作者提出了一种特征驱动的强化学习框架，采用校正后的奖励函数以无交易基准评估性能，避免策略惰性，并结合了以线性为主的策略和封闭式执行代理，以实现高效且可解释的训练。在2021年至2024年对北欧四个竞价区的滚动前向评估中，该方法相比仅现货基准实现了统计显著的利润提升，投资组合实验表明跨区池化策略可与特定区域模型相媲美，而迁移学习结果揭示了市场存在两簇结构，使得在数据有限的新区域中也能有效部署。
Safe Flow Q-Learning: Offline Safe Reinforcement Learning with Reachability-Based Flow Policies
Authors: Mumuksh Tayal, Manan Tayal, Ravi Prakash
First: 2026-03-16T11:28:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T11:28:47+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 6 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline safe reinforcement learning (RL) seeks reward-maximizing policies from static datasets under strict safety constraints. Existing methods often rely on soft expected-cost objectives or iterative generative inference, which can be insufficient for safety-critical real-time control. We propose Safe Flow Q-Learning (SafeFQL), which extends FQL to safe offline RL by combining a Hamilton--Jacobi reachability-inspired safety value function with an efficient one-step flow policy. SafeFQL learns the safety value via a self-consistency Bellman recursion, trains a flow policy by behavioral cloning, and distills it into a one-step actor for reward-maximizing safe action selection without rejection sampling at deployment. To account for finite-data approximation error in the learned safety boundary, we add a conformal prediction calibration step that adjusts the safety threshold and provides finite-sample probabilistic safety coverage. Empirically, SafeFQL trades modestly higher offline training cost for substantially lower inference latency than diffusion-style safe generative baselines, which is advantageous for real-time safety-critical deployment. Across boat navigation, and Safety Gymnasium MuJoCo tasks, SafeFQL matches or exceeds prior offline safe RL performance while substantially reducing constraint violations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：安全流Q学习：基于可达性流策略的离线安全强化学习
离线安全强化学习旨在从静态数据集中学习满足严格安全约束的奖励最大化策略。现有方法常依赖软期望成本目标或迭代生成推断，对安全关键实时控制存在不足。本文提出安全流Q学习（SafeFQL），通过将汉密尔顿-雅可比可达性启发的安全值函数与高效单步流策略结合，将FQL扩展至安全离线强化学习。SafeFQL通过自洽贝尔曼递归学习安全值函数，通过行为克隆训练流策略，并将其蒸馏为单步执行器，在部署时无需拒绝采样即可实现奖励最大化的安全动作选择。针对学习安全边界的有限数据近似误差，我们增加了共形预测校准步骤以调整安全阈值并提供有限样本概率安全覆盖。实验表明，相比扩散式安全生成基线方法，SafeFQL以适度增加的离线训练成本显著降低推理延迟，这对实时安全关键部署具有优势。在船舶导航与Safety Gymnasium MuJoCo任务中，SafeFQL达到或超越现有离线安全强化学习性能，同时大幅减少约束违反。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of offline safe reinforcement learning, where policies must maximize reward from static datasets while strictly adhering to safety constraints, a critical need for real-time control applications where existing methods relying on soft cost objectives or iterative inference can be inadequate. The proposed method, Safe Flow Q-Learning (SafeFQL), extends Flow Q-Learning by integrating a Hamilton-Jacobi reachability-inspired safety value function with an efficient one-step flow policy; it learns the safety value via a self-consistency Bellman recursion, trains the flow policy through behavioral cloning, and distills it into a one-step actor for safe action selection without deployment-time rejection sampling, supplemented by a conformal prediction step to calibrate the safety threshold for probabilistic coverage against finite-data errors. Experimental results on boat navigation and Safety Gymnasium MuJoCo tasks demonstrate that SafeFQL matches or surpasses prior offline safe RL performance with significantly fewer constraint violations, trading moderately higher offline training costs for substantially lower inference latency compared to diffusion-based baselines, making it advantageous for safety-critical real-time deployment.
本文针对离线安全强化学习中的挑战，即从静态数据集中学习策略时需在严格安全约束下最大化奖励，这对实时控制应用至关重要，而现有基于软成本目标或迭代推理的方法往往不足。所提出的方法Safe Flow Q-Learning（SafeFQL）通过将汉密尔顿-雅可比可达性启发的安全值函数与高效的一步流策略相结合，扩展了流Q学习；它通过自洽贝尔曼递归学习安全值，通过行为克隆训练流策略，并将其蒸馏为一步执行器以在部署时无需拒绝采样即可选择安全动作，并辅以共形预测步骤来校准安全阈值，以应对有限数据误差提供概率安全覆盖。在船舶导航和安全健身房MuJoCo任务上的实验结果表明，SafeFQL匹配或超越了先前离线安全强化学习的性能，同时显著减少了约束违反，与基于扩散的基线相比，以适度增加的离线训练成本换取了大幅降低的推理延迟，这使其在安全关键的实时部署中具有优势。
Sampling-guided exploration of active feature selection policies
Authors: Gabriel Bernardino, Anders Jonsson, Patrick Clarysse, Nicolas Duchateau
First: 2026-03-16T11:07:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T11:07:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Determining the most appropriate features for machine learning predictive models is challenging regarding performance and feature acquisition costs. In particular, global feature choice is limited given that some features will only benefit a subset of instances. In previous work, we proposed a reinforcement learning approach to sequentially recommend which modality to acquire next to reach the best information/cost ratio, based on the instance-specific information already acquired. We formulated the problem as a Markov Decision Process where the state's dimensionality changes during the episode, avoiding data imputation, contrary to existing works. However, this only allowed processing a small number of features, as all possible combinations of features were considered. Here, we address these limitations with two contributions: 1) we expand our framework to larger datasets with a heuristic-based strategy that focuses on the most promising feature combinations, and 2) we introduce a post-fit regularisation strategy that reduces the number of different feature combinations, leading to compact sequences of decisions. We tested our method on four binary classification datasets (one involving high-dimensional variables), the largest of which had 56 features and 4500 samples. We obtained better performance than state-of-the-art methods, both in terms of accuracy and policy complexity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于采样的主动特征选择策略探索
为机器学习预测模型确定最合适的特征在性能和特征获取成本方面均具挑战性。特别是全局特征选择受限，因为某些特征仅对部分实例有益。先前工作中，我们提出一种强化学习方法，基于已获取的实例特定信息，按顺序推荐下一步应获取哪种模态以达到最佳信息/成本比。我们将该问题建模为马尔可夫决策过程，其状态维度在过程中动态变化，避免了数据插补，与现有方法不同。然而，由于需考虑所有可能的特征组合，该方法仅能处理少量特征。本文通过两项改进突破这些限制：1）采用启发式策略扩展框架至更大数据集，聚焦于最有潜力的特征组合；2）引入后拟合正则化策略，减少不同特征组合的数量，从而生成紧凑的决策序列。我们在四个二元分类数据集（其中一个包含高维变量）上测试了方法，最大数据集含56个特征和4500个样本。实验表明，该方法在准确率和策略复杂度方面均优于现有先进方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of active feature selection for machine learning, where acquiring all features is costly and not all features benefit every instance equally. To overcome the computational limitations of evaluating all feature combinations in prior reinforcement learning approaches, the authors propose a heuristic-based strategy to focus on promising feature subsets and a post-fit regularization method to simplify decision sequences. Experimental results on four binary classification datasets, including one with high-dimensional data, demonstrate that the method outperforms state-of-the-art techniques in both accuracy and policy complexity.
本文针对机器学习中主动特征选择的挑战，即获取所有特征成本高昂且并非所有特征对每个实例都有同等益处。为了克服先前强化学习方法中评估所有特征组合的计算限制，作者提出了一种基于启发式的策略来聚焦有潜力的特征子集，以及一种后拟合正则化方法来简化决策序列。在四个二元分类数据集（包括一个高维数据）上的实验结果表明，该方法在准确性和策略复杂性方面均优于现有先进技术。
PrototypeNAS: Rapid Design of Deep Neural Networks for Microcontroller Units
Authors: Mark Deutel, Simon Geis, Axel Plinge
First: 2026-03-16T10:59:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:59:19+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 6 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Enabling efficient deep neural network (DNN) inference on edge devices with different hardware constraints is a challenging task that typically requires DNN architectures to be specialized for each device separately. To avoid the huge manual effort, one can use neural architecture search (NAS). However, many existing NAS methods are resource-intensive and time-consuming because they require the training of many different DNNs from scratch. Furthermore, they do not take the resource constraints of the target system into account. To address these shortcomings, we propose PrototypeNAS, a zero-shot NAS method to accelerate and automate the selection, compression, and specialization of DNNs to different target microcontroller units (MCUs). We propose a novel three-step search method that decouples DNN design and specialization from DNN training for a given target platform. First, we present a novel search space that not only cuts out smaller DNNs from a single large architecture, but instead combines the structural optimization of multiple architecture types, as well as optimization of their pruning and quantization configurations. Second, we explore the use of an ensemble of zero-shot proxies during optimization instead of a single one. Third, we propose the use of Hypervolume subset selection to distill DNN architectures from the Pareto front of the multi-objective optimization that represent the most meaningful tradeoffs between accuracy and FLOPs. We evaluate the effectiveness of PrototypeNAS on 12 different datasets in three different tasks: image classification, time series classification, and object detection. Our results demonstrate that PrototypeNAS is able to identify DNN models within minutes that are small enough to be deployed on off-the-shelf MCUs and still achieve accuracies comparable to the performance of large DNN models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PrototypeNAS：面向微控制器单元的深度神经网络快速设计方法
在具有不同硬件约束的边缘设备上实现高效的深度神经网络推理是一项挑战性任务，通常需要为每个设备单独定制DNN架构。为避免巨大的人工成本，可采用神经架构搜索技术。然而，现有许多NAS方法因需从头训练大量不同DNN而资源密集且耗时，且未考虑目标系统的资源约束。为此，我们提出PrototypeNAS——一种零样本NAS方法，用于加速和自动化DNN的选择、压缩及针对不同微控制器的定制化。我们提出新颖的三步搜索法，将DNN设计与定制从目标平台的训练过程中解耦：首先构建新型搜索空间，不仅能从单一大型架构中裁剪小型DNN，还能融合多种架构类型的结构优化及其剪枝与量化配置优化；其次在优化过程中采用零样本代理集成而非单一代理；最后提出使用超体积子集选择法，从多目标优化的帕累托前沿中提取能最佳平衡精度与计算量的DNN架构。我们在图像分类、时间序列分类和目标检测三类任务的12个数据集上评估PrototypeNAS，结果表明该方法能在数分钟内识别出可部署于商用MCU的微型DNN模型，其精度仍可与大型DNN模型相媲美。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for PrototypeNAS is to automate the design of efficient deep neural networks for microcontroller units (MCUs) without the resource-intensive training of many models from scratch, as typical neural architecture search (NAS) methods do. The method introduces a zero-shot NAS approach with a three-step process: it defines a novel search space combining structural optimization, pruning, and quantization; uses an ensemble of zero-shot proxies for evaluation; and applies Hypervolume subset selection to extract optimal architectures from a Pareto front balancing accuracy and computational cost (FLOPs). Experimental results across 12 datasets for image classification, time-series classification, and object detection show that PrototypeNAS can quickly identify compact DNN models deployable on standard MCUs while maintaining accuracy comparable to larger models.
PrototypeNAS 的动机是为微控制器单元（MCU）自动设计高效的深度神经网络，避免传统神经架构搜索（NAS）方法需要从头训练大量模型的高资源消耗问题。该方法提出了一种零样本NAS流程，包含三个步骤：定义了一个结合结构优化、剪枝和量化的新型搜索空间；使用零样本代理集成进行评估；并应用超体积子集选择从平衡精度和计算成本（FLOPs）的帕累托前沿中提取最优架构。在图像分类、时间序列分类和目标检测的12个数据集上的实验结果表明，PrototypeNAS 能快速识别出可在标准MCU上部署的紧凑DNN模型，同时保持与大型模型相当的精度。
Delphos: A reinforcement learning framework for assisting discrete choice model specification
Authors: Gabriel Nova, Stephane Hess, Sander van Cranenburgh
First: 2025-06-06T15:40:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:58:11+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Delphos, a deep reinforcement learning framework for assisting the discrete choice model specification process. Delphos aims to support the modeller by providing automated, data-driven suggestions for utility specifications, thereby reducing the effort required to develop and refine utility functions. Delphos conceptualises model specification as a sequential decision-making problem, inspired by the way human choice modellers iteratively construct models through a series of reasoned specification decisions. In this setting, an agent learns to specify high-performing candidate models by choosing a sequence of modelling actions, such as selecting variables, accommodating both generic and alternative-specific taste parameters, applying non-linear transformations, and including interactions with covariates, while interacting with a modelling environment that estimates each candidate and returns a reward signal. Specifically, Delphos uses a Deep Q-Network that receives delayed rewards based on modelling outcomes (e.g., log-likelihood) and behavioural expectations (e.g., parameter signs), and distributes this signal across the sequence of actions to learn which modelling decisions lead to well-performing candidates. We evaluate Delphos on both simulated and empirical datasets using multiple reward settings. In simulated cases, learning curves, Q-value patterns, and performance metrics show that the agent learns to adaptively explore strategies to propose well-performing models across search spaces, while covering only a small fraction of the feasible modelling space. We further apply the framework to two empirical datasets to demonstrate its practical use. These experiments illustrate the ability of Delphos to generate competitive, behaviourally plausible models and highlight the potential of this adaptive, learning-based framework to assist the model specification process.
中文标题/摘要

本文介绍Delphos——一个用于辅助离散选择模型设定过程的深度强化学习框架。该框架旨在通过提供数据驱动的效用函数自动设定建议，降低构建与优化效用函数所需的工作量。Delphos将模型设定概念化为序列决策问题，其设计灵感来源于人类建模者通过一系列理性设定决策迭代构建模型的方式。在此框架中，智能体通过与建模环境交互（该环境负责评估每个候选模型并返回奖励信号），学习通过选择建模动作序列（如变量选择、通用/备选特定偏好参数设置、非线性变换应用、协变量交互项引入等）来设定高性能候选模型。具体而言，Delphos采用深度Q网络接收基于建模结果（如对数似然值）和行为预期（如参数符号）的延迟奖励，并将该信号分配到动作序列中以学习哪些建模决策能产生性能优异的候选模型。我们通过模拟与实证数据集在多种奖励设置下评估Delphos：模拟案例中的学习曲线、Q值模式和性能指标表明，智能体能够学习自适应探索策略，在仅覆盖可行建模空间极小部分的情况下，提出跨搜索空间的高性能模型；两个实证数据集的应用进一步展示了框架的实用价值。实验证明Delphos能生成具有竞争力且行为合理的模型，凸显了这种基于自适应学习的框架在辅助模型设定过程中的潜力。

Experimental results on simulated and empirical datasets show that the agent efficiently explores the search space to propose high-performing, behaviorally plausible models while covering only a small fraction of possible specifications, demonstrating its practical utility in automating model refinement.

Affordable Precision Agriculture: A Deployment-Oriented Review of Low-Cost, Low-Power Edge AI and TinyML for Resource-Constrained Farming Systems
Authors: Riya Samanta, Bidyut Saha
First: 2026-03-16T10:38:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:38:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Precision agriculture increasingly integrates artificial intelligence to enhance crop monitoring, irrigation management, and resource efficiency. Nevertheless, the vast majority of the current systems are still mostly cloud-based and require reliable connectivity, which hampers the adoption to smaller scale, smallholder farming and underdeveloped country systems. Using recent literature reviews, ranging from 2023 to 2026, this review covers deployments of Edge AI, focused on the evolution and acceptance of Tiny Machine Learning, in low-cost and low-powered agriculture. A hardware-targeted deployment-oriented study has shown pronounced variation in architecture with microcontroller-class platforms i.e. ESP32, STM32, ATMega dominating the inference options, in parallel with single-board computers and UAV-assisted solutions. Quantitative synthesis shows quantization is the dominant optimization strategy; the approach in many works identified: around 50% of such works are quantized, while structured pruning, multi-objective compression and hardware aware neural architecture search are relatively under-researched. Also, resource profiling practices are not uniform: while model size is occasionally reported, explicit flash, RAM, MAC, latency and millijoule level energy metrics are not well documented, hampering reproducibility and cross-system comparison. Moreoever, to bridge the gap between research prototypes and deployment-ready systems, the review also presents a literature-informed deployment perspective in the form of a privacy-preserving layered Edge AI architecture for agriculture, synthesizing the key system-level design insights emerging from the surveyed works. Overall, the findings demonstrate a clear architectural shift toward localized inference with centralized training asymmetry.
中文标题/摘要
标题：经济型精准农业：面向资源受限农业系统的低成本、低功耗边缘AI与微型机器学习部署综述
精准农业日益融合人工智能技术以提升作物监测、灌溉管理和资源利用效率。然而，当前绝大多数系统仍主要基于云端部署并依赖稳定网络连接，这阻碍了其在小规模农户及欠发达地区农业系统的推广应用。本文基于2023至2026年的近期文献，系统综述了边缘AI在低成本、低功耗农业场景中的部署实践，重点关注微型机器学习的技术演进与应用现状。一项面向硬件部署的研究显示，系统架构呈现显著差异：微控制器级平台（如ESP32、STM32、ATMega）在推理方案中占据主导地位，同时单板计算机与无人机辅助解决方案并行发展。量化分析表明，模型量化是主流的优化策略——约50%的研究采用该技术，而结构化剪枝、多目标压缩及硬件感知的神经架构搜索等领域研究相对不足。资源评估实践亦未标准化：模型尺寸偶有报道，但闪存占用、内存消耗、乘加运算量、推理延迟及毫焦级能耗等关键指标普遍缺失，制约了研究的可复现性与跨系统比较。为弥合研究原型与部署就绪系统之间的差距，本文进一步提出一种基于文献的隐私保护分层边缘AI农业架构，整合了现有研究中的关键系统级设计洞见。总体而言，研究发现农业AI系统正朝着'本地化推理-集中化训练'的非对称架构范式清晰转型。
Summary / 总结
This review is motivated by the need to adapt precision agriculture's AI capabilities for resource-constrained, small-scale farming systems where cloud dependency and connectivity are barriers. The method involves a deployment-oriented analysis of recent literature on low-cost Edge AI and TinyML, examining hardware platforms, model optimization techniques, and system architectures. The main experimental results highlight a dominant use of microcontroller-class devices like the ESP32 for inference, with model quantization being the most common optimization strategy, while noting significant gaps in standardized resource profiling and under-exploration of techniques like pruning and neural architecture search. The review culminates in proposing a privacy-preserving layered Edge AI architecture to bridge the gap between research and practical deployment, underscoring a broader shift towards localized, asymmetric AI systems in agriculture.
本综述的动机在于，需要使精准农业的人工智能能力适应资源受限的小规模农业系统，因为这些系统中云依赖和网络连接是主要障碍。其方法是对近期关于低成本边缘人工智能和微型机器学习的文献进行面向部署的分析，考察硬件平台、模型优化技术和系统架构。主要实验结果表明，ESP32等微控制器级设备在推理中占主导地位，模型量化是最常见的优化策略，同时指出在标准化资源性能分析方面存在显著差距，且剪枝、神经架构搜索等技术探索不足。该综述最终提出了一个隐私保护的层次化边缘人工智能架构，以弥合研究与实际部署之间的差距，强调了农业向本地化、非对称人工智能系统转变的总体趋势。
Interference-Aware K-Step Reachable Communication in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ziyu Cheng, Jinsheng Ren, Zhouxian Jiang, Chenzhihang Li, Rongye Shi, Bin Liang, Jun Yang
First: 2026-03-16T10:07:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:07:33+00:00
Comments: multi-agent reinforcement learning, communication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Effective communication is pivotal for addressing complex collaborative tasks in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). Yet, limited communication bandwidth and dynamic, intricate environmental topologies present significant challenges in identifying high-value communication partners. Agents must consequently select collaborators under uncertainty, lacking a priori knowledge of which partners can deliver task-critical information. To this end, we propose Interference-Aware K-Step Reachable Communication (IA-KRC), a novel framework that enhances cooperation via two core components: (1) a K-Step reachability protocol that confines message passing to physically accessible neighbors, and (2) an interference-prediction module that optimizes partner choice by minimizing interference while maximizing utility. Compared to existing methods, IA-KRC enables substantially more persistent and efficient cooperation despite environmental interference. Comprehensive evaluations confirm that IA-KRC achieves superior performance compared to state-of-the-art baselines, while demonstrating enhanced robustness and scalability in complex topological and highly dynamic multi-agent scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体强化学习中的干扰感知K步可达通信
在多智能体强化学习（MARL）中，有效通信对解决复杂协作任务至关重要。然而，有限的通信带宽和动态复杂的环境拓扑给识别高价值通信伙伴带来显著挑战。智能体需在不确定性下选择合作者，且缺乏对哪些伙伴能提供任务关键信息的先验知识。为此，我们提出干扰感知K步可达通信（IA-KRC）框架，通过两个核心组件增强协作：（1）K步可达协议，将消息传递限制在物理可访问的邻居范围内；（2）干扰预测模块，通过最小化干扰同时最大化效用优化伙伴选择。与现有方法相比，IA-KRC能在环境干扰下实现更持久高效的协作。综合评估表明，IA-KRC在复杂拓扑和高动态多智能体场景中，相比前沿基线方法具有更优性能，同时展现出更强的鲁棒性和可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenges of limited bandwidth and dynamic topologies in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), which hinder the identification of high-value communication partners, this paper proposes the Interference-Aware K-Step Reachable Communication (IA-KRC) framework. The method introduces a K-step reachability protocol to restrict communication to physically accessible neighbors and an interference-prediction module to optimize partner selection by balancing utility maximization with interference minimization. Experimental results demonstrate that IA-KRC achieves superior performance, robustness, and scalability compared to state-of-the-art baselines in complex, dynamic multi-agent scenarios, enabling more persistent and efficient cooperation.
本文针对多智能体强化学习中因通信带宽有限和环境拓扑动态复杂而难以识别高价值通信伙伴的挑战，提出了干扰感知K步可达通信（IA-KRC）框架。该方法的核心包括一个将消息传递限制在物理可达邻居的K步可达协议，以及一个通过最小化干扰、最大化效用来优化伙伴选择的干扰预测模块。实验结果表明，在复杂的拓扑和高度动态的多智能体场景中，IA-KRC相比现有先进基线实现了更优的性能，并展现出更强的鲁棒性和可扩展性，促进了更持久高效的合作。
Shorten After You're Right: Lazy Length Penalties for Reasoning RL
Authors: Danlong Yuan, Tian Xie, Shaohan Huang, Zhuocheng Gong, Huishuai Zhang, Chong Luo, Furu Wei, Dongyan Zhao
First: 2025-05-18T07:46:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:03:58+00:00
Comments: Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large reasoning models, such as OpenAI o1 or DeepSeek R1, have demonstrated remarkable performance on reasoning tasks but often incur a long reasoning path with significant memory and time costs. Existing methods primarily aim to shorten reasoning paths by introducing additional training data and stages. In this paper, we propose three critical reward designs integrated directly into the reinforcement learning process of large reasoning models, which reduce the response length without extra training stages. Experiments on four settings show that our method significantly decreases response length while maintaining or even improving performance. Specifically, in a logic reasoning setting, we achieve a 40% reduction in response length averaged by steps alongside a 14% gain in performance. For math problems, we reduce response length averaged by steps by 33% while preserving performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：正确后即缩短：推理强化学习中的惰性长度惩罚机制
大型推理模型（如OpenAI o1或DeepSeek R1）在推理任务中展现出卓越性能，但其冗长的推理路径常伴随高昂的内存与时间开销。现有方法主要通过引入额外训练数据和阶段来缩短推理路径。本文提出三种关键奖励设计，直接集成至大型推理模型的强化学习过程中，无需额外训练阶段即可缩减响应长度。在四种实验场景中，本方法在保持甚至提升性能的同时显著降低响应长度。具体而言，在逻辑推理场景中，我们实现了步骤平均响应长度减少40%，同时性能提升14%；在数学问题场景中，步骤平均响应长度减少33%且性能保持不变。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the inefficiency of large reasoning models, which often produce lengthy reasoning paths that incur high memory and time costs, without requiring additional training stages. The method introduces three novel reward designs integrated directly into the reinforcement learning process to penalize unnecessary reasoning steps and encourage concise outputs. Experimental results across four settings demonstrate that this approach significantly reduces response length while maintaining or improving performance, with a 40% reduction in steps and a 14% performance gain in logic reasoning, and a 33% step reduction in math problems while preserving accuracy.
本研究旨在解决大型推理模型因生成冗长推理路径而导致高内存和时间成本的问题，且无需额外训练阶段。方法是在强化学习过程中直接集成三种关键奖励设计，以惩罚不必要的推理步骤并鼓励简洁输出。在四个实验设置中的结果表明，该方法在保持或提升性能的同时显著缩短了响应长度，在逻辑推理中平均步骤减少40%且性能提升14%，在数学问题上平均步骤减少33%且准确率得以保持。
RoboMD: Uncovering Robot Vulnerabilities through Semantic Potential Fields
Authors: Som Sagar, Jiafei Duan, Sreevishakh Vasudevan, Yifan Zhou, Heni Ben Amor, Dieter Fox, Ransalu Senanayake
First: 2024-12-03T20:34:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T09:03:20+00:00
Comments: 26 Pages, 20 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robot manipulation policies, while central to the promise of physical AI, are highly vulnerable in the presence of external variations in the real world. Diagnosing these vulnerabilities is hindered by two key challenges: (i) the relevant variations to test against are often unknown, and (ii) direct testing in the real world is costly and unsafe. We introduce a framework that tackles both issues by learning a separate deep reinforcement learning (deep RL) policy for vulnerability prediction through virtual runs on a continuous vision-language embedding trained with limited success-failure data. By treating this embedding space, which is rich in semantic and visual variations, as a potential field, the policy learns to move toward vulnerable regions while being repelled from success regions. This vulnerability prediction policy, trained on virtual rollouts, enables scalable and safe vulnerability analysis without expensive physical trials. By querying this policy, our framework builds a probabilistic vulnerability-likelihood map. Experiments across simulation benchmarks and a physical robot arm show that our framework uncovers up to 23% more unique vulnerabilities than state-of-the-art vision-language baselines, revealing subtle vulnerabilities overlooked by heuristic testing. Additionally, we show that fine-tuning the manipulation policy with the vulnerabilities discovered by our framework improves manipulation performance with much less fine-tuning data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RoboMD：通过语义势场揭示机器人脆弱性
机器人操作策略作为物理AI实现的核心，在现实世界外部变化下极为脆弱。诊断这些脆弱性面临两大挑战：(1) 需测试的相关变化往往未知；(2) 现实世界直接测试成本高且不安全。我们提出一种框架，通过在经有限成败数据训练的连续视觉-语言嵌入空间进行虚拟推演，学习独立的深度强化学习策略以预测脆弱性。该嵌入空间富含语义与视觉变化，将其视为势场后，策略学会向脆弱区域移动并远离成功区域。这种通过虚拟推演训练的脆弱性预测策略，无需昂贵物理试验即可实现可扩展的安全脆弱性分析。通过查询该策略，框架构建出概率化脆弱性似然图。在仿真基准与实体机械臂上的实验表明，本框架比最先进的视觉-语言基线多发现23%的独特脆弱性，能揭示启发式测试忽略的细微漏洞。此外，利用框架发现的脆弱性对操作策略进行微调，能以更少的微调数据显著提升操作性能。
