The paper is motivated by the need to diagnose vulnerabilities in robot manipulation policies, which are sensitive to real-world variations, but direct testing is costly and unknown variations hinder diagnosis. The method introduces a framework that learns a deep RL policy for vulnerability prediction by performing virtual rollouts on a continuous vision-language embedding, treating it as a semantic potential field to guide exploration toward vulnerable regions. Experimental results across simulation and a physical robot arm show the framework uncovers up to 23% more unique vulnerabilities than vision-language baselines, and fine-tuning with these vulnerabilities improves manipulation performance with less data.
本文的动机是诊断机器人操作策略的脆弱性，这些策略对现实世界变化敏感，但直接测试成本高且未知变化阻碍诊断。方法提出一个框架，通过在连续视觉语言嵌入上进行虚拟推演来学习深度强化学习策略进行脆弱性预测，将其视为语义势场以引导探索脆弱区域。实验结果表明，在仿真和物理机械臂上，该框架比现有视觉语言基线多发现高达23%的独特脆弱性，且利用这些脆弱性进行微调能以更少数据提升操作性能。
Fuz-RL: A Fuzzy-Guided Robust Framework for Safe Reinforcement Learning under Uncertainty
Authors: Xu Wan, Chao Yang, Cheng Yang, Jie Song, Mingyang Sun
First: 2026-02-24T09:50:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T08:28:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safe Reinforcement Learning (RL) is crucial for achieving high performance while ensuring safety in real-world applications. However, the complex interplay of multiple uncertainty sources in real environments poses significant challenges for interpretable risk assessment and robust decision-making. To address these challenges, we propose Fuz-RL, a fuzzy measure-guided robust framework for safe RL. Specifically, our framework develops a novel fuzzy Bellman operator for estimating robust value functions using Choquet integrals. Theoretically, we prove that solving the Fuz-RL problem (in Constrained Markov Decision Process (CMDP) form) is equivalent to solving distributionally robust safe RL problems (in robust CMDP form), effectively avoiding min-max optimization. Empirical analyses on safe-control-gym and safety-gymnasium scenarios demonstrate that Fuz-RL effectively integrates with existing safe RL baselines in a model-free manner, significantly improving both safety and control performance under various types of uncertainties in observation, action, and dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Fuz-RL：一种模糊引导的鲁棒框架，用于不确定性下的安全强化学习
安全强化学习（RL）对于在现实应用中确保安全的同时实现高性能至关重要。然而，真实环境中多种不确定性源的复杂交互，为可解释的风险评估和鲁棒决策带来了重大挑战。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了Fuz-RL，一种基于模糊测度引导的鲁棒框架，用于安全RL。具体而言，该框架通过Choquet积分构建了一种新颖的模糊贝尔曼算子，用于估计鲁棒值函数。理论上，我们证明求解Fuz-RL问题（以约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP）形式）等价于求解分布鲁棒的安全RL问题（以鲁棒CMDP形式），从而有效避免了极小极大优化。在safe-control-gym和safety-gymnasium场景上的实证分析表明，Fuz-RL能以无模型方式有效整合现有安全RL基线方法，在观测、动作和动力学等多种不确定性条件下，显著提升安全性和控制性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of ensuring safety in reinforcement learning (RL) under real-world uncertainties, where multiple sources of uncertainty complicate risk assessment and decision-making. It introduces Fuz-RL, a fuzzy measure-guided robust framework that employs a novel fuzzy Bellman operator based on Choquet integrals to estimate robust value functions, theoretically linking it to distributionally robust safe RL problems without requiring min-max optimization. Experimental results on safe-control-gym and safety-gymnasium scenarios show that Fuz-RL integrates model-free with existing safe RL baselines, enhancing both safety and control performance across observation, action, and dynamics uncertainties.
本文针对强化学习在现实世界不确定性下确保安全性的挑战，其中多种不确定性来源使得风险评估和决策变得复杂。它提出了Fuz-RL，一个模糊测度引导的鲁棒框架，采用基于Choquet积分的新型模糊贝尔曼算子来估计鲁棒值函数，理论上将其与分布鲁棒安全强化学习问题等价，避免了最小-最大优化。在safe-control-gym和safety-gymnasium场景上的实验结果表明，Fuz-RL以无模型方式与现有安全强化学习基线集成，在观测、动作和动力学等多种不确定性下显著提升了安全性和控制性能。
Masked Auto-Regressive Variational Acceleration: Fast Inference Makes Practical Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuxuan Gu, Weimin Bai, Yifei Wang, Weijian Luo, He Sun
First: 2025-11-19T07:24:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T08:01:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Masked auto-regressive diffusion models (MAR) benefit from the expressive modeling ability of diffusion models and the flexibility of masked auto-regressive ordering. However, vanilla MAR suffers from slow inference due to its hierarchical inference mechanism: an outer AR unmasking loop and an inner diffusion denoising chain. Such decoupled structure not only harm the generation efficiency but also hinder the practical use of MAR for reinforcement learning (RL), an increasingly critical paradigm for generative model post-training.To address this fundamental issue, we introduce MARVAL (Masked Auto-regressive Variational Acceleration), a distillation-based framework that compresses the diffusion chain into a single AR generation step while preserving the flexible auto-regressive unmasking order. Such a distillation with MARVAL not only yields substantial inference acceleration but, crucially, makes RL post-training with verifiable rewards practical, resulting in scalable yet human-preferred fast generative models. Our contributions are twofold: (1) a novel score-based variational objective for distilling masked auto-regressive diffusion models into a single generation step without sacrificing sample quality; and (2) an efficient RL framework for masked auto-regressive models via MARVAL-RL. On ImageNet 256*256, MARVAL-Huge achieves an FID of 2.00 with more than 30 times speedup compared with MAR-diffusion, and MARVAL-RL yields consistent improvements in CLIP and image-reward scores on ImageNet datasets with entity names. In conclusion, MARVAL demonstrates the first practical path to distillation and RL of masked auto-regressive diffusion models, enabling fast sampling and better preference alignments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：掩码自回归变分加速：快速推理实现实用强化学习
掩码自回归扩散模型（MAR）结合了扩散模型的强大建模能力与掩码自回归排序的灵活性，但其分层推理机制（外层自回归解掩循环与内层扩散去噪链）导致推理速度缓慢。这种解耦结构不仅影响生成效率，也阻碍了MAR在强化学习（RL）中的实际应用。为解决这一问题，我们提出MARVAL（掩码自回归变分加速），这是一个基于蒸馏的框架，可将扩散链压缩为单步自回归生成，同时保留灵活的解掩顺序。MARVAL蒸馏不仅实现了显著的推理加速，更关键的是使基于可验证奖励的RL后训练变得实用，从而构建出可扩展且符合人类偏好的快速生成模型。我们的贡献包括：（1）提出基于分数的变分目标，将掩码自回归扩散模型蒸馏为单步生成且不损失样本质量；（2）通过MARVAL-RL为掩码自回归模型构建高效RL框架。在ImageNet 256*256数据集上，MARVAL-Huge以2.00的FID指标实现超过MAR扩散模型30倍的加速，MARVAL-RL在包含实体名称的ImageNet数据集中持续提升CLIP与图像奖励分数。综上，MARVAL首次为掩码自回归扩散模型提供了实用的蒸馏与RL路径，实现了快速采样与更好的偏好对齐。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the slow inference problem of masked auto-regressive diffusion models (MAR), which limits their practical use in reinforcement learning (RL) due to a hierarchical structure involving an outer auto-regressive loop and an inner diffusion chain. To solve this, the authors propose MARVAL, a distillation framework that compresses the diffusion process into a single auto-regressive step while maintaining flexible unmasking order, enabling fast inference and making RL post-training feasible. Experimental results on ImageNet 256*256 show that MARVAL-Huge achieves an FID of 2.00 with over 30 times speedup compared to MAR-diffusion, and MARVAL-RL improves CLIP and image-reward scores, demonstrating effective preference alignment.
该论文针对掩码自回归扩散模型（MAR）推理速度慢的问题，其分层结构（外层自回归循环和内层扩散链）限制了在强化学习（RL）中的实际应用。为此，作者提出了MARVAL，一个蒸馏框架，将扩散过程压缩为单步自回归生成，同时保持灵活的掩码解除顺序，从而实现快速推理并使RL后训练变得可行。在ImageNet 256*256上的实验结果表明，MARVAL-Huge实现了2.00的FID分数，相比MAR-diffusion加速超过30倍，且MARVAL-RL在CLIP和图像奖励分数上均有提升，证明了其有效的偏好对齐能力。
On the Adversarial Transferability of Generalized "Skip Connections"
Authors: Yisen Wang, Yichuan Mo, Dongxian Wu, Mingjie Li, Xingjun Ma, Zhouchen Lin
Venue: IEEE Transactions on Pattern Analysis and Machine Intelligence, 2026
First: 2024-10-11T16:17:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T07:53:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Skip connection is an essential ingredient for modern deep models to be deeper and more powerful. Despite their huge success in normal scenarios (state-of-the-art classification performance on natural examples), we investigate and identify an interesting property of skip connections under adversarial scenarios, namely, the use of skip connections allows easier generation of highly transferable adversarial examples. Specifically, in ResNet-like models (with skip connections), we find that biasing backpropagation to favor gradients from skip connections--while suppressing those from residual modules via a decay factor--allows one to craft adversarial examples with high transferability. Based on this insight, we propose the Skip Gradient Method (SGM). Although starting from ResNet-like models in vision domains, we further extend SGM to more advanced architectures, including Vision Transformers (ViTs), models with varying-length paths, and other domains such as natural language processing. We conduct comprehensive transfer-based attacks against diverse model families, including ResNets, Transformers, Inceptions, Neural Architecture Search-based models, and Large Language Models (LLMs). The results demonstrate that employing SGM can greatly improve the transferability of crafted attacks in almost all cases. Furthermore, we demonstrate that SGM can still be effective under more challenging settings such as ensemble-based attacks, targeted attacks, and against defense equipped models. At last, we provide theoretical explanations and empirical insights on how SGM works. Our findings not only motivate new adversarial research into the architectural characteristics of models but also open up further challenges for secure model architecture design. Our code is available at https://github.com/mo666666/SGM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：论广义“跳跃连接”的对抗迁移性
跳跃连接是现代深度模型实现更深层、更强大性能的关键要素。尽管其在正常场景下（在自然样本上达到最先进的分类性能）取得了巨大成功，本研究探索并揭示了跳跃连接在对抗场景下的一个有趣特性：跳跃连接的使用使得生成高迁移性的对抗样本更为容易。具体而言，在类ResNet模型（含跳跃连接）中，我们发现通过衰减因子抑制残差模块梯度、同时偏置反向传播以强化跳跃连接梯度的方式，能够构造出具有高迁移性的对抗样本。基于这一洞见，我们提出了跳跃梯度方法（SGM）。虽然最初针对视觉领域的类ResNet模型，我们进一步将SGM扩展至更先进的架构，包括视觉Transformer（ViT）、可变路径长度模型以及自然语言处理等其他领域。我们对多种模型族开展了全面的基于迁移的攻击实验，涵盖ResNet、Transformer、Inception、基于神经架构搜索的模型以及大语言模型（LLM）。结果表明，在几乎所有情况下采用SGM都能显著提升所构造攻击的迁移性。此外，我们验证了SGM在更具挑战性的场景中依然有效，包括基于集成的攻击、定向攻击以及针对具备防御机制的模型。最后，我们从理论解释和实证角度阐明了SGM的作用机理。本研究的发现不仅为针对模型架构特性的对抗研究提供了新思路，也为安全模型架构设计提出了进一步挑战。代码已开源：https://github.com/mo666666/SGM。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the role of skip connections in deep neural networks under adversarial conditions, motivated by the observation that these architectural components, while beneficial for standard performance, may facilitate the generation of highly transferable adversarial examples. The method introduces the Skip Gradient Method (SGM), which biases backpropagation to prioritize gradients from skip connections over those from residual modules via a decay factor, thereby crafting more transferable adversarial attacks. Experimental results across diverse model families, including ResNets, Vision Transformers, Inception networks, and even Large Language Models, demonstrate that SGM significantly enhances attack transferability in nearly all cases, including challenging scenarios like ensemble-based and targeted attacks, while also providing theoretical and empirical insights into its effectiveness.
本文研究了深度神经网络中跳跃连接在对抗场景下的作用，其动机是观察到这种虽然有益于标准性能的架构组件，可能更容易生成高迁移性的对抗样本。方法上提出了跳跃梯度方法（SGM），该方法通过衰减因子使反向传播过程偏向跳跃连接的梯度，同时抑制残差模块的梯度，从而生成迁移性更强的对抗攻击。实验结果表明，在包括ResNet、视觉Transformer、Inception网络乃至大语言模型在内的多种模型族上，SGM几乎在所有情况下都能显著提升攻击的迁移性，包括集成攻击、定向攻击等更具挑战性的场景，同时为SGM的有效性提供了理论和实证解释。
Buffer Matters: Unleashing the Power of Off-Policy Reinforcement Learning in Large Language Model Reasoning
Authors: Xu Wan, Yansheng Wang, Wenqi Huang, Mingyang Sun
First: 2026-02-24T09:35:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T07:07:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional on-policy Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) frameworks suffer from experience waste and reward homogeneity, which directly hinders learning efficiency on difficult samples during large language models post-training. In this paper, we introduce Batch Adaptation Policy Optimization (BAPO), an off-policy RLVR framework to improve the data efficiency in large language models post-training. It dynamically selects training batches by re-evaluating historically difficult samples and reusing high-quality ones, while holding a lower bound guarantee for policy improvement. Extensive experiments further demonstrate that BAPO achieves an average 12.5% improvement over GRPO across mathematics, planning, and visual reasoning tasks. Crucially, BAPO successfully resolves 40.7% of problems that base models consistently fail to solve.
中文标题/摘要
标题：缓冲区的重要性：释放离线策略强化学习在大语言模型推理中的潜力
传统的基于可验证奖励的在线策略强化学习框架存在经验浪费和奖励同质化问题，这直接阻碍了大语言模型后训练阶段在困难样本上的学习效率。本文提出批量自适应策略优化，一种离线策略的RLVR框架，旨在提升大语言模型后训练的数据效率。该框架通过重新评估历史困难样本并复用高质量样本，动态选择训练批次，同时为策略改进提供下界保证。大量实验进一步表明，在数学、规划和视觉推理任务上，BAPO相比GRPO平均提升12.5%。关键的是，BAPO成功解决了基础模型持续无法解决的40.7%的问题。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiencies of on-policy reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) in large language model post-training, which suffers from experience waste and reward homogeneity, this paper proposes Batch Adaptation Policy Optimization (BAPO), an off-policy RLVR framework. The method dynamically selects training batches by re-evaluating historically difficult samples and reusing high-quality ones, while ensuring a theoretical lower bound for policy improvement. Experimental results show that BAPO achieves an average 12.5% performance improvement over GRPO across mathematics, planning, and visual reasoning tasks, and successfully resolves 40.7% of problems that base models consistently fail to solve.
针对传统基于策略的强化学习与可验证奖励框架在大语言模型后训练中存在经验浪费和奖励同质化、阻碍困难样本学习效率的问题，本文提出了批量自适应策略优化方法，一种离策略的强化学习框架。该方法通过重新评估历史困难样本并重用高质量样本，动态选择训练批次，同时保证了策略改进的理论下界。主要实验结果表明，该方法在数学、规划和视觉推理任务上平均性能比GRPO提升12.5%，并成功解决了基础模型持续无法解决的40.7%的问题。
Generating solution paths of Markovian stochastic differential equations using diffusion models
Authors: Xuefeng Gao, Jiale Zha, Xun Yu Zhou
First: 2025-09-10T16:17:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:58:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces a new approach to generating sample paths of unknown Markovian stochastic differential equations (SDEs) using diffusion models, a class of generative AI methods commonly employed in image and video applications. Unlike the traditional Monte Carlo methods for simulating SDEs, which require explicit specifications of the drift and diffusion coefficients, ours takes a model-free, data-driven approach. Given a finite set of sample paths from an SDE, we utilize conditional diffusion models to generate new, synthetic paths of the same SDE. Numerical experiments show that our method consistently outperforms two alternative methods in terms of the Kullback--Leibler (KL) divergence between the distributions of the target SDE paths and the generated ones. Moreover, we present a theoretical error analysis deriving an explicit bound on the said KL divergence. Finally, in simulation and empirical studies, we leverage these synthetically generated sample paths to boost the performance of reinforcement learning algorithms for continuous-time mean--variance portfolio selection, hinting promising applications of our study in financial analysis and decision-making.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用扩散模型生成马尔可夫随机微分方程的解路径
本文提出了一种新方法，利用扩散模型（一类常用于图像和视频生成的生成式人工智能方法）生成未知马尔可夫随机微分方程（SDE）的样本路径。与模拟SDE的传统蒙特卡洛方法需明确指定漂移和扩散系数不同，本方法采用无模型、数据驱动的策略。给定SDE的有限样本路径集，我们利用条件扩散模型生成同一SDE的新合成路径。数值实验表明，在目标SDE路径分布与生成路径分布的Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度方面，本方法持续优于两种替代方法。此外，我们提出了理论误差分析，推导了上述KL散度的显式边界。最后，在模拟与实证研究中，我们利用这些合成样本路径提升连续时间均值-方差投资组合选择强化学习算法的性能，预示了本研究在金融分析与决策中的潜在应用前景。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to generate sample paths for Markovian stochastic differential equations (SDEs) without requiring explicit drift and diffusion coefficients, this paper proposes a model-free, data-driven method using conditional diffusion models. The approach leverages a finite set of existing SDE paths to synthesize new paths, and numerical experiments demonstrate its superiority over alternative methods in terms of lower Kullback-Leibler divergence between generated and target path distributions. Main results include a theoretical error bound on this divergence and empirical applications showing that the synthetic paths enhance reinforcement learning performance in continuous-time mean-variance portfolio selection, indicating potential for financial analysis.
本文针对无需显式漂移和扩散系数即可生成马尔可夫随机微分方程样本路径的需求，提出了一种基于条件扩散模型的无模型数据驱动方法。该方法利用有限现有路径合成新路径，数值实验表明其在生成路径与目标路径分布的KL散度上优于其他方法。主要结果包括该散度的理论误差界，以及实证应用显示合成路径能提升连续时间均值-方差投资组合选择中强化学习的性能，暗示了在金融分析中的潜在应用价值。
GlobalRAG: Enhancing Global Reasoning in Multi-hop Question Answering via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jinchang Luo, Mingquan Cheng, Fan Wan, Ni Li, Xiaoling Xia, Shuangshuang Tian, Tingcheng Bian, Haiwei Wang, Haohuan Fu, Yan Tao
First: 2025-10-23T13:35:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:51:44+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 3 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has recently shown promise in improving retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). Despite these advances, its effectiveness in multi-hop question answering (QA) remains limited by two fundamental limitations: (i) global planning absence to structure multi-step reasoning, and (ii) unfaithful execution, which hinders effective query formulation and consistent use of retrieved evidence. We propose GlobalRAG, a reinforcement learning framework designed to enhance global reasoning in multi-hop QA. GlobalRAG decomposes questions into subgoals, coordinates retrieval with reasoning, and refines evidence iteratively. To guide this process, we introduce Planning Quality Reward and SubGoal Completion Reward, which encourage coherent planning and reliable subgoal execution. In addition, a progressive weight annealing strategy balances process-oriented and outcome-based objectives. Extensive experiments on both in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks demonstrate that GlobalRAG significantly outperforms strong baselines while using only 8k training data (42% of the training data used by strong baselines), achieving average improvements of 14.2% in both EM and F1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GlobalRAG：通过强化学习增强多跳问答中的全局推理能力
强化学习近期在改进检索增强生成（RAG）方面展现出潜力。然而，其在多跳问答（QA）中的有效性仍受限于两个根本问题：（i）缺乏构建多步推理的全局规划；（ii）执行过程不可靠，影响有效查询构建与检索证据的一致性使用。我们提出GlobalRAG——一个旨在增强多跳QA中全局推理的强化学习框架。该框架将问题分解为子目标，协调检索与推理过程，并迭代优化证据。为引导此过程，我们设计了规划质量奖励与子目标完成奖励，以促进连贯规划与可靠执行。此外，渐进式权重退火策略平衡了过程导向与结果导向的目标。在领域内与跨领域基准上的大量实验表明，GlobalRAG仅使用8k训练数据（相当于基线模型训练数据的42%）即显著超越强基线模型，在EM和F1指标上平均提升14.2%。

The paper addresses limitations in applying reinforcement learning to retrieval-augmented generation for multi-hop question answering, specifically the lack of global planning and unfaithful execution that hinder structured reasoning and evidence use. It proposes GlobalRAG, a framework that decomposes questions into subgoals, coordinates retrieval with reasoning, and iteratively refines evidence using novel rewards for planning quality and subgoal completion, along with a progressive weight annealing strategy to balance process and outcome objectives. Experimental results on in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks show that GlobalRAG significantly outperforms strong baselines with only 8k training data, achieving average improvements of 14.2% in both EM and F1 scores.
该论文针对强化学习在检索增强生成中应用于多跳问答时的局限性，即缺乏全局规划和执行不忠实，这阻碍了结构化推理和证据的有效利用。它提出了GlobalRAG框架，通过将问题分解为子目标、协调检索与推理、并迭代优化证据，引入了规划质量奖励和子目标完成奖励来引导过程，同时采用渐进权重退火策略平衡过程与结果目标。在领域内和领域外基准测试上的实验结果表明，GlobalRAG仅使用8k训练数据就显著优于强基线方法，在EM和F1分数上平均提升了14.2%。
MARVL: Multi-Stage Guidance for Robotic Manipulation via Vision-Language Models
Authors: Xunlan Zhou, Xuanlin Chen, Shaowei Zhang, Xiangkun Li, ShengHua Wan, Xiaohai Hu, Lei Yuan, Le Gan, De-chuan Zhan
First: 2026-01-28T11:25:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:30:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing dense reward functions is pivotal for efficient robotic Reinforcement Learning (RL). However, most dense rewards rely on manual engineering, which fundamentally limits the scalability and automation of reinforcement learning. While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) offer a promising path to reward design, naive VLM rewards often misalign with task progress, struggle with spatial grounding, and show limited understanding of task semantics. To address these issues, we propose MARVL-Multi-stAge guidance for Robotic manipulation via Vision-Language models. MARVL fine-tunes a VLM for spatial and semantic consistency and decomposes tasks into multi-stage subtasks with task direction projection for trajectory sensitivity. Empirically, MARVL significantly outperforms existing VLM-reward methods on the Meta-World benchmark, demonstrating superior sample efficiency and robustness on sparse-reward manipulation tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MARVL：基于视觉语言模型的多阶段引导机器人操作框架
设计密集奖励函数对高效机器人强化学习至关重要，但现有方法多依赖人工设计，制约了强化学习的可扩展性与自动化。视觉语言模型虽为奖励设计提供了新途径，但其原始奖励常存在任务进度失准、空间定位困难及语义理解局限等问题。为此，我们提出MARVL——基于视觉语言模型的多阶段机器人操作引导框架。该框架通过微调视觉语言模型提升空间与语义一致性，并利用任务方向投影将任务分解为具有轨迹敏感性的多阶段子任务。实验表明，MARVL在Meta-World基准测试中显著优于现有视觉语言模型奖励方法，在稀疏奖励操作任务上展现出更优的样本效率与鲁棒性。

Experimental results on the Meta-World benchmark show that MARVL significantly outperforms existing VLM-reward methods, achieving superior sample efficiency and robustness in sparse-reward manipulation tasks.

Sample-Efficient Hypergradient Estimation for Decentralized Bi-Level Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mikoto Kudo, Takumi Tanabe, Akifumi Wachi, Youhei Akimoto
First: 2026-03-16T06:11:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:11:00+00:00
Comments: 26 pages. Accepted at ICAPS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many strategic decision-making problems, such as environment design for warehouse robots, can be naturally formulated as bi-level reinforcement learning (RL), where a leader agent optimizes its objective while a follower solves a Markov decision process (MDP) conditioned on the leader's decisions. In many situations, a fundamental challenge arises when the leader cannot intervene in the follower's optimization process; it can only observe the optimization outcome. We address this decentralized setting by deriving the hypergradient of the leader's objective, i.e., the gradient of the leader's strategy that accounts for changes in the follower's optimal policy. Unlike prior hypergradient-based methods that require extensive data for repeated state visits or rely on gradient estimators whose complexity can increase substantially with the high-dimensional leader's decision space, we leverage the Boltzmann covariance trick to derive an alternative hypergradient formulation. This enables efficient hypergradient estimation solely from interaction samples, even when the leader's decision space is high-dimensional. Additionally, to our knowledge, this is the first method that enables hypergradient-based optimization for 2-player Markov games in decentralized settings. Experiments highlight the impact of hypergradient updates and demonstrate our method's effectiveness in both discrete and continuous state tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：去中心化双层强化学习中样本高效的超梯度估计方法
许多战略决策问题（如仓库机器人的环境设计）可自然建模为双层强化学习：领导者智能体优化其目标，而跟随者在领导者决策条件下求解马尔可夫决策过程。当领导者无法干预跟随者优化过程、仅能观测优化结果时，核心挑战随之产生。本文通过推导领导者目标的超梯度（即考虑跟随者最优策略变化的领导者策略梯度）来解决这一去中心化场景。相较于现有需要大量重复状态访问数据、或梯度估计器复杂度随高维决策空间急剧增加的超梯度方法，我们利用玻尔兹曼协方差技巧推导出替代的超梯度形式，实现仅通过交互样本即可高效估计超梯度（即使领导者决策空间为高维）。据我们所知，这是首个在去中心化场景中实现基于超梯度的双人马尔可夫博弈优化的方法。实验验证了超梯度更新的有效性，并在离散与连续状态任务中证明了本方法的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of decentralized bi-level reinforcement learning, where a leader agent must optimize its objective based only on observing the outcomes of a follower's independent optimization process, without direct intervention. To tackle this, the authors derive a hypergradient for the leader's objective by employing the Boltzmann covariance trick, which allows for efficient estimation of this gradient using only interaction samples, even in high-dimensional decision spaces, and extends hypergradient-based optimization to decentralized two-player Markov games. Experimental results demonstrate that the hypergradient updates are impactful and the method is effective across both discrete and continuous state tasks.
本文针对去中心化双层强化学习中的挑战，即领导者智能体只能观察跟随者独立优化过程的结果，而无法直接干预，需据此优化自身目标。为解决此问题，作者利用玻尔兹曼协方差技巧推导了领导者目标的超梯度，使得仅通过交互样本即可高效估计该梯度，即使在高维决策空间中也能适用，并将基于超梯度的优化方法首次扩展到去中心化的双人马尔可夫博弈中。实验结果表明，超梯度更新具有显著影响，且该方法在离散和连续状态任务中均表现出有效性。
Overthinking Reduction with Decoupled Rewards and Curriculum Data Scheduling
Authors: Shuyang Jiang, Yusheng Liao, Ya Zhang, Yanfeng Wang, Yu Wang
Venue: ICLR 2026 oral presentation
First: 2025-09-30T06:04:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T05:33:52+00:00
Comments: 30 pages; Accepted as an oral presentation at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While large reasoning models trained with critic-free reinforcement learning and verifiable rewards (RLVR) represent the state-of-the-art, their practical utility is hampered by ``overthinking'', a critical issue where models generate excessively long reasoning paths without any performance benefit. Existing solutions that penalize length often fail, inducing performance degradation due to a fundamental misalignment between trajectory-level rewards and token-level optimization. In this work, we introduce a novel framework, DECS, built on our theoretical discovery of two previously unaddressed flaws in current length rewards: (1) the erroneous penalization of essential exploratory tokens and (2) the inadvertent rewarding of partial redundancy. Our framework's innovations include (i) a first-of-its-kind decoupled token-level reward mechanism that surgically distinguishes and penalizes redundant tokens, and (ii) a novel curriculum batch scheduling strategy to master the efficiency-efficacy equilibrium. Experimental results show DECS can achieve a dramatic reduction in reasoning tokens by over 50\% across seven benchmarks while simultaneously maintaining or even improving performance. It demonstrates conclusively that substantial gains in reasoning efficiency can be achieved without compromising a model's underlying reasoning power. Code is available at https://github.com/pixas/DECS.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解耦奖励与课程数据调度：对过度思考问题的优化研究
尽管采用无评判强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）训练的大型推理模型代表了当前最高水平，但其实际应用受到“过度思考”问题的严重制约——模型生成过长的推理路径却未带来性能提升。现有惩罚长度的方案常因轨迹级奖励与词元级优化的根本错位而失效，甚至导致性能下降。本研究基于对当前长度奖励机制两个未受重视缺陷的理论发现：（1）对必要探索性词元的错误惩罚；（2）对部分冗余内容的无意奖励，提出了创新框架DECS。该框架包含两大突破：（i）首创的解耦词元级奖励机制，能精准识别并惩罚冗余词元；（ii）创新的课程批次调度策略，以掌握效率与效能的平衡。实验表明，DECS在七个基准测试中实现推理词元量减少超50%，同时保持甚至提升模型性能，确证了在不损害模型底层推理能力的前提下显著提升推理效率的可能性。代码已开源：https://github.com/pixas/DECS。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the problem of 'overthinking' in large reasoning models, where models produce excessively long reasoning paths without performance gains, this paper introduces the DECS framework. The method addresses flaws in existing length-penalty approaches by proposing a decoupled token-level reward mechanism that specifically penalizes redundant tokens and a curriculum batch scheduling strategy to balance efficiency and efficacy. Experimental results across seven benchmarks demonstrate that DECS reduces reasoning tokens by over 50% while maintaining or improving performance, showing that significant efficiency gains can be achieved without compromising reasoning power.
针对大型推理模型中存在的“过度思考”问题，即模型生成过长的推理路径却无性能提升，本文提出了DECS框架。该方法通过引入解耦的令牌级奖励机制来精准惩罚冗余令牌，并采用课程批次调度策略来平衡效率与效果，以解决现有长度惩罚方法的缺陷。在七个基准测试上的实验结果表明，DECS能将推理令牌减少超过50%，同时保持或提升性能，证明了在不损害推理能力的前提下可实现显著的效率提升。
Breaking the SFT Plateau: Multimodal Structured Reinforcement Learning for Chart-to-Code Generation
Authors: Lei Chen, Xuanle Zhao, Zhixiong Zeng, Jing Huang, Liming Zheng, Yufeng Zhong, Lin Ma
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-08-19T07:40:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T04:37:34+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While reinforcement learning (RL) has proven highly effective for general reasoning in vision-language models, its application to tasks requiring deep understanding of information-rich images and structured output generation remains underexplored. Chart-to-code generation exemplifies this challenge, demanding complex reasoning over visual charts to produce structured code. Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) alone is often insufficient, highlighting the need for effective RL strategies tailored to structured outputs. In this paper, we systematically investigate the performance plateau of SFT through large-scale experiments and propose Multimodal Structured Reinforcement Learning (MSRL) for chart-to-code generation. We construct the largest training corpus to date, with 3 million chart-code pairs curated from real-world tables in arXiv papers, addressing the limitations of previous synthetic datasets. Despite achieving state-of-the-art performance, our experiments show that simply increasing SFT data eventually leads to diminishing improvements. To break this plateau, MSRL employs a multi-granularity reward system that integrates both textual and visual feedback. At the textual level, rule-based rewards validate fine-grained code details, while at the visual level, a model-based reward assesses the structural similarity between rendered code and ground-truth charts. We implement a two-stage curriculum training strategy, first optimizing the model with textual rewards and then incorporating visual signals for further enhancement. Experimental results demonstrate that MSRL substantially breaks the SFT plateau, improving high-level metrics by 6.2% and 9.9% on ChartMimic and ReachQA benchmarks, respectively. Notably, our method outperforms all existing approaches in the chart domain and achieves competitive results with advanced closed-source models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破SFT瓶颈：面向图表转代码生成的多模态结构化强化学习
尽管强化学习在视觉语言模型的通用推理任务中成效显著，但其在需要深度理解信息密集型图像并生成结构化输出的任务中仍待深入探索。图表转代码生成正是此类挑战的典型代表，它要求对视觉图表进行复杂推理以生成结构化代码。仅依赖监督微调往往不足，凸显了需要针对结构化输出定制有效强化学习策略的必要性。本文通过大规模实验系统性地研究了SFT的性能瓶颈，并提出用于图表转代码生成的多模态结构化强化学习框架。我们构建了迄今最大的训练语料库，包含从arXiv论文真实表格中整理的300万图表-代码对，解决了先前合成数据集的局限性。尽管取得了最先进的性能，实验表明单纯增加SFT数据最终会导致改进收益递减。为突破此瓶颈，MSRL采用多粒度奖励系统，整合文本与视觉反馈：文本层面通过基于规则的奖励验证细粒度代码细节，视觉层面则通过基于模型的奖励评估渲染代码与真实图表间的结构相似性。我们实施两阶段课程训练策略，先以文本奖励优化模型，再融入视觉信号进行增强。实验结果表明，MSRL显著突破了SFT瓶颈，在ChartMimic和ReachQA基准上分别将高级指标提升6.2%和9.9%。值得注意的是，本方法在图表领域超越所有现有方案，并与先进闭源模型取得可比结果。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the performance plateau of supervised fine-tuning (SFT) in chart-to-code generation, a task requiring complex reasoning from information-rich images to produce structured code. The authors propose Multimodal Structured Reinforcement Learning (MSRL), which utilizes a multi-granularity reward system combining rule-based textual feedback for code details and a model-based visual reward for structural similarity between rendered and ground-truth charts, trained via a two-stage curriculum. Experiments on a large-scale corpus of 3 million real-world chart-code pairs show MSRL breaks the SFT plateau, improving high-level metrics by 6.2% on ChartMimic and 9.9% on ReachQA, outperforming existing chart-domain methods and achieving competitive results with advanced closed-source models.
本文针对监督微调在图表到代码生成任务中出现的性能瓶颈问题展开研究，该任务需要从信息丰富的图像中进行复杂推理以生成结构化代码。作者提出了多模态结构化强化学习方法，采用多粒度奖励系统，结合了基于规则的文本反馈来验证代码细节，以及基于模型的视觉奖励来评估生成代码与真实图表之间的结构相似性，并通过两阶段课程策略进行训练。基于构建的300万真实世界图表-代码对的大规模语料实验表明，该方法显著突破了监督微调的性能平台，在ChartMimic和ReachQA基准上分别将高级指标提升了6.2%和9.9%，超越了现有图表领域方法，并与先进的闭源模型取得了竞争性结果。
LLM-Driven Instance-Specific Heuristic Generation and Selection
Authors: Shaofeng Zhang, Shengcai Liu, Ning Lu, Jiahao Wu, Ji Liu, Yew-Soon Ong, Ke Tang
First: 2025-05-31T09:54:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T04:10:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Combinatorial optimization problems are widely encountered in real-world applications. A critical research challenge lies in designing high-quality heuristic algorithms that efficiently approximate optimal solutions within a reasonable time. In recent years, many works have explored integrating Large Language Models (LLMs) with Evolutionary Algorithms to automate heuristic algorithm design through prompt engineering. However, these approaches generally adopt a problem-specific paradigm, applying a single algorithm across all problem instances, failing to account for the heterogeneity across instances. In this paper, we propose InstSpecHH, a novel framework that introduces the concept of instance-specific heuristic generation. InstSpecHH partitions the overall problem class into sub-classes based on instance features and performs differentiated, automated heuristic design for each problem subclass. By tailoring heuristics to the unique features of different sub-classes, InstSpecHH achieves better performance at the problem class level while avoiding redundant heuristic generation for similar instances, thus reducing computational overhead. This approach effectively balances the trade-off between the cost of automatic heuristic design and the quality of the obtained solutions. To evaluate the performance of InstSpecHH, we conduct comprehensive experiments on 4,500 subclasses of the Online Bin Packing Problem (OBPP) and 365 subclasses of the Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem (CVRP). Experimental results show that InstSpecHH demonstrates strong intra-subclass and inter-subclass generalization capabilities. Compared to previous problem-specific methods, InstSpecHH reduces the average optimality gap by 6.06\% for OBPP and 0.66\% for CVRP. These results highlight the potential of instance-aware automatic heuristic design to further enhance solution quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型的实例特定启发式生成与选择
组合优化问题在现实应用中广泛存在。核心研究挑战在于设计高质量的启发式算法，以在合理时间内高效逼近最优解。近年来，许多研究探索通过提示工程将大语言模型与进化算法相结合，实现启发式算法的自动化设计。然而，这些方法通常采用问题特定范式，对所有问题实例应用单一算法，未能考虑实例间的异质性。本文提出InstSpecHH框架，引入实例特定启发式生成的概念。该框架基于实例特征将整体问题类别划分为子类，并对每个问题子类进行差异化的自动化启发式设计。通过为不同子类的独特特征定制启发式，InstSpecHH在问题类别层面实现了更优性能，同时避免对相似实例的冗余启发式生成，从而降低计算开销。该方法有效平衡了自动启发式设计成本与所得解质量之间的权衡。为评估InstSpecHH性能，我们在在线装箱问题的4500个子类和容量约束车辆路径问题的365个子类上进行了全面实验。结果表明，InstSpecHH展现出强大的子类内与子类间泛化能力。与先前问题特定方法相比，InstSpecHH将在线装箱问题的平均最优间隙降低了6.06%，容量约束车辆路径问题降低了0.66%。这些结果凸显了实例感知的自动启发式设计在进一步提升解质量方面的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitation of existing LLM-driven heuristic design methods, which apply a single algorithm to all instances of a combinatorial optimization problem, ignoring instance heterogeneity. The proposed method, InstSpecHH, introduces an instance-specific heuristic generation framework that partitions a problem class into sub-classes based on instance features and performs automated, differentiated heuristic design for each subclass, balancing design cost and solution quality. Experimental results on the Online Bin Packing Problem and Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem, involving thousands of subclasses, show that InstSpecHH achieves strong generalization and reduces the average optimality gap by 6.06% and 0.66% respectively compared to prior problem-specific approaches.
本研究的动机是解决现有基于大语言模型的启发式设计方法的局限性，这些方法对组合优化问题的所有实例采用单一算法，忽略了实例间的异质性。所提出的方法InstSpecHH引入了一个实例特定的启发式生成框架，该框架根据实例特征将问题类别划分为子类，并为每个子类执行自动化、差异化的启发式设计，从而平衡设计成本与求解质量。在在线装箱问题和带容量车辆路径问题上的实验结果表明，该方法在数千个子类上表现出强大的泛化能力，与先前的问题特定方法相比，平均最优性差距分别降低了6.06%和0.66%。
Bayesian Optimization with Gaussian Processes to Accelerate Stationary Point Searches
Authors: Rohit Goswami
First: 2026-03-11T17:20:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T04:02:24+00:00
Comments: 60 pages, 24 figures. Invited article for ACS Physical Chemistry Au
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accelerating the explorations of stationary points on potential energy surfaces building local surrogates spans decades of effort. Done correctly, surrogates reduce required evaluations by an order of magnitude while preserving the accuracy of the underlying theory. We present a unified Bayesian Optimization view of minimization, single point saddle searches, and double ended saddle searches through a unified six-step surrogate loop, differing only in the inner optimization target and acquisition criterion. The framework uses Gaussian process regression with derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning. The Optimal Transport GP extensions of farthest point sampling with Earth mover's distance, MAP regularization via variance barrier and oscillation detection, and adaptive trust radius form concrete extensions of the same basic methodology, improving accuracy and efficiency. We also demonstrate random Fourier features decouple hyperparameter training from predictions enabling favorable scaling for high-dimensional systems. Accompanying pedagogical Rust code demonstrates that all applications use the exact same Bayesian optimization loop, bridging the gap between theoretical formulation and practical execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯过程的贝叶斯优化加速势能面驻点搜索
通过构建局部代理模型加速势能面驻点探索已历经数十年研究。正确实施的代理模型能在保持基础理论精度的前提下，将所需计算量降低一个数量级。本文提出统一的贝叶斯优化框架，通过六步代理循环统一处理极小值点搜索、单点鞍点搜索和双端鞍点搜索，仅在内层优化目标和采集准则上存在差异。该框架采用含导数观测的高斯过程回归、反距离核函数及主动学习策略。通过最远点采样与推土机距离的最优传输GP扩展、基于方差屏障与振荡检测的MAP正则化、自适应信任半径等具体方法延伸了基础框架，提升了精度与效率。随机傅里叶特征的应用实现超参数训练与预测解耦，为高维系统提供优越的扩展性。配套的Rust教学代码表明所有应用均采用完全相同的贝叶斯优化循环，弥合了理论构建与实际执行间的鸿沟。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the long-standing challenge of efficiently exploring stationary points on potential energy surfaces, this paper presents a unified Bayesian Optimization framework using Gaussian processes to accelerate such searches. The method employs a six-step surrogate loop with Gaussian process regression incorporating derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning, extended with techniques like Optimal Transport GP for sampling and random Fourier features for scalable hyperparameter training. Key experimental results demonstrate that the framework reduces required evaluations by an order of magnitude while maintaining accuracy, effectively unifying minimization and saddle point searches, and its practical implementation is showcased through accompanying pedagogical code.
本文旨在解决势能面上驻点搜索效率低下的长期挑战，提出了一个基于高斯过程的统一贝叶斯优化框架来加速此类搜索。该方法采用一个六步代理循环，结合了具有导数观测的高斯过程回归、反距离核与主动学习，并通过最优传输高斯过程进行采样扩展以及随机傅里叶特征实现可扩展的超参数训练。主要实验结果表明，该框架在保持精度的同时将所需评估次数减少了一个数量级，有效统一了极小值和鞍点搜索，并通过配套的教学代码展示了其实际应用。
CRAFT: Calibrated Reasoning with Answer-Faithful Traces via Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Hop Question Answering
Authors: Yu Liu, Wenxiao Zhang, Diandian Guo, Cong Cao, Fangfang Yuan, Qiang Sun, Yanbing Liu, Jin B. Hong, Zhiyuan Ma
First: 2026-02-01T17:33:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T03:48:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrieval-augmented large language models, when optimized with outcome-level rewards, can achieve strong answer accuracy on multi-hop questions. However, under noisy retrieval, models frequently suffer from "right-answer-wrong-reason failures": they may exploit spurious shortcuts or produce reasoning traces weakly grounded in the supporting evidence. Furthermore, the lack of structured output control prevents reliable auditing of the underlying reasoning quality. To address this, we propose CRAFT (Calibrated Reasoning with Answer-Faithful Traces), a reinforcement learning framework for the response generation stage of retrieval-augmented multi-hop question answering. CRAFT trains models to produce structured reasoning traces with configurable levels of auditability (e.g., by selectively retaining planning, evidence citation, or reasoning steps). Training combines two complementary forms of supervision: deterministic rewards enforce verifiable constraints, including format compliance, answer correctness, and citation-set validity, while a judge-based reward audits semantic faithfulness by evaluating reasoning consistency and evidence grounding. Experiments show that CRAFT improves both answer accuracy and reasoning faithfulness across model scales. Notably, semantic judge-based rewards improve answer accuracy rather than compromise it, enabling CRAFT (7B) to achieve performance competitive with strong closed-source models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CRAFT：基于强化学习的答案忠实轨迹校准推理用于多跳问答
检索增强的大型语言模型在通过结果级奖励优化后，能在多跳问题上实现较高的答案准确率。然而，在噪声检索条件下，模型常出现“答案正确但推理错误”的故障：它们可能利用虚假捷径或生成与支持证据关联薄弱的推理轨迹。此外，缺乏结构化输出控制阻碍了对底层推理质量的可靠审计。为此，我们提出CRAFT（基于答案忠实轨迹的校准推理），这是一个针对检索增强多跳问答响应生成阶段的强化学习框架。CRAFT训练模型生成具有可配置审计级别的结构化推理轨迹（例如选择性保留规划、证据引用或推理步骤）。训练结合两种互补的监督形式：确定性奖励强制执行可验证约束，包括格式合规性、答案正确性和引用集有效性；而基于评判器的奖励通过评估推理一致性和证据锚定性来审计语义忠实度。实验表明，CRAFT在不同规模模型上均提升了答案准确率和推理忠实度。值得注意的是，基于语义评判器的奖励不仅未损害答案准确率，反而提升了该指标，使CRAFT（7B参数）达到了与强闭源模型相竞争的性能水平。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue in retrieval-augmented large language models where, under noisy retrieval, models often produce correct answers but with flawed reasoning traces that exploit shortcuts or lack grounding in evidence, and it also highlights the lack of structured output for auditing reasoning quality. To solve this, the authors propose CRAFT, a reinforcement learning framework that trains models to generate structured reasoning traces with configurable auditability by combining deterministic rewards for format compliance, answer correctness, and citation validity with judge-based rewards for semantic faithfulness in reasoning consistency and evidence grounding. Experimental results demonstrate that CRAFT enhances both answer accuracy and reasoning faithfulness across different model scales, with semantic judge-based rewards boosting accuracy rather than compromising it, allowing a 7B model to achieve performance competitive with strong closed-source models.
该论文针对检索增强大语言模型在噪声检索下常出现“答案正确但推理错误”的问题，即模型可能利用虚假捷径或产生与证据脱节的推理轨迹，同时缺乏结构化输出来审计推理质量。为解决此问题，作者提出了CRAFT框架，通过强化学习训练模型生成可配置审计级别的结构化推理轨迹，结合确定性奖励（用于格式合规性、答案正确性和引用有效性）与基于评判者的奖励（用于评估推理一致性和证据接地的语义忠实度）。实验结果表明，CRAFT在不同规模模型上均提升了答案准确性和推理忠实度，其中语义评判者奖励不仅未损害准确性反而提高了它，使一个7B模型实现了与强闭源模型竞争的性能。
DeFRiS: Silo-Cooperative IoT Applications Scheduling via Decentralized Federated Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhiyu Wang, Mohammad Goudarzi, Mingming Gong, Rajkumar Buyya
First: 2026-03-16T02:02:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T02:02:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Next-generation IoT applications increasingly span across autonomous administrative entities, necessitating silo-cooperative scheduling to leverage diverse computational resources while preserving data privacy. However, realizing efficient cooperation faces significant challenges arising from infrastructure heterogeneity, Non-IID workload shifts, and the inherent risks of adversarial environments. Existing approaches, relying predominantly on centralized coordination or independent learning, fail to address the incompatibility of state-action spaces across heterogeneous silos and lack robustness against malicious attacks. This paper proposes DeFRiS, a Decentralized Federated Reinforcement Learning framework for robust and scalable Silo-cooperative IoT application scheduling. DeFRiS integrates three synergistic innovations: (i) an action-space-agnostic policy utilizing candidate resource scoring to enable seamless knowledge transfer across heterogeneous silos; (ii) a silo-optimized local learning mechanism combining Generalized Advantage Estimation (GAE) with clipped policy updates to resolve sparse delayed reward challenges; and (iii) a Dual-Track Non-IID robust decentralized aggregation protocol leveraging gradient fingerprints for similarity-aware knowledge transfer and anomaly detection, and gradient tracking for optimization momentum. Extensive experiments on a distributed testbed with 20 heterogeneous silos and realistic IoT workloads demonstrate that DeFRiS significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing average response time by 6.4% and energy consumption by 7.2%, while lowering tail latency risk (CVaR$_{0.95}$) by 10.4% and achieving near-zero deadline violations. Furthermore, DeFRiS achieves over 3 times better performance retention as the system scales and over 8 times better stability in adversarial environments compared to the best-performing baseline.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeFRiS：基于去中心化联邦强化学习的孤岛协同物联网应用调度
下一代物联网应用日益跨越自治管理实体，需通过孤岛协同调度以整合异构计算资源并保障数据隐私。然而，基础设施异构性、非独立同分布负载偏移及对抗性环境风险，为高效协同带来严峻挑战。现有方法主要依赖中心化协调或独立学习，难以解决异构孤岛间状态-动作空间不兼容问题，且缺乏对抗恶意攻击的鲁棒性。本文提出DeFRiS——一种基于去中心化联邦强化学习的鲁棒可扩展孤岛协同物联网应用调度框架。该框架融合三项协同创新：（1）采用候选资源评分的动作空间无关策略，实现跨异构孤岛的无缝知识迁移；（2）结合广义优势估计与截断策略更新的孤岛优化本地学习机制，解决稀疏延迟奖励难题；（3）基于梯度指纹的双轨非独立同分布鲁棒去中心化聚合协议，通过相似性感知知识迁移与异常检测实现梯度追踪优化动量。在含20个异构孤岛的分布式测试平台上，基于真实物联网负载的广泛实验表明：DeFRiS显著优于现有基线方法，平均响应时间降低6.4%，能耗减少7.2%，尾部延迟风险（CVaR$_{0.95}$）下降10.4%，截止时间违规率趋近于零。此外，在系统扩展时DeFRiS性能保持能力超最优基线3倍以上，在对抗环境中稳定性提升超8倍。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for privacy-preserving and efficient scheduling of IoT applications across autonomous administrative silos with heterogeneous resources and non-IID workloads, this paper proposes DeFRiS, a decentralized federated reinforcement learning framework. The method introduces an action-space-agnostic policy for cross-silo knowledge transfer, a local learning mechanism with Generalized Advantage Estimation to handle sparse rewards, and a dual-track robust aggregation protocol for non-IID resilience and security. Experimental results on a 20-silo testbed show DeFRiS reduces average response time by 6.4% and energy consumption by 7.2%, significantly lowers tail latency risk and deadline violations, and demonstrates superior scalability and adversarial robustness compared to baselines.
本文针对跨自治管理域、资源异构且工作负载非独立同分布的物联网应用调度需求，旨在实现隐私保护下的高效协同，提出了DeFRiS这一去中心化联邦强化学习框架。该方法融合了三项创新：采用与动作空间无关的策略实现跨异构孤岛的知识迁移，结合广义优势估计的本地学习机制应对稀疏奖励，以及利用梯度指纹和跟踪的双轨聚合协议保证非独立同分布环境下的鲁棒性。在包含20个异构孤岛的分布式测试平台上的实验表明，DeFRiS显著优于现有基线，平均响应时间降低6.4%，能耗降低7.2%，尾部延迟风险和截止时间违规大幅减少，并在系统扩展性和对抗环境稳定性方面表现卓越。
Deterministic Policy Gradient for Reinforcement Learning with Continuous Time and State
Authors: Ziheng Cheng, Xin Guo, Yufei Zhang
First: 2025-09-28T07:53:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T00:09:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The theory of continuous-time reinforcement learning (RL) has progressed rapidly in recent years. While the ultimate objective of RL is typically to learn deterministic control policies, most existing continuous-time RL methods rely on stochastic policies. Such approaches often require sampling actions at very high frequencies, and involve computationally expensive expectations over continuous action spaces, resulting in high-variance gradient estimates and slow convergence. In this paper, we introduce and develop deterministic policy gradient (DPG) methods for continuous-time RL. We derive a continuous-time policy gradient formula expressed as the expected gradient of an advantage rate function and establish a martingale characterization for both the value function and the advantage rate. These theoretical results provide tractable estimators for deterministic policy gradients in continuous-time RL. Building on this foundation, we propose a model-free continuous-time Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (CT-DDPG) algorithm that enables stable learning for general reinforcement learning problems with continuous time-and-state. Numerical experiments show that CT-DDPG achieves superior stability and faster convergence compared to existing stochastic-policy methods, across a wide range of learning tasks with varying time discretizations and noise levels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续时间与状态强化学习的确定性策略梯度方法
近年来，连续时间强化学习理论发展迅速。尽管强化学习的最终目标通常是学习确定性控制策略，但现有连续时间强化学习方法大多依赖随机策略。这类方法通常需要以极高频率采样动作，并涉及对连续动作空间进行计算代价高昂的期望运算，导致梯度估计方差大、收敛速度慢。本文针对连续时间强化学习提出并发展了确定性策略梯度方法。我们推导出以优势率函数梯度期望形式表达的连续时间策略梯度公式，并为值函数与优势率建立了鞅表征。这些理论结果为连续时间强化学习中的确定性策略梯度提供了可处理的估计量。在此基础上，我们提出一种无模型的连续时间深度确定性策略梯度算法，该算法能够为具有连续时间与状态的通用强化学习问题实现稳定学习。数值实验表明，在多种时间离散化程度和噪声水平的学习任务中，该算法相比现有随机策略方法具有更优的稳定性和更快的收敛速度。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational inefficiency and high variance of stochastic policies in continuous-time reinforcement learning, which require frequent action sampling and expensive expectations, this paper introduces deterministic policy gradient methods for continuous-time RL. The method derives a policy gradient formula as the expected gradient of an advantage rate function, establishes martingale characterizations for value and advantage, and proposes a model-free CT-DDPG algorithm. Experimental results demonstrate that CT-DDPG achieves superior stability and faster convergence compared to stochastic-policy methods across various tasks with different time discretizations and noise levels.
针对连续时间强化学习中随机策略计算效率低、方差高的问题，该方法引入了确定性策略梯度方法。通过推导优势率函数的期望梯度作为策略梯度公式，建立价值和优势的鞅表征，并提出了无模型的CT-DDPG算法。实验结果表明，在不同时间离散化和噪声水平的学习任务中，CT-DDPG相比随机策略方法具有更优的稳定性和更快的收敛速度。
MapReduce LoRA: Advancing the Pareto Front in Multi-Preference Optimization for Generative Models
Authors: Chieh-Yun Chen, Zhonghao Wang, Qi Chen, Zhifan Ye, Min Shi, Yue Zhao, Yinan Zhao, Hui Qu, Wei-An Lin, Yiru Shen, Ajinkya Kale, Irfan Essa, Humphrey Shi
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-11-25T18:49:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T23:35:20+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026; Code: https://github.com/SHI-Labs/MapReduce-LoRA
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) with reward models has advanced alignment of generative models to human aesthetic and perceptual preferences. However, jointly optimizing multiple rewards often incurs an alignment tax, improving one dimension while degrading others. To address this, we introduce two complementary methods: MapReduce LoRA and Reward-aware Token Embedding (RaTE). MapReduce LoRA trains preference-specific LoRA experts in parallel and iteratively merges them to refine a shared base model; RaTE learns reward-specific token embeddings that compose at inference for flexible preference control. Experiments on Text-to-Image generation (Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium and FLUX.1-dev) show improvements of 36.1%, 4.6%, and 55.7%, and 32.7%, 4.3%, and 67.1% on GenEval, PickScore, and OCR, respectively. On Text-to-Video generation (HunyuanVideo), visual and motion quality improve by 48.1% and 90.0%, respectively. On the language task, Helpful Assistant, with Llama-2 7B, helpful and harmless improve by 43.4% and 136.7%, respectively. Our framework sets a new state-of-the-art multi-preference alignment recipe across modalities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MapReduce LoRA：推进生成模型多偏好优化的帕累托前沿
基于奖励模型的人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）提升了生成模型与人类审美及感知偏好的对齐能力。然而，联合优化多个奖励常引发对齐代价，即提升某一维度时损害其他维度。为此，我们提出两种互补方法：MapReduce LoRA 与奖励感知词元嵌入（RaTE）。MapReduce LoRA 并行训练针对特定偏好的LoRA专家模型，并通过迭代融合优化共享基础模型；RaTE 学习奖励特定的词元嵌入，在推理时组合以实现灵活偏好控制。在文生图任务（Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium 与 FLUX.1-dev）中，GenEval、PickScore 与 OCR 指标分别提升36.1%、4.6%、55.7% 和 32.7%、4.3%、67.1%；在文生视频任务（HunyuanVideo）中，视觉与运动质量分别提升48.1% 与90.0%；在语言任务（Helpful Assistant，基于Llama-2 7B）中，帮助性与无害性分别提升43.4% 与136.7%。本框架为跨模态多偏好对齐确立了新的最优方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the alignment tax in multi-preference optimization for generative models, where improving one preference often degrades others. The authors propose two methods: MapReduce LoRA, which trains and merges preference-specific LoRA experts in parallel to refine a base model, and Reward-aware Token Embedding (RaTE), which learns reward-specific embeddings for flexible inference-time control. Experimental results across text-to-image, text-to-video, and language tasks demonstrate significant improvements, such as gains of up to 67.1% on image metrics and 136.7% on language safety, establishing a new state-of-the-art in multi-preference alignment.
本文针对生成模型多偏好优化中的对齐税问题，即提升某一偏好常导致其他偏好退化，提出了两种方法：MapReduce LoRA并行训练并迭代合并偏好特定的LoRA专家以优化基础模型，以及奖励感知词嵌入（RaTE）学习奖励特定的词嵌入以实现灵活的推理时控制。在文本到图像、文本到视频和语言任务上的实验结果显示显著提升，如图像指标最高提升67.1%，语言安全性提升136.7%，从而在多模态多偏好对齐方面确立了新的先进方案。
VisionCoach: Reinforcing Grounded Video Reasoning via Visual-Perception Prompting
Authors: Daeun Lee, Shoubin Yu, Yue Zhang, Mohit Bansal
First: 2026-03-15T23:32:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T23:32:02+00:00
Comments: Project website: https://visioncoach.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Video reasoning requires models to locate and track question-relevant evidence across frames. While reinforcement learning (RL) with verifiable rewards improves accuracy, it still struggles to achieve reliable spatio-temporal grounding during the reasoning process. Moreover, improving grounding typically relies on scaled training data or inference-time perception tools, which increases annotation cost or computational cost. To address this challenge, we propose VisonCoach, an input-adaptive RL framework that improves spatio-temporal grounding through visual prompting as training-time guidance. During RL training, visual prompts are selectively applied to challenging inputs to amplify question-relevant evidence and suppress distractors. The model then internalizes these improvements through self-distillation, enabling grounded reasoning directly on raw videos without visual prompting at inference. VisonCoach consists of two components: (1) Visual Prompt Selector, which predicts appropriate prompt types conditioned on the video and question, and (2) Spatio-Temporal Reasoner, optimized with RL under visual prompt guidance and object-aware grounding rewards that enforce object identity consistency and multi-region bounding-box overlap. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VisonCoach achieves state-of-the-art performance under comparable settings, across diverse video reasoning, video understanding, and temporal grounding benchmarks (V-STAR, VideoMME, World-Sense, VideoMMMU, PerceptionTest, and Charades-STA), while maintaining a single efficient inference pathway without external tools. Our results show that visual prompting during training improves grounded video reasoning, while self-distillation enables the model to internalize this ability without requiring prompts at inference time.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VisionCoach：通过视觉感知提示强化视频推理的时空定位能力
视频推理要求模型在连续帧中定位并追踪与问题相关的证据。尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RL）提升了准确性，但在推理过程中仍难以实现可靠的时空定位。此外，改进定位能力通常依赖大规模训练数据或推理时的感知工具，这会增加标注成本或计算开销。为解决这一挑战，我们提出VisionCoach——一种输入自适应的强化学习框架，通过视觉提示作为训练时指导来提升时空定位能力。在强化学习训练过程中，视觉提示被选择性地应用于具有挑战性的输入，以增强问题相关证据并抑制干扰信息。模型随后通过自蒸馏将这些改进内化，从而在推理时无需视觉提示即可直接对原始视频进行定位推理。VisionCoach包含两个核心组件：（1）视觉提示选择器：根据视频和问题预测适用的提示类型；（2）时空推理器：在视觉提示引导及对象感知定位奖励（强化对象身份一致性与多区域边界框重叠）下通过强化学习优化。大量实验表明，在可比较的设置下，VisionCoach在多样化视频推理、视频理解和时序定位基准（V-STAR、VideoMME、World-Sense、VideoMMMU、PerceptionTest和Charades-STA）上均达到最先进性能，同时保持单一高效推理路径且无需外部工具。我们的结果表明，训练时的视觉提示能有效提升视频定位推理能力，而自蒸馏技术使模型无需推理时提示即可内化这种能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of achieving reliable spatio-temporal grounding in video reasoning tasks, where existing reinforcement learning methods often struggle without costly data scaling or inference-time perception tools. The authors propose VisionCoach, an input-adaptive RL framework that uses visual-perception prompting during training to selectively amplify question-relevant evidence and suppress distractors in challenging inputs, followed by self-distillation to internalize these improvements. Experimental results show state-of-the-art performance across multiple video reasoning benchmarks, including V-STAR and VideoMME, while maintaining efficient inference without external tools.
该论文针对视频推理任务中时空定位不可靠的挑战，现有强化学习方法常依赖昂贵的数据扩展或推理时感知工具。作者提出VisionCoach框架，在训练时通过视觉提示自适应地增强问题相关证据并抑制干扰，再通过自蒸馏内化这些改进。实验结果表明，在V-STAR、VideoMME等多个视频推理基准上取得了先进性能，同时无需外部工具即可实现高效推理。
ELASTIC: Efficient Once For All Iterative Search for Object Detection on Microcontrollers
Authors: Tony Tran, Qin Lin, Bin Hu
First: 2025-03-27T21:35:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T22:48:14+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Deploying high-performance object detectors on TinyML platforms poses significant challenges due to tight hardware constraints and the modular complexity of modern detection pipelines. Neural Architecture Search (NAS) offers a path toward automation, but existing methods either restrict optimization to individual modules, sacrificing cross-module synergy, or require global searches that are computationally intractable. We propose ELASTIC (Efficient Once for AlL IterAtive Search for ObjecT DetectIon on MiCrocontrollers), a unified, hardware-aware NAS framework that alternates optimization across modules (e.g., backbone, neck, and head) in a cyclic fashion. ELASTIC introduces a novel Population Passthrough mechanism in evolutionary search that retains high-quality candidates between search stages, yielding faster convergence, up to an 8% final mAP gain, and eliminates search instability observed without population passthrough. In a controlled comparison, empirical results show ELASTIC achieves +4.75% higher mAP and 2x faster convergence than progressive NAS strategies on SVHN, and delivers a +9.09% mAP improvement on PascalVOC given the same search budget. ELASTIC achieves 72.3% mAP on PascalVOC, outperforming MCUNET by 20.9% and TinyissimoYOLO by 16.3%. When deployed on MAX78000/MAX78002 microcontrollers, ELASTICderived models outperform Analog Devices' TinySSD baselines, reducing energy by up to 71.6%, lowering latency by up to 2.4x, and improving mAP by up to 6.99 percentage points across multiple datasets. The experimental videos and codes are available on the project website (https://nail-uh.github.io/elastic.github.io/).
中文标题/摘要
标题：ELASTIC：面向微控制器对象检测的高效一次性全模块迭代搜索框架
在TinyML平台上部署高性能对象检测器面临硬件资源严格受限与现代检测流程模块化复杂性的双重挑战。神经架构搜索（NAS）为实现自动化提供了路径，但现有方法要么将优化局限于单个模块（牺牲跨模块协同），要么依赖计算上不可行的全局搜索。本文提出ELASTIC（面向微控制器对象检测的高效一次性全模块迭代搜索框架），这是一种统一的硬件感知NAS框架，通过循环交替方式优化各模块（如骨干网络、颈部网络和检测头）。ELASTIC在进化搜索中引入创新的种群传递机制，在搜索阶段间保留高质量候选架构，从而加速收敛（最终mAP提升最高达8%），并消除了无种群传递时出现的搜索不稳定性。在对照实验中，ELASTIC在SVHN数据集上比渐进式NAS策略的mAP提高4.75%、收敛速度快2倍；在相同搜索预算下，对PascalVOC数据集的mAP提升达9.09%。ELASTIC在PascalVOC上达到72.3% mAP，分别超越MCUNET 20.9%和TinyissimoYOLO 16.3%。在MAX78000/MAX78002微控制器部署时，ELASTIC衍生模型全面优于Analog Devices的TinySSD基线：在多个数据集上能耗降低最高达71.6%，延迟减少最高达2.4倍，mAP提升最高达6.99个百分点。实验视频与代码已发布于项目网站（https://nail-uh.github.io/elastic.github.io/）。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the difficulty of deploying high-performance object detectors on microcontrollers due to hardware constraints and the modular complexity of detection pipelines, where existing Neural Architecture Search (NAS) methods either optimize modules in isolation or require prohibitively expensive global searches. To address this, the authors propose ELASTIC, a unified hardware-aware NAS framework that cyclically alternates optimization across modules like the backbone, neck, and head, incorporating a novel Population Passthrough mechanism in evolutionary search to retain high-quality candidates between stages for faster convergence and improved stability. Experimental results demonstrate that ELASTIC achieves significant gains: it outperforms progressive NAS strategies with a 4.75% higher mAP and 2x faster convergence on SVHN, attains a 9.09% mAP improvement on PascalVOC within the same search budget, and reaches 72.3% mAP on PascalVOC, surpassing MCUNET by 20.9% and TinyissimoYOLO by 16.3%; when deployed on MAX78000/MAX78002 microcontrollers, ELASTIC-derived models reduce energy by up to 71.6%, lower latency by up to 2.4x, and improve mAP by up to 6.99 percentage points compared to baselines.
本文的动机在于，由于硬件限制和目标检测流程的模块化复杂性，在微控制器上部署高性能目标检测器面临挑战，而现有的神经架构搜索方法要么孤立地优化模块，要么需要计算成本高昂的全局搜索。为此，作者提出了ELASTIC，这是一个统一的硬件感知神经架构搜索框架，它以循环方式交替优化骨干网络、颈部网络和头部等模块，并在进化搜索中引入了一种新颖的种群传递机制，以在搜索阶段之间保留高质量候选方案，从而实现更快的收敛和更高的稳定性。实验结果表明，ELASTIC取得了显著提升：在SVHN数据集上，相比渐进式神经架构搜索策略，其mAP提高了4.75%，收敛速度加快2倍；在相同搜索预算下，PascalVOC数据集的mAP提升了9.09%，并达到72.3%的mAP，分别超过MCUNET 20.9%和TinyissimoYOLO 16.3%；在MAX78000/MAX78002微控制器上部署时，ELASTIC衍生的模型相比基线最高可降低71.6%的能耗、减少2.4倍的延迟，并在多个数据集上将mAP提升高达6.99个百分点。
EcoFair-CH-MARL: Scalable Constrained Hierarchical Multi-Agent RL with Real-Time Emission Budgets and Fairness Guarantees
Authors: Saad Alqithami
Venue: Frontiers in Artificial Intelligence and Applications, 2025
First: 2026-03-15T21:40:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T21:40:40+00:00
Comments: Conference: The 28th European Conference on Artificial Intelligence (ECAI)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Global decarbonisation targets and tightening market pressures demand maritime logistics solutions that are simultaneously efficient, sustainable, and equitable. We introduce EcoFair-CH-MARL, a constrained hierarchical multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that unifies three innovations: (i) a primal-dual budget layer that provably bounds cumulative emissions under stochastic weather and demand; (ii) a fairness-aware reward transformer with dynamically scheduled penalties that enforces max-min cost equity across heterogeneous fleets; and (iii) a two-tier policy architecture that decouples strategic routing from real-time vessel control, enabling linear scaling in agent count. New theoretical results establish O(\sqrt{T}) regret for both constraint violations and fairness loss. Experiments on a high-fidelity maritime digital twin (16 ports, 50 vessels) driven by automatic identification system traces, plus an energy-grid case study, show up to 15% lower emissions, 12% higher through-put, and a 45% fair-cost improvement over state-of-the-art hierarchical and constrained MARL baselines. In addition, EcoFair-CH-MARL achieves stronger equity (lower Gini and higher min-max welfare) than fairness-specific MARL baselines (e.g., SOTO, FEN), and its modular design is compatible with both policy- and value-based learners. EcoFair-CH-MARL therefore advances the feasibility of large-scale, regulation-compliant, and socially responsible multi-agent coordination in safety-critical domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EcoFair-CH-MARL：具有实时排放预算与公平性保障的可扩展约束分层多智能体强化学习
全球脱碳目标与日益严峻的市场压力要求海运物流方案同时具备高效性、可持续性与公平性。本文提出EcoFair-CH-MARL——一种约束分层多智能体强化学习框架，融合三大创新：(i) 原对偶预算层，可在随机天气与需求下可证明地约束累积排放；(ii) 具备动态调度惩罚机制的公平感知奖励转换器，确保异构船队间的最大最小成本公平；(iii) 双层策略架构，将战略路径规划与实时船舶控制解耦，实现智能体数量的线性扩展。新理论结果证明约束违反与公平性损失的遗憾上界均为O(√T)。基于自动识别系统轨迹的高保真海运数字孪生实验（16个港口、50艘船舶）及能源电网案例研究表明：相较于最先进的分层与约束MARL基线，本框架降低排放达15%，提升吞吐量12%，公平成本改善45%。此外，EcoFair-CH-MARL较专用公平性MARL基线（如SOTO、FEN）具有更强公平性（更低基尼系数与更高最小最大福利），其模块化设计兼容策略基与价值基学习器。因此，本框架推动了安全关键领域大规模、合规且社会责任导向的多智能体协调的可行性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for maritime logistics solutions that balance efficiency, sustainability, and equity under global decarbonization pressures, this paper introduces EcoFair-CH-MARL, a constrained hierarchical multi-agent reinforcement learning framework. The method integrates a primal-dual budget layer to bound cumulative emissions, a fairness-aware reward transformer for cost equity across fleets, and a two-tier policy architecture that decouples strategic routing from real-time control for scalability. Experimental results on a high-fidelity maritime digital twin and an energy-grid case study demonstrate up to 15% lower emissions, 12% higher throughput, and a 45% improvement in fair-cost compared to state-of-the-art baselines, alongside stronger equity metrics and theoretical guarantees on constraint and fairness regret.
为应对全球脱碳目标和市场压力，寻求同时兼顾效率、可持续性与公平性的海事物流解决方案，本文提出了EcoFair-CH-MARL，一个约束分层多智能体强化学习框架。该方法融合了三个创新：一个原始-对偶预算层以约束累积排放，一个具有动态惩罚的公平感知奖励转换器以确保异构船队间的成本公平，以及一个将战略路由与实时控制解耦的双层策略架构以实现可扩展性。在高保真海事数字孪生和能源网格案例的实验表明，相比先进基线，该框架实现了排放降低15%、吞吐量提高12%、公平成本改善45%，并获得了更强的公平性指标及约束与公平损失的理论后悔界保证。
Nemotron-CrossThink: Scaling Self-Learning beyond Math Reasoning
Authors: Syeda Nahida Akter, Shrimai Prabhumoye, Matvei Novikov, Seungju Han, Ying Lin, Evelina Bakhturina, Eric Nyberg, Yejin Choi, Mostofa Patwary, Mohammad Shoeybi, Bryan Catanzaro
First: 2025-04-15T21:37:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T20:53:21+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 10 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown strong reasoning capabilities, particularly when enhanced through Reinforcement Learning (RL). While prior work has successfully applied RL to mathematical reasoning -- where rules and correctness are well-defined -- generalizing these methods to broader reasoning domains remains challenging due to limited data, the lack of verifiable reward structures, and diverse task requirements. In this work, we propose NEMOTRON-CROSSTHINK, a framework that systematically incorporates multi-domain corpora, including both synthetic and real-world question-answer pairs, into RL training to improve generalization across diverse reasoning tasks. NEMOTRON-CROSSTHINK addresses key challenges by (1) incorporating data from varied sources spanning STEM, humanities, social sciences, etc.; (2) applying structured templates (e.g., multiple-choice and open-ended) to control answer-space complexity; (3) filtering for verifiable answers; and (4) optimizing data blending strategies that utilizes data from multiple sources effectively. Our approach enables scalable and verifiable reward modeling beyond mathematics and demonstrates improved accuracies on both math (MATH-500: +30.1%, AMC23:+27.5%) and non-math reasoning benchmarks (MMLU-PRO: +12.8%, GPQA-DIAMOND: +11.3%, AGIEVAL: +15.1%, SUPERGPQA: +3.8%). Moreover, NEMOTRON-CROSSTHINK exhibits significantly improved response efficiency -- using 28% fewer tokens for correct answers -- highlighting more focused and effective reasoning. Through NEMOTRON-CROSSTHINK, we demonstrate that integrating multi-domain, multi-format data in RL leads to more accurate, efficient, and generalizable LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Nemotron-CrossThink：将自学习扩展至数学推理之外
大型语言模型（LLMs）已展现出强大的推理能力，尤其是在通过强化学习（RL）增强后。先前研究已成功将RL应用于规则和正确性定义明确的数学推理领域，但由于数据有限、缺乏可验证的奖励机制以及任务需求多样化，将这些方法推广至更广泛的推理领域仍具挑战性。本研究提出NEMOTRON-CROSSTHINK框架，通过系统性地将多领域语料（包括合成与真实世界问答对）纳入RL训练，以提升模型在多样化推理任务中的泛化能力。该框架通过以下方式应对关键挑战：（1）整合STEM、人文、社会科学等多源数据；（2）应用结构化模板（如选择题与开放式问题）控制答案空间复杂度；（3）筛选可验证答案；（4）优化多源数据混合策略。我们的方法实现了超越数学领域的可扩展可验证奖励建模，在数学推理基准（MATH-500：+30.1%，AMC23：+27.5%）与非数学推理基准（MMLU-PRO：+12.8%，GPQA-DIAMOND：+11.3%，AGIEVAL：+15.1%，SUPERGPQA：+3.8%）上均取得精度提升。此外，NEMOTRON-CROSSTHINK显著提升响应效率——正确答案的token使用量减少28%，体现了更聚焦高效的推理能力。本研究证明，在RL中整合多领域、多格式数据能构建更精准、高效且泛化能力更强的LLMs。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of extending reinforcement learning (RL) from well-defined mathematical reasoning to broader domains with limited data and verifiable rewards, this paper introduces Nemotron-CrossThink, a framework that systematically integrates multi-domain corpora—including synthetic and real-world question-answer pairs—into RL training to enhance generalization. The method addresses key issues by incorporating diverse data from STEM, humanities, and social sciences, applying structured templates to manage answer complexity, filtering for verifiable answers, and optimizing data blending strategies. Experimental results show significant accuracy improvements on both math benchmarks (e.g., MATH-500: +30.1%) and non-math reasoning tasks (e.g., MMLU-PRO: +12.8%), alongside a 28% reduction in tokens for correct answers, indicating more efficient and focused reasoning.
本文的动机在于将强化学习从规则清晰的数学推理推广到更广泛的领域，这些领域存在数据有限和可验证奖励结构缺乏的挑战。为此，论文提出了Nemotron-CrossThink框架，通过系统地将多领域语料（包括合成和真实世界的问答对）整合到强化学习训练中，以提升泛化能力。该方法通过整合STEM、人文和社会科学等多样数据源、应用结构化模板控制答案复杂度、筛选可验证答案以及优化数据混合策略来解决关键问题。实验结果表明，该框架在数学基准（如MATH-500：+30.1%）和非数学推理任务（如MMLU-PRO：+12.8%）上均实现了显著准确率提升，同时正确回答的令牌使用量减少了28%，体现了更高效和集中的推理能力。
A Loss Landscape Visualization Framework for Interpreting Reinforcement Learning: An ADHDP Case Study
Authors: Jingyi Liu, Jian Guo, Eberhard Gill
First: 2026-03-15T20:47:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T20:47:30+00:00
Comments: Submitted to Acta Astronautica
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning algorithms have been widely used in dynamic and control systems. However, interpreting their internal learning behavior remains a challenge. In the authors' previous work, a critic match loss landscape visualization method was proposed to study critic training. This study extends that method into a framework which provides a multi-perspective view of the learning dynamics, clarifying how value estimation, policy optimization, and temporal-difference (TD) signals interact during training. The proposed framework includes four complementary components; a three-dimensional reconstruction of the critic match loss surface that shows how TD targets shape the optimization geometry; an actor loss landscape under a frozen critic that reveals how the policy exploits that geometry; a trajectory combining time, Bellman error, and policy weights that indicates how updates move across the surface; and a state-TD map that identifies the state regions that drive those updates. The Action-Dependent Heuristic Dynamic Programming (ADHDP) algorithm for spacecraft attitude control is used as a case study. The framework is applied to compare several ADHDP variants and shows how training stabilizers and target updates change the optimization landscape and affect learning stability. Therefore, the proposed framework provides a systematic and interpretable tool for analyzing reinforcement learning behavior across algorithmic designs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习可解释性的损失地形可视化框架：以ADHDP为例
强化学习算法已广泛应用于动态控制系统，但其内部学习行为的可解释性仍具挑战。作者先前提出了一种评论家匹配损失地形可视化方法以研究评论家训练。本研究将该方法扩展为一个框架，提供学习动态的多视角视图，阐明训练过程中价值估计、策略优化与时间差分信号的交互机制。该框架包含四个互补组件：展示时间差分目标如何塑造优化几何的评论家匹配损失面三维重建；在固定评论家下揭示策略如何利用该几何的行动者损失地形；结合时间、贝尔曼误差与策略权重的轨迹，显示更新如何在损失面上移动；以及识别驱动更新的状态区域的状态-时间差分映射。以航天器姿态控制中的动作依赖启发式动态规划算法为例，应用该框架比较多种ADHDP变体，展示训练稳定器与目标更新如何改变优化地形并影响学习稳定性。因此，该框架为跨算法设计的强化学习行为分析提供了系统化、可解释的工具。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of interpreting the internal learning behavior of reinforcement learning algorithms in dynamic control systems, this study extends a prior critic match loss visualization method into a comprehensive multi-perspective framework. The method integrates four components: a 3D critic loss surface reconstruction, an actor loss landscape under a frozen critic, a trajectory combining time and errors, and a state-TD map, collectively clarifying interactions among value estimation, policy optimization, and temporal-difference signals. Using the Action-Dependent Heuristic Dynamic Programming (ADHDP) algorithm for spacecraft attitude control as a case study, experimental results demonstrate the framework's utility in comparing ADHDP variants, revealing how training stabilizers and target updates alter the optimization landscape and impact learning stability, thereby providing a systematic interpretability tool for algorithmic analysis.
本研究针对强化学习算法在动态控制系统中内部学习行为难以解释的问题，将先前提出的评论家匹配损失可视化方法扩展为一个多视角的综合框架。该方法整合了四个组件：三维评论家损失表面重建、固定评论家下的演员损失景观、结合时间与误差的轨迹以及状态时序差分映射，共同阐明了价值估计、策略优化和时序差分信号之间的交互作用。以航天器姿态控制中的动作依赖启发式动态规划（ADHDP）算法为例，实验结果表明该框架能有效比较不同ADHDP变体，揭示训练稳定器和目标更新如何改变优化几何并影响学习稳定性，从而为算法设计提供了一个系统化的可解释性分析工具。
HoRD: Robust Humanoid Control via History-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning and Online Distillation
Authors: Puyue Wang, Jiawei Hu, Yan Gao, Junyan Wang, Yu Zhang, Gillian Dobbie, Tao Gu, Wafa Johal, Ting Dang, Hong Jia
First: 2026-02-04T10:41:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T20:44:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Humanoid robots can suffer significant performance drops under small changes in dynamics, task specifications, or environment setup. We propose HoRD, a two-stage learning framework for robust humanoid control under domain shift. First, we train a high-performance teacher policy via history-conditioned reinforcement learning, where the policy infers latent dynamics context from recent state--action trajectories to adapt online to diverse randomized dynamics. Second, we perform online distillation to transfer the teacher's robust control capabilities into a transformer-based student policy that operates on sparse root-relative 3D joint keypoint trajectories. By combining history-conditioned adaptation with online distillation, HoRD enables a single policy to adapt zero-shot to unseen domains without per-domain retraining. Extensive experiments show HoRD outperforms strong baselines in robustness and transfer, especially under unseen domains and external perturbations. Code and project page are available at https://tonywang-0517.github.io/hord/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HoRD：基于历史条件强化学习与在线蒸馏的鲁棒人形机器人控制
人形机器人在动力学、任务规范或环境设置的微小变化下可能出现性能显著下降。本文提出HoRD，一种面向领域偏移下鲁棒人形控制的两阶段学习框架。首先，通过历史条件强化学习训练高性能教师策略，该策略从近期状态-动作轨迹推断潜在动力学上下文，以在线适应多样随机化动力学。其次，执行在线蒸馏，将教师的鲁棒控制能力迁移至基于Transformer的学生策略，该策略以稀疏的根关节相对三维关键点轨迹为输入。通过结合历史条件适应与在线蒸馏，HoRD使单一策略能够零样本适应未见领域，无需逐领域重新训练。大量实验表明，HoRD在鲁棒性与迁移性上优于强基线方法，尤其在未见领域和外部扰动下表现突出。代码与项目页面详见 https://tonywang-0517.github.io/hord/。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the vulnerability of humanoid robots to performance degradation under minor domain shifts, such as changes in dynamics or task specifications. To enhance robustness, the authors propose HoRD, a two-stage framework: first, a teacher policy is trained using history-conditioned reinforcement learning to infer latent dynamics context from recent trajectories and adapt online to randomized dynamics; second, online distillation transfers this capability to a transformer-based student policy that processes sparse joint keypoint trajectories. Experimental results demonstrate that HoRD outperforms baselines in robustness and zero-shot transfer to unseen domains, effectively handling external perturbations without per-domain retraining.
该论文针对人形机器人在动态或任务规范等微小领域变化下性能下降的问题，提出了一种增强鲁棒性的方法。作者设计了HoRD两阶段框架：首先，通过历史条件强化学习训练教师策略，使其从近期轨迹推断潜在动态上下文并在线适应随机化动态；其次，通过在线蒸馏将这种能力迁移到基于Transformer的学生策略中，该策略处理稀疏的关节关键点轨迹。实验结果表明，HoRD在鲁棒性和零样本迁移到未见领域方面优于基线方法，能有效应对外部扰动且无需针对每个领域重新训练。
Adapting Critic Match Loss Landscape Visualization to Off-policy Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jingyi Liu, Jian Guo, Eberhard Gill
First: 2026-03-15T20:21:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T20:21:22+00:00
Comments: Revised manuscript, submitted to Astrodynamics
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This work extends an established critic match loss landscape visualization method from online to off-policy reinforcement learning (RL), aiming to reveal the optimization geometry behind critic learning. Off-policy RL differs from stepwise online actor-critic learning in its replay-based data flow and target computation. Based on these two structural differences, the critic match loss landscape visualization method is adapted to the Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm by aligning the loss evaluation with its batch-based data flow and target computation, using a fixed replay batch and precomputed critic targets from the selected policy. Critic parameters recorded during training are projected onto a principal component plane, where the critic match loss is evaluated to form a 3-D landscape with an overlaid 2-D optimization path. Applied to a spacecraft attitude control problem, the resulting landscapes are analyzed both qualitatively and quantitatively using sharpness, basin area, and local anisotropy metrics, together with temporal landscape snapshots. Comparisons between convergent SAC, divergent SAC, and divergent Action-Dependent Heuristic Dynamic Programming (ADHDP) cases reveal distinct geometric patterns and optimization behaviors under different algorithmic structures. The results demonstrate that the adapted critic match loss visualization framework serves as a geometric diagnostic tool for analyzing critic optimization dynamics in replay-based off-policy RL-based control problems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：将评论家匹配损失地形可视化方法适配至离策略强化学习
本研究将成熟的评论家匹配损失地形可视化方法从在线强化学习扩展至离策略强化学习，旨在揭示评论家学习背后的优化几何结构。离策略强化学习与逐步在线执行者-评论家学习在基于经验回放的数据流和目标计算方面存在差异。基于这两点结构差异，通过将损失评估与基于批次的数据流及目标计算对齐，采用固定回放批次和从选定策略预计算的评论家目标，将评论家匹配损失地形可视化方法适配至软执行者-评论家算法。训练过程中记录的评论家参数被投影至主成分平面，通过评估评论家匹配损失形成叠加二维优化路径的三维地形图。应用于航天器姿态控制问题时，结合锐度、盆地面积和局部各向异性度量指标及时序地形快照，对生成的地形进行定性与定量分析。通过比较收敛性软执行者-评论家、发散性软执行者-评论家以及发散性动作依赖启发式动态规划三种案例，揭示了不同算法结构下独特的几何模式与优化行为。结果表明，适配后的评论家匹配损失可视化框架可作为几何诊断工具，用于分析基于经验回放的离策略强化学习控制问题中的评论家优化动态。

This work adapts an existing critic match loss landscape visualization method from online to off-policy reinforcement learning, motivated by the need to uncover the optimization geometry underlying critic learning in replay-based settings. The method is tailored to the Soft Actor-Critic algorithm by aligning loss evaluation with its batch data flow and target computation, using fixed replay batches and precomputed critic targets. Experimental results on a spacecraft attitude control problem, analyzed via sharpness and anisotropy metrics, reveal distinct geometric patterns and optimization behaviors in convergent versus divergent cases, demonstrating the framework's utility as a diagnostic tool for critic optimization dynamics in off-policy RL control.
本研究将已有的评论家匹配损失地形可视化方法从在线强化学习扩展到离线策略强化学习，旨在揭示基于经验回放的评论家学习背后的优化几何结构。该方法针对软演员-评论家算法，通过将损失评估与其批处理数据流和目标计算对齐，使用固定的回放批次和预计算的评论家目标来实现。在航天器姿态控制问题上的实验结果表明，通过锐度、盆地面积等指标分析，收敛与发散的算法案例展现出不同的几何模式和优化行为，验证了该适配框架可作为分析离线策略强化学习控制问题中评论家优化动态的几何诊断工具。
Machine Learning-Driven Intelligent Memory System Design: From On-Chip Caches to Storage
Authors: Rahul Bera, Rakesh Nadig, Onur Mutlu
First: 2026-03-15T20:02:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T20:02:05+00:00
Comments: Extended version of the IEEE Micro 2026 article
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the data-rich environment in which memory systems of modern computing platforms operate, many state-of-the-art architectural policies employed in the memory system rely on static, human-designed heuristics that fail to truly adapt to the workload and system behavior via principled learning methodologies. In this article, we propose a fundamentally different design approach: using lightweight and practical machine learning (ML) methods to enable adaptive, data-driven control throughout the memory hierarchy. We present three ML-guided architectural policies: (1) Pythia, a reinforcement learning-based data prefetcher for on-chip caches, (2) Hermes, a perceptron learning-based off-chip predictor for multi-level cache hierarchies, and (3) Sibyl, a reinforcement learning-based data placement policy for hybrid storage systems. Our evaluation shows that Pythia, Hermes, and Sibyl significantly outperform the best-prior human-designed policies, while incurring modest hardware overheads. Collectively, this article demonstrates that integrating adaptive learning into memory subsystems can lead to intelligent, self-optimizing architectures that unlock performance and efficiency gains beyond what is possible with traditional human-designed approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：机器学习驱动的智能内存系统设计：从片上缓存到存储
尽管现代计算平台的内存系统运行在数据丰富的环境中，但许多内存系统中采用的先进架构策略仍依赖于静态、人工设计的启发式方法，未能通过系统化的学习机制真正适应工作负载与系统行为。本文提出一种根本不同的设计思路：利用轻量级且实用的机器学习方法，在整个内存层次结构中实现自适应、数据驱动的控制。我们介绍了三种基于机器学习的架构策略：（1）Pythia，一种基于强化学习的片上缓存数据预取器；（2）Hermes，一种基于感知器学习的多级缓存层次结构片外预测器；（3）Sibyl，一种基于强化学习的混合存储系统数据放置策略。评估表明，Pythia、Hermes和Sibyl在硬件开销适中的情况下，显著优于现有最佳的人工设计策略。本文整体论证了将自适应学习融入内存子系统，能够构建智能、自优化的架构，从而突破传统人工设计方法的局限，实现性能与效率的进一步提升。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of static, human-designed heuristics in modern memory systems, this paper proposes a machine learning-driven approach to enable adaptive, data-driven control across the memory hierarchy. The method introduces three lightweight ML-guided architectural policies: Pythia, a reinforcement learning-based prefetcher for on-chip caches; Hermes, a perceptron learning-based predictor for multi-level cache hierarchies; and Sibyl, a reinforcement learning-based placement policy for hybrid storage.
