CARE What Fails: Contrastive Anchored-REflection for Verifiable Multimodal Reasoning
Authors: Yongxin Wang, Zhicheng Yang, Meng Cao, Mingfei Han, Haokun Lin, Yingying Zhu, Xiaojun Chang, Xiaodan Liang
First: 2025-12-22T16:34:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T18:49:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Group-relative reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) often wastes the most informative data it already has the failures. When all rollouts are wrong, gradients stall; when one happens to be correct, the update usually ignores why the others are close-but-wrong, and credit can be misassigned to spurious chains. We present CARE (Contrastive Anchored REflection), a failure-centric post-training framework for multimodal reasoning that turns errors into supervision. CARE combines: (i) an anchored-contrastive objective that forms a compact subgroup around the best rollout and a set of semantically proximate hard negatives, performs within-subgroup z-score normalization with negative-only scaling, and includes an all-negative rescue to prevent zero-signal batches; and (ii) Reflection-Guided Resampling (RGR), a one-shot structured self-repair that rewrites a representative failure and re-scores it with the same verifier, converting near-misses into usable positives without any test-time reflection. CARE improves accuracy and training smoothness while explicitly increasing the share of learning signal that comes from failures. On Qwen2.5-VL-7B, CARE lifts macro-averaged accuracy by 4.6 points over GRPO across six verifiable visual-reasoning benchmarks; with Qwen3-VL-8B it reaches competitive or state-of-the-art results on MathVista and MMMU-Pro under an identical evaluation protocol.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CARE何以为失：面向可验证多模态推理的对比锚定反思
基于可验证奖励的组相对强化学习（RLVR）常浪费已掌握的最具信息量的失败数据。当所有推演皆错误时梯度停滞；当偶然出现正确推演时，更新过程通常忽略其他近似错误案例的成因，且可能将奖励错误分配至伪因果链。本文提出CARE（对比锚定反思）——一种以失败为中心的多模态推理后训练框架，将错误转化为监督信号。CARE整合：（i）锚定对比目标：围绕最佳推演构建紧凑子群及语义相近的困难负例集，实施子群内仅负例缩放的Z分数归一化，并包含全负例救援机制以避免零信号批次；（ii）反思引导重采样（RGR）：通过单次结构化自修复重写典型失败案例，并用相同验证器重新评分，将近似错误转化为可用正例而无需测试阶段反思。CARE在提升准确率与训练平滑度的同时，显式增加源自失败的学习信号占比。在Qwen2.5-VL-7B上，CARE于六项可验证视觉推理基准的宏平均准确率较GRPO提升4.6个百分点；配合Qwen3-VL-8B时，在相同评估协议下于MathVista和MMMU-Pro达到竞争性或最优水平。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that group-relative reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) often fails to effectively learn from incorrect rollouts, leading to stalled gradients or misassigned credit. To address this, the authors propose CARE (Contrastive Anchored REflection), a failure-centric post-training framework that transforms errors into supervision through an anchored-contrastive objective and Reflection-Guided Resampling (RGR), which rewrites representative failures for reuse. Experimental results show that CARE improves accuracy and training smoothness by leveraging failures, increasing macro-averaged accuracy by 4.6 points over GRPO on six verifiable visual-reasoning benchmarks with Qwen2.5-VL-7B and achieving competitive or state-of-the-art performance on MathVista and MMMU-Pro with Qwen3-VL-8B.
本文的动机是观察到基于可验证奖励的群体相对强化学习（RLVR）常无法有效从错误中学习，导致梯度停滞或信用分配错误。为此，作者提出CARE（对比锚定反思）框架，通过锚定对比目标和反思引导重采样（RGR）将错误转化为监督信号，重写代表性失败案例以供重用。实验结果表明，CARE利用失败数据提升了准确性和训练平滑度，在Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型上，其在六个可验证视觉推理基准上的宏观平均准确率比GRPO提高了4.6个百分点；使用Qwen3-VL-8B时，在相同评估协议下于MathVista和MMMU-Pro上达到了竞争性或最先进的性能。
Separable neural architectures as a primitive for unified predictive and generative intelligence
Authors: Reza T. Batley, Apurba Sarker, Rajib Mostakim, Andrew Klichine, Sourav Saha
First: 2026-03-12T17:56:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T18:39:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Intelligent systems across physics, language and perception often exhibit factorisable structure, yet are typically modelled by monolithic neural architectures that do not explicitly exploit this structure. The separable neural architecture (SNA) addresses this by formalising a representational class that unifies additive, quadratic and tensor-decomposed neural models. By constraining interaction order and tensor rank, SNAs impose a structural inductive bias that factorises high-dimensional mappings into low-arity components. Separability need not be a property of the system itself: it often emerges in the coordinates or representations through which the system is expressed. Crucially, this coordinate-aware formulation reveals a structural analogy between chaotic spatiotemporal dynamics and linguistic autoregression. By treating continuous physical states as smooth, separable embeddings, SNAs enable distributional modelling of chaotic systems. This approach mitigates the nonphysical drift characteristics of deterministic operators whilst remaining applicable to discrete sequences. The compositional versatility of this approach is demonstrated across four domains: autonomous waypoint navigation via reinforcement learning, inverse generation of multifunctional microstructures, distributional modelling of turbulent flow and neural language modelling. These results establish the separable neural architecture as a domain-agnostic primitive for predictive and generative intelligence, capable of unifying both deterministic and distributional representations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：可分离神经架构：作为统一预测与生成智能的基础构件
跨物理、语言与感知的智能系统常呈现可分解结构，但现有模型多采用未显式利用该结构的单一神经架构。可分离神经架构通过形式化一类统一加性、二次及张量分解神经模型的表示类别，解决了这一问题。通过约束交互阶数与张量秩，该架构施加结构性归纳偏置，将高维映射分解为低元组分。可分离性未必是系统固有属性，而常体现于表达系统的坐标或表示中。关键的是，这种坐标感知的构建揭示了混沌时空动力学与语言自回归间的结构类比。通过将连续物理状态视为平滑可分离嵌入，该架构实现了混沌系统的分布建模。此方法在保持适用于离散序列的同时，缓解了确定性算子的非物理漂移特性。该架构的组合灵活性在四个领域得到验证：基于强化学习的自主航点导航、多功能微结构的逆向生成、湍流的分布建模及神经语言建模。这些成果确立了可分离神经架构作为领域无关的预测与生成智能基础构件，能够统一确定性与分布性表示。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that many intelligent systems exhibit factorizable structures, yet conventional neural models often fail to explicitly leverage this property. To address this, the authors propose the separable neural architecture (SNA), a method that formalizes a representational class unifying additive, quadratic, and tensor-decomposed models by constraining interaction order and tensor rank, thereby imposing a structural inductive bias that factorizes high-dimensional mappings. Experimental results across four domains—autonomous navigation via reinforcement learning, inverse generation of multifunctional microstructures, distributional modeling of turbulent flow, and neural language modeling—demonstrate that SNAs effectively mitigate nonphysical drift in chaotic systems and handle discrete sequences, establishing them as a versatile primitive for unified predictive and generative intelligence.
本文的动机在于观察到许多智能系统表现出可分解的结构，但传统神经模型往往未能明确利用这一特性。为此，作者提出了可分离神经架构（SNA）方法，通过约束交互阶数和张量秩，形式化了一个统一加法、二次和张量分解模型的表示类别，从而施加结构归纳偏置以分解高维映射。在四个领域的实验结果表明，包括通过强化学习的自主航点导航、多功能微结构的逆生成、湍流的分布建模以及神经语言建模，SNA有效缓解了混沌系统中的非物理漂移并处理离散序列，确立了其作为统一预测和生成智能的通用基元。
Visualizing Critic Match Loss Landscapes for Interpretation of Online Reinforcement Learning Control Algorithms
Authors: Jingyi Liu, Jian Guo, Eberhard Gill
First: 2026-03-15T18:20:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T18:20:12+00:00
Comments: Revised manuscript, submitted to Acta Astronautica
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has proven its power on various occasions. However, its performance is not always guaranteed when system dynamics change. Instead, it largely relies on users' empirical experience. For reinforcement learning algorithms with an actor-critic structure, the critic neural network reflects the approximation and optimization process in the RL algorithm. Analyzing the performance of the critic neural network helps to understand the mechanism of the algorithm. To support systematic interpretation of such algorithms in dynamic control problems, this work proposes a critic match loss landscape visualization method for online reinforcement learning. The method constructs a loss landscape by projecting recorded critic parameter trajectories onto a low-dimensional linear subspace. The critic match loss is evaluated over the projected parameter grid using fixed reference state samples and temporal-difference targets. This yields a three-dimensional loss surface together with a two-dimensional optimization path that characterizes critic learning behavior. To extend analysis beyond visual inspection, quantitative landscape indices and a normalized system performance index are introduced, enabling structured comparison across different training outcomes. The approach is demonstrated using the Action-Dependent Heuristic Dynamic Programming algorithm on cart-pole and spacecraft attitude control tasks. Comparative analyses across projection methods and training stages reveal distinct landscape characteristics associated with stable convergence and unstable learning. The proposed framework enables both qualitative and quantitative interpretation of critic optimization behavior in online reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：可视化在线强化学习控制算法中评论家匹配损失地形以支持算法解释
强化学习已在多种场景中展现其强大能力，但其性能在系统动态变化时并不总能保证，很大程度上依赖于用户的经验。对于具有演员-评论家结构的强化学习算法，评论家神经网络反映了算法中的逼近与优化过程。分析评论家神经网络的性能有助于理解算法机制。为支持在动态控制问题中对这类算法进行系统性解释，本研究提出了一种用于在线强化学习的评论家匹配损失地形可视化方法。该方法通过将记录的评论家参数轨迹投影到低维线性子空间来构建损失地形，并利用固定参考状态样本与时序差分目标在投影参数网格上评估评论家匹配损失，从而生成三维损失曲面及表征评论家学习行为的二维优化路径。为超越视觉检查的分析，引入了量化地形指标与归一化系统性能指标，支持对不同训练结果进行结构化比较。该方法通过倒立摆和航天器姿态控制任务中的动作依赖启发式动态规划算法进行了验证。对不同投影方法和训练阶段的比较分析揭示了与稳定收敛及不稳定学习相关的显著地形特征。所提框架实现了对在线强化学习中评论家优化行为的定性与定量解释。

The proposed method visualizes the critic match loss landscape by projecting the critic neural network's parameter trajectories onto a low-dimensional subspace and evaluating the loss over a grid using fixed state samples and temporal-difference targets, yielding a 3D loss surface with a 2D optimization path. In experiments with Action-Dependent Heuristic Dynamic Programming on cart-pole and spacecraft attitude control tasks, the visualization and introduced quantitative landscape indices revealed distinct characteristics correlating with stable convergence versus unstable learning, enabling structured qualitative and quantitative analysis of critic optimization behavior.
本研究的动机是，当系统动态变化时，在线强化学习控制算法的性能难以保证且依赖经验调参，因此需要更好地解释和理解其机制。该方法通过将评判器神经网络的参数轨迹投影到低维子空间，并使用固定状态样本和时间差分目标在网格上评估损失，构建了评判器匹配损失景观，从而生成带有二维优化路径的三维损失曲面。在基于动作相关启发式动态规划对倒立摆和航天器姿态控制任务的实验中，可视化结果及引入的定量景观指标揭示了与稳定收敛和不稳定学习相关的不同特征，实现了对评判器优化行为的结构化定性与定量分析。
Learning Unmasking Policies for Diffusion Language Models
Authors: Metod Jazbec, Theo X. Olausson, Louis Béthune, Pierre Ablin, Michael Kirchhof, João Monteiro, Victor Turrisi, Jason Ramapuram, Marco Cuturi
First: 2025-12-09T20:44:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T18:11:47+00:00
Comments: V3: Added qualitative analyses, more detailed explanations and new additional experiments in the appendices
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion (Large) Language Models (dLLMs) now match the downstream performance of their autoregressive counterparts on many tasks, while holding the promise of being more efficient during inference. One critical design aspect of dLLMs is the sampling procedure that selects which tokens to unmask at each diffusion step. Indeed, recent work has found that heuristic strategies such as confidence thresholding improve both sample quality and token throughput compared to random unmasking. However, such heuristics have downsides: they require manual tuning, and we observe that their performance degrades with larger block sizes. In this work, we instead propose to train sampling procedures using reinforcement learning. Specifically, we formalize masked diffusion sampling as a Markov decision process in which the dLLM serves as the environment, and propose a lightweight policy based on a single-layer transformer that maps dLLM token confidences to unmasking decisions. Our experiments show that these trained policies match the performance of state-of-the-art heuristics when combined with semi-autoregressive (block) generation, while outperforming them in the full-diffusion setting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：扩散语言模型的解掩码策略学习
扩散（大）语言模型（dLLMs）已在多项任务中达到与自回归模型相当的下游性能，同时具备更高的推理效率潜力。dLLMs的关键设计环节是采样过程，即在每个扩散步骤中选择解掩码的标记。近期研究表明，相比随机解掩码，基于置信度阈值等启发式策略能同时提升样本质量和标记吞吐量。但此类启发式方法存在缺陷：需手动调参，且我们发现其性能随块尺寸增大而下降。本研究转而提出通过强化学习训练采样过程：将掩码扩散采样形式化为马尔可夫决策过程（dLLM作为环境），并设计基于单层Transformer的轻量级策略，将dLLM标记置信度映射至解掩码决策。实验表明，训练所得策略在半自回归（块）生成场景中与前沿启发式方法性能相当，在全扩散场景中则表现更优。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the inefficiency of heuristic token unmasking strategies in diffusion language models by proposing a reinforcement learning approach to learn optimal unmasking policies. The method formalizes the sampling process as a Markov decision process, employing a lightweight transformer-based policy that uses token confidences to decide which tokens to unmask at each diffusion step. Experimental results demonstrate that the learned policies achieve performance comparable to state-of-the-art heuristics in semi-autoregressive generation and surpass them in full-diffusion settings, while eliminating the need for manual tuning.
本文针对扩散语言模型中启发式令牌解掩策略效率不足的问题，提出了一种基于强化学习的方法来学习最优解掩策略。该方法将采样过程形式化为马尔可夫决策过程，采用一个轻量级的基于Transformer的策略网络，根据令牌置信度决定每个扩散步骤中应解掩的令牌。实验结果表明，学习的策略在半自回归生成中与最先进的启发式方法性能相当，在全扩散设置中则表现更优，同时避免了手动调参的需求。
VLA-Thinker: Boosting Vision-Language-Action Models through Thinking-with-Image Reasoning
Authors: Chaoyang Wang, Wenrui Bao, Sicheng Gao, Bingxin Xu, Yu Tian, Yogesh S. Rawat, Yunhao Ge, Yuzhang Shang
First: 2026-03-15T17:59:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T17:59:51+00:00
Comments: We introduce VLA-Thinker, the first VLA model capable of thinking-with-image reasoning, which models visual perception as a dynamically invocable reasoning action, enabling Multimodal Embodied Chain-of-Thought
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown promising capabilities for embodied intelligence, but most existing approaches rely on text-based chain-of-thought reasoning where visual inputs are treated as static context. This limits the ability of the model to actively revisit the environment and resolve ambiguities during long-horizon tasks. We propose VLA-Thinker, a thinking-with-image reasoning framework that models perception as a dynamically invocable reasoning action. To train such a system, we introduce a two-stage training pipeline consisting of (1) an SFT cold-start phase with curated visual Chain-of-Thought data to activate structured reasoning and tool-use behaviors, and (2) GRPO-based reinforcement learning to align complete reasoning-action trajectories with task-level success. Extensive experiments on LIBERO and RoboTwin 2.0 benchmarks demonstrate that VLA-Thinker significantly improves manipulation performance, achieving 97.5% success rate on LIBERO and strong gains across long-horizon robotic tasks. Project and Codes: https://cywang735.github.io/VLA-Thinker/ .
中文标题/摘要

The motivation for VLA-Thinker is to overcome the limitation of existing Vision-Language-Action models, which treat visual input as static context in text-based reasoning, thereby hindering active environmental revisiting and ambiguity resolution in long-horizon tasks. The method introduces a thinking-with-image reasoning framework that models perception as a dynamically invocable reasoning action, trained via a two-stage pipeline: first, supervised fine-tuning with curated visual Chain-of-Thought data to activate structured reasoning, followed by GRPO-based reinforcement learning to align reasoning-action trajectories with task success. A Survey of Reinforcement Learning For Economics
Authors: Pranjal Rawat
First: 2026-03-09T21:43:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T17:49:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This survey (re)introduces reinforcement learning methods to economists. The curse of dimensionality limits how far exact dynamic programming can be effectively applied, forcing us to rely on suitably "small" problems or our ability to convert "big" problems into smaller ones. While this reduction has been sufficient for many classical applications, a growing class of economic models resists such reduction. Reinforcement learning algorithms offer a natural, sample-based extension of dynamic programming, extending tractability to problems with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. I review the theory connecting classical planning to modern learning algorithms and demonstrate their mechanics through simulated examples in pricing, inventory control, strategic games, and preference elicitation. I also examine the practical vulnerabilities of these algorithms, noting their brittleness, sample inefficiency, sensitivity to hyperparameters, and the absence of global convergence guarantees outside of tabular settings. The successes of reinforcement learning remain strictly bounded by these constraints, as well as a reliance on accurate simulators. When guided by economic structure, reinforcement learning provides a remarkably flexible framework. It stands as an imperfect, but promising, addition to the computational economist's toolkit. A companion survey (Rust and Rawat, 2026b) covers the inverse problem of inferring preferences from observed behavior. All simulation code is publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在经济学中的应用综述
本文向经济学家（重新）介绍了强化学习方法。维度灾难限制了精确动态规划的有效应用范围，迫使我们依赖适当的“小”问题或将“大”问题转化为较小问题的能力。尽管这种简化对许多经典应用已足够，但越来越多的经济模型难以进行此类简化。强化学习算法提供了一种基于样本的动态规划自然扩展，将可处理性延伸至高维状态、连续动作和策略交互的问题。本文回顾了连接经典规划与现代学习算法的理论，并通过定价、库存控制、策略博弈和偏好诱导的模拟示例展示其机制。同时，文章分析了这些算法的实际脆弱性，包括其脆弱性、样本效率低下、对超参数的敏感性，以及在非表格化场景中缺乏全局收敛保证。强化学习的成功仍严格受限于这些约束以及对精确模拟器的依赖。在经济结构的指导下，强化学习提供了一个极为灵活的框架，虽不完美但前景可期，是计算经济学家工具箱的有力补充。配套综述（Rust与Rawat，2026b）涵盖了从观测行为推断偏好的逆问题。所有模拟代码均已公开。
Summary / 总结
This survey aims to introduce reinforcement learning (RL) to economists as a method to overcome the curse of dimensionality in dynamic programming, which restricts classical approaches to small or reducible problems. The method involves using sample-based RL algorithms to extend tractability to economic models with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. Experimental results from simulated examples in pricing, inventory control, games, and preference elicitation demonstrate RL's flexibility, but also reveal practical vulnerabilities such as brittleness, sample inefficiency, hyperparameter sensitivity, and lack of global convergence guarantees, limiting its success to contexts with accurate simulators and guided economic structure.
本综述旨在向经济学家介绍强化学习方法，以解决动态规划中维度灾难的限制，该限制迫使经典方法仅适用于小型或可简化的问题。该方法利用基于样本的强化学习算法，将可处理性扩展到具有高维状态、连续动作和策略互动的经济模型中。在定价、库存控制、策略游戏和偏好诱导的模拟实验结果表明，强化学习具有灵活性，但也揭示了其实际脆弱性，如脆弱性、样本效率低下、超参数敏感性以及缺乏全局收敛保证，这些约束使其成功依赖于准确的模拟器和经济结构的指导。
Parametrized Sharing for Multi-Agent Hybrid DRL for Multiple Multi-Functional RISs-Aided Downlink NOMA Networks
Authors: Chi-Te Kuo, Li-Hsiang Shen, Jyun-Jhe Huang
First: 2026-01-02T02:44:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T16:24:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-functional reconfigurable intelligent surface (MF-RIS) is conceived to address the communication efficiency thanks to its extended signal coverage from its active RIS capability and self-sustainability from energy harvesting (EH). We investigate the architecture of multi-MF-RISs to assist non-orthogonal multiple access (NOMA) downlink networks. We formulate an energy efficiency (EE) maximization problem by optimizing power allocation, transmit beamforming and MF-RIS configurations of amplitudes, phase-shifts and EH ratios, as well as the position of MF-RISs, while satisfying constraints of available power, user rate requirements, and self-sustainability property. We design a parametrized sharing scheme for multi-agent hybrid deep reinforcement learning (PMHRL), where the multi-agent proximal policy optimization (PPO) and deep-Q network (DQN) handle continuous and discrete variables, respectively. The simulation results have demonstrated that proposed PMHRL has the highest EE compared to other benchmarks, including cases without parametrized sharing, pure PPO and DQN. Moreover, the proposed multi-MF-RISs-aided downlink NOMA achieves the highest EE compared to scenarios of no-EH/amplification, traditional RISs, and deployment without RISs/MF-RISs under different multiple access.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多智能体混合深度强化学习的参数化共享策略在多功能可重构智能表面辅助下行NOMA网络中的应用
多功能可重构智能表面（MF-RIS）凭借其主动RIS能力带来的扩展信号覆盖和能量收集（EH）实现的自持特性，旨在提升通信效率。本文研究了多MF-RIS辅助非正交多址（NOMA）下行网络的架构，通过联合优化功率分配、发射波束成形、MF-RIS的幅度/相移/EH比率配置及其部署位置，构建了能量效率（EE）最大化问题，并满足可用功率、用户速率需求和自持特性约束。设计了一种多智能体混合深度强化学习参数化共享方案（PMHRL），其中多智能体近端策略优化（PPO）和深度Q网络（DQN）分别处理连续与离散变量。仿真结果表明，相较于无参数化共享、纯PPO和DQN等基准方案，所提PMHRL实现了最高的EE。此外，在不同多址场景下，所提多MF-RIS辅助下行NOMA方案相比无EH/放大、传统RIS以及无RIS/MF-RIS部署的场景均获得了最优EE性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to enhance communication efficiency and self-sustainability in wireless networks through multi-functional reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (MF-RISs), which combine active signal amplification with energy harvesting. The method proposes a parametrized sharing scheme for multi-agent hybrid deep reinforcement learning (PMHRL), integrating proximal policy optimization for continuous variables like power allocation and beamforming with deep-Q networks for discrete variables such as RIS configurations and positions, to maximize energy efficiency in a downlink NOMA system. Experimental results show that PMHRL outperforms benchmarks including non-sharing, pure PPO, and DQN approaches, and that the multi-MF-RISs-aided NOMA setup achieves higher energy efficiency compared to scenarios without energy harvesting, traditional RISs, or no RIS deployment.
本文旨在通过多功能可重构智能表面（MF-RISs）提升无线网络的通信效率和自持能力，MF-RISs结合了主动信号放大和能量收集功能。方法上，提出了一种参数化共享的多智能体混合深度强化学习方案（PMHRL），整合近端策略优化处理连续变量（如功率分配和波束成形）和深度Q网络处理离散变量（如RIS配置和位置），以优化下行非正交多址接入网络的能效。实验结果表明，PMHRL在能效上优于无参数共享、纯近端策略优化和深度Q网络等基准方法，且基于多MF-RISs的非正交多址接入方案在能效上超越了无能量收集、传统RIS或无RIS部署的场景。
Physics-Informed Policy Optimization via Analytic Dynamics Regularization
Authors: Namai Chandra, Liu Mohan, Zhihao Gu, Lin Wang
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-03-15T16:20:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T16:20:45+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 8 figures. Submitted to ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has achieved strong performance in robotic control; however, state-of-the-art policy learning methods, such as actor-critic methods, still suffer from high sample complexity and often produce physically inconsistent actions. This limitation stems from neural policies implicitly rediscovering complex physics from data alone, despite accurate dynamics models being readily available in simulators. In this paper, we introduce a novel physics-informed RL framework, called PIPER, that seamlessly integrates physical constraints directly into neural policy optimization with analytical soft physics constraints. At the core of our method is the integration of a differentiable Lagrangian residual as a regularization term within the actor's objective. This residual, extracted from a robot's simulator description, subtly biases policy updates towards dynamically consistent solutions. Crucially, this physics integration is realized through an additional loss term during policy optimization, requiring no alterations to existing simulators or core RL algorithms. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method significantly improves learning efficiency, stability, and control accuracy, establishing a new paradigm for efficient and physically consistent robotic control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于解析动力学正则化的物理信息策略优化
强化学习（RL）在机器人控制领域已取得显著成效，但最先进的策略学习方法（如演员-评论家方法）仍面临样本复杂度高且常产生物理不一致动作的问题。这一局限源于神经网络策略仅从数据中隐式重新发现复杂物理规律，尽管仿真器中已有精确的动力学模型可用。本文提出名为PIPER的新型物理信息强化学习框架，通过解析软物理约束将物理限制无缝集成至神经策略优化中。该方法的核心是在演员目标函数中引入可微拉格朗日残差作为正则化项。该残差从机器人仿真描述中提取，能微妙地将策略更新导向动力学一致的解。关键在于，这种物理集成通过策略优化过程中的附加损失项实现，无需修改现有仿真器或核心强化学习算法。大量实验表明，该方法显著提升了学习效率、稳定性和控制精度，为高效且物理一致的机器人控制建立了新范式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high sample complexity and physically inconsistent actions of standard actor-critic reinforcement learning methods in robotic control, this paper introduces PIPER, a physics-informed RL framework that integrates analytical soft physics constraints directly into policy optimization. The method incorporates a differentiable Lagrangian residual from a robot's simulator as a regularization term in the actor's objective, biasing updates toward dynamically consistent solutions without modifying simulators or core RL algorithms. Experimental results demonstrate that PIPER significantly improves learning efficiency, stability, and control accuracy, establishing a new paradigm for efficient and physically consistent robotic control.
针对机器人控制中标准行动者-评论家强化学习方法样本复杂度高、动作物理不一致的问题，本文提出了PIPER框架，将解析软物理约束直接集成到策略优化中。该方法的核心是将机器人模拟器中的可微拉格朗日残差作为正则化项纳入行动者目标，在不修改模拟器或核心RL算法的情况下，引导策略更新趋向动态一致解。大量实验表明，该方法显著提升了学习效率、稳定性和控制精度，为高效且物理一致的机器人控制建立了新范式。
QLLM: Do We Really Need a Mixing Network for Credit Assignment in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning?
Authors: Yuanjun Li, Zhouyang Jiang, Bin Zhang, Mingchao Zhang, Junhao Zhao, Zhiwei Xu
First: 2025-04-17T14:07:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T14:37:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Credit assignment remains a fundamental challenge in multi agent reinforcement learning (MARL) and is commonly addressed through value decomposition under the centralized training with decentralized ex ecution (CTDE) paradigm. However, existing value decomposition meth ods typically rely on predefined mixing networks that require additional training, often leading to imprecise credit attribution and limited in terpretability. We propose QLLM, a novel framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to construct training-free credit assign ment functions (TFCAFs), where the TFCAFs are nonlinear with re spect to the global state and offer enhanced interpretability while intro ducing no extra learnable parameters. A coder-evaluator framework is employed to ensure the correctness and executability of the generated code. Extensive experiments on standard MARL benchmarks demon strate that QLLM consistently outperforms baselines while requiring fewer learnable parameters. Furthermore, it demonstrates generalization across a broad set of value decomposition algorithms. Code is available at https://github.com/MaoMaoLYJ/pymarl-qllm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QLLM：多智能体强化学习中的信用分配真的需要混合网络吗？
信用分配是多智能体强化学习（MARL）的核心挑战，通常通过集中训练分散执行（CTDE）范式下的价值分解方法解决。然而，现有价值分解方法普遍依赖需要额外训练的预定义混合网络，常导致信用分配不精确且可解释性有限。本文提出QLLM框架，利用大语言模型（LLMs）构建免训练的信用分配函数（TFCAFs）。该函数相对于全局状态具有非线性特性，在无需引入额外可学习参数的同时显著提升可解释性。通过采用编码器-评估器框架确保生成代码的正确性与可执行性。在标准MARL基准上的大量实验表明，QLLM在减少可学习参数的同时持续优于基线方法，并能泛化至多种价值分解算法。代码已开源：https://github.com/MaoMaoLYJ/pymarl-qllm。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of credit assignment in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), where existing methods often rely on predefined, trainable mixing networks that can lead to imprecise credit attribution and poor interpretability. The authors propose QLLM, a novel framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to construct training-free credit assignment functions (TFCAFs), which are nonlinear with respect to the global state and introduce no additional learnable parameters, while a coder-evaluator framework ensures the correctness of the generated code. Experimental results on standard MARL benchmarks show that QLLM consistently outperforms baseline methods with fewer parameters and demonstrates strong generalization across various value decomposition algorithms.
本文针对多智能体强化学习中的信用分配挑战，现有方法通常依赖预定义且需训练的组合网络，这可能导致信用分配不精确且可解释性差。作者提出QLLM框架，利用大语言模型构建无需训练的信用分配函数，该函数相对于全局状态是非线性的，不引入额外可学习参数，并通过编码器-评估器框架确保生成代码的正确性。在标准多智能体强化学习基准上的实验表明，QLLM在参数更少的情况下持续优于基线方法，并在多种价值分解算法中展现出良好的泛化能力。
Co-rewarding: Stable Self-supervised RL for Eliciting Reasoning in Large Language Models
Authors: Zizhuo Zhang, Jianing Zhu, Xinmu Ge, Zihua Zhao, Zhanke Zhou, Xuan Li, Xiao Feng, Jiangchao Yao, Bo Han
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-08-01T08:09:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T14:23:42+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) is effective to improve the reasoning ability of large language models (LLMs), its reliance on human-annotated labels leads to the scaling up dilemma, especially for complex tasks. Recent self-rewarding methods investigate a label-free alternative to unlock the reasoning capabilities of LLMs, yet they frequently encounter the non-negligible training collapse issue, as the single-view supervision signal easily forms the self-consistent illusion, yielding the reward hacking. Inspired by the success of self-supervised learning, we propose \textit{Co-rewarding}, a novel self-supervised RL framework that improves training stability by seeking complementary supervision from another views. Specifically, we instantiate Co-rewarding in two ways: (1) \textit{Co-rewarding-I} is a data-side instantiation that derives reward signals from contrastive agreement across semantically analogous questions; and (2) \textit{Co-rewarding-II} is a model-side instantiation that maintains a slowly-updated reference teacher with pseudo labels to realize self-distillation. Intuitively, such instantiations introduce different levels of discrepancy to increase the difficulty of training collapse on trivial reasoning solutions. We also explore their orthogonally combined version to further boost the performance. Empirically, Co-rewarding exhibits stable training across various setups, and outperforms other self-rewarding baselines by $+3.31\%$ improvements on average on multiple mathematical reasoning benchmarks, especially by $+7.49\%$ on Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct. Notably, Co-rewarding reaches or even surpasses RLVR with ground-truth (GT) label in several cases, such as a Pass@$1$ of $94.01\%$ on GSM8K with Qwen3-8B-Base remarkably higher than GT. Our code is released at https://github.com/tmlr-group/Co-rewarding.
中文标题/摘要
标题：协同奖励：基于稳定自监督强化学习激发大语言模型推理能力
尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）能有效提升大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但其对人工标注标签的依赖导致扩展困境，尤其在复杂任务中。近期自奖励方法探索了无需标注的替代方案以释放LLMs的推理潜力，却常面临不可忽视的训练崩溃问题——单视角监督信号易形成自洽幻觉，导致奖励破解。受自监督学习成功启发，我们提出\textit{协同奖励}，一种新颖的自监督强化学习框架，通过从其他视角寻求互补监督来提升训练稳定性。具体实现包括：（1）\textit{协同奖励-I}为数据侧实例化，通过语义相似问题的对比一致性生成奖励信号；（2）\textit{协同奖励-II}为模型侧实例化，通过维护带伪标签的缓更新参考教师实现自蒸馏。这两种实例化通过引入不同层级的差异度，增加模型陷入平凡推理解的训练崩溃难度。我们还探索了二者的正交组合版本以进一步提升性能。实验表明，协同奖励在多种设置下均保持稳定训练，在多个数学推理基准上平均超越其他自奖励基线$+3.31\%$，尤其在Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct上提升$+7.49\%$。值得注意的是，协同奖励在多个场景（如Qwen3-8B-Base在GSM8K上达到$94.01\%$的Pass@$1$）达到甚至超越基于真实标签的RLVR。代码已开源：https://github.com/tmlr-group/Co-rewarding。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the scaling limitations of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for improving reasoning in large language models (LLMs), which relies on costly human labels, and the instability of label-free self-rewarding methods that often suffer from training collapse due to self-consistent illusions. To overcome this, the authors propose Co-rewarding, a self-supervised RL framework that enhances stability by introducing complementary supervision through two instantiations: Co-rewarding-I, which derives rewards from contrastive agreement across semantically similar questions, and Co-rewarding-II, which uses a slowly-updated reference teacher for self-distillation, both designed to increase discrepancy and prevent trivial solutions. Experimental results show that Co-rewarding achieves stable training and outperforms other self-rewarding baselines by an average of +3.31% on multiple mathematical reasoning benchmarks, with notable gains like +7.49% on Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct, and even matches or surpasses RLVR with ground-truth labels in cases such as a 94.01% Pass@1 on GSM8K with Qwen3-8B-Base.
本文针对使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在提升大语言模型推理能力时依赖昂贵人工标注导致的扩展困境，以及无标注自奖励方法因自洽幻觉易引发训练崩溃的不稳定性问题，提出了一种名为协同奖励的自监督强化学习框架。该框架通过引入互补监督来增强稳定性，具体实例化为两种方式：协同奖励-I从语义相似问题的对比一致性中推导奖励信号，协同奖励-II则通过维护一个缓慢更新的参考教师模型进行自蒸馏，两者均旨在增加差异以防止训练陷入平凡解。实验结果表明，协同奖励在多种设置下实现了稳定训练，在多个数学推理基准测试中平均优于其他自奖励基线3.31%，如在Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct上提升7.49%，并在某些情况下达到甚至超越了使用真实标签的RLVR性能，例如使用Qwen3-8B-Base在GSM8K上取得了94.01%的Pass@1分数。
Taxonomy and Trends in Reinforcement Learning for Robotics and Control Systems: A Structured Review
Authors: Kumater Ter, Abolanle Adetifa, Daniel Udekwe
First: 2025-10-11T20:16:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T14:14:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a foundational approach for enabling intelligent robotic behavior in dynamic and uncertain environments. This work presents an in-depth review of RL principles, advanced deep reinforcement learning (DRL) algorithms, and their integration into robotic and control systems. Beginning with the formalism of Markov Decision Processes (MDPs), the study outlines essential elements of the agent-environment interaction and explores core algorithmic strategies including actor-critic methods, value-based learning, and policy gradients. Emphasis is placed on modern DRL techniques such as DDPG, TD3, PPO, and SAC, which have shown promise in solving high-dimensional, continuous control tasks. A structured taxonomy is introduced to categorize RL applications across domains such as locomotion, manipulation, multi-agent coordination, and human-robot interaction, along with training methodologies and deployment readiness levels. The review synthesizes recent research efforts, highlighting technical trends, design patterns, and the growing maturity of RL in real-world robotics. Overall, this work aims to bridge theoretical advances with practical implementations, providing a consolidated perspective on the evolving role of RL in autonomous robotic systems.

标题：机器人学与控制系统中强化学习的分类体系与发展趋势：结构化综述

Enhancing Sample Efficiency in Multi-Agent RL with Uncertainty Quantification and Selective Exploration
Authors: Tom Danino, Nahum Shimkin
First: 2025-06-03T13:13:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T14:07:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) methods have achieved state-of-the-art results on a range of multi-agent tasks. Yet, MARL algorithms typically require significantly more environment interactions than their single-agent counterparts to converge, a problem exacerbated by the difficulty in exploring over a large joint action space and the high variance intrinsic to MARL environments. To tackle these issues, we propose a novel algorithm that combines a decomposed centralized critic with decentralized ensemble learning, incorporating several key contributions. The main component in our scheme is a selective exploration method that leverages ensemble kurtosis. We extend the global decomposed critic with a diversity-regularized ensemble of individual critics and utilize its excess kurtosis to guide exploration toward high-uncertainty states and actions. To improve sample efficiency, we train the centralized critic with a novel truncated variation of the TD($λ$) algorithm, enabling efficient off-policy learning with reduced variance. On the actor side, our suggested algorithm adapts the mixed samples approach to MARL, mixing on-policy and off-policy loss functions for training the actors. This approach balances between stability and efficiency and outperforms purely off-policy learning. The evaluation shows our method outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on standard MARL benchmarks, including a variety of SMAC II maps.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于不确定性量化与选择性探索提升多智能体强化学习的样本效率
多智能体强化学习方法已在多项多智能体任务中取得先进成果，但其收敛通常需要比单智能体方法更多的环境交互，这一难点因大规模联合动作空间的探索困难及环境固有高方差而加剧。为此，我们提出一种结合分解式中心化评价器与去中心化集成学习的新算法，包含以下核心贡献：采用基于集成峰度的选择性探索机制，通过多样性正则化的个体评价器集成扩展全局分解评价器，并利用其超值峰度引导智能体探索高不确定性的状态与动作；为提升样本效率，采用截断型TD(λ)算法变体训练中心化评价器，实现方差更小的高效离策略学习；在执行器层面，算法将混合样本方法适配至多智能体场景，融合同策略与离策略损失函数进行训练，在稳定性与效率间取得平衡。实验表明，本方法在包括多种SMAC II地图的标准多智能体强化学习基准测试中均优于现有先进基线。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the high sample inefficiency of multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), which stems from the large joint action space and high environmental variance. The proposed method enhances sample efficiency by introducing a decomposed centralized critic combined with decentralized ensemble learning, where a selective exploration mechanism uses ensemble kurtosis to guide agents toward high-uncertainty states and actions. It employs a truncated TD(λ) algorithm for low-variance off-policy critic training and mixes on-policy and off-policy losses for actor training to balance stability and efficiency. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on standard MARL benchmarks, including various SMAC II maps.
本文针对多智能体强化学习（MARL）中因联合动作空间大和环境方差高导致的样本效率低下问题，提出了一种新方法。该方法通过结合分解的集中式评论家与去中心化集成学习来提高样本效率，其中选择性探索机制利用集成峰度引导智能体探索高不确定性的状态和动作。它采用截断TD(λ)算法进行低方差的离策略评论家训练，并混合策略和离策略损失进行执行器训练以平衡稳定性和效率。实验结果表明，该方法在包括多种SMAC II地图在内的标准MARL基准测试中优于现有先进基线。
From $\boldsymbol{\logπ}$ to $\boldsymbolπ$: Taming Divergence in Soft Clipping via Bilateral Decoupled Decay of Probability Gradient Weight
Authors: Xiaoliang Fu, Jiaye Lin, Yangyi Fang, Chaowen Hu, Cong Qin, Zekai Shao, Binbin Zheng, Lu Pan, Ke Zeng
First: 2026-03-15T14:00:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T14:00:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has catalyzed a leap in Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning, yet its optimization dynamics remain fragile. Standard algorithms like GRPO enforce stability via ``hard clipping'', which inadvertently stifles exploration by discarding gradients of tokens outside the trust region. While recent ``soft clipping'' methods attempt to recover these gradients, they suffer from a critical challenge: relying on log-probability gradient ($\nabla_θ\log π_θ$) yields divergent weights as probabilities vanish, destabilizing LLM training. We rethink this convention by establishing probability gradient ($\nabla_θπ_θ$) as the superior optimization primitive. Accordingly, we propose Decoupled Gradient Policy Optimization (DGPO), which employs a decoupled decay mechanism based on importance sampling ratios. By applying asymmetric, continuous decay to boundary tokens, DGPO resolves the conflict between stability and sustained exploration. Extensive experiments across DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen series models (1.5B/7B/14B) demonstrate that DGPO consistently outperforms strong baselines on various mathematical benchmarks, offering a robust and scalable solution for RLVR. Our code and implementation are available at: https://github.com/VenomRose-Juri/DGPO-RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从$\boldsymbol{\logπ}$到$\boldsymbolπ$：通过概率梯度权重的双边解耦衰减驯服软截断中的发散问题
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）推动了大型语言模型（LLM）推理能力的飞跃，但其优化动态仍显脆弱。GRPO等标准算法通过“硬截断”强制稳定性，却因丢弃信任区域外词元的梯度而无意中抑制了探索。尽管近期“软截断”方法尝试恢复这些梯度，却面临关键挑战：依赖对数概率梯度（$\nabla_θ\log π_θ$）会在概率趋零时产生发散权重，破坏LLM训练的稳定性。我们通过确立概率梯度（$\nabla_θπ_θ$）作为更优的优化基元来重新审视这一惯例，据此提出解耦梯度策略优化（DGPO）。该方法基于重要性采样比率采用解耦衰减机制，通过对边界词元施加非对称连续衰减，解决了稳定性与持续探索之间的冲突。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen系列模型（1.5B/7B/14B）上的大量实验表明，DGPO在各类数学基准测试中持续超越强基线，为RLVR提供了稳健且可扩展的解决方案。代码实现已开源：https://github.com/VenomRose-Juri/DGPO-RL。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the fragility of optimization dynamics in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for Large Language Models, where standard hard clipping methods hinder exploration by discarding gradients, and recent soft clipping approaches suffer from instability due to divergent weights from log-probability gradients. The method introduces Decoupled Gradient Policy Optimization (DGPO), which rethinks the optimization primitive by using probability gradients instead of log-probability gradients and employs a decoupled decay mechanism based on importance sampling ratios with asymmetric, continuous decay for boundary tokens to balance stability and exploration. Main experimental results show that DGPO consistently outperforms strong baselines across various mathematical benchmarks using DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen series models (1.5B/7B/14B), demonstrating its robustness and scalability for RLVR.
本研究的动机源于可验证奖励强化学习在大型语言模型推理中优化动态的脆弱性，其中标准的硬裁剪方法因丢弃梯度而抑制探索，而最近的软裁剪方法则因依赖对数概率梯度导致权重发散而不稳定。方法上提出了解耦梯度策略优化，通过使用概率梯度替代对数概率梯度作为优化原语，并基于重要性采样比率采用解耦衰减机制，对边界令牌进行不对称连续衰减，以解决稳定性与持续探索之间的冲突。主要实验结果表明，在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen系列模型上，DGPO在多种数学基准测试中 consistently 优于强基线，为RLVR提供了一个鲁棒且可扩展的解决方案。
SPARQ: Spiking Early-Exit Neural Networks for Energy-Efficient Edge AI
Authors: Parth Patne, Mahdi Taheri, Ali Mahani, Maksim Jenihhin, Reza Mahani, Christian Herglotz
First: 2026-03-15T13:38:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T13:38:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Spiking neural networks (SNNs) offer inherent energy efficiency due to their event-driven computation model, making them promising for edge AI deployment. However, their practical adoption is limited by the computational overhead of deep architectures and the absence of input-adaptive control. This work presents SPARQ, a unified framework that integrates spiking computation, quantization-aware training, and reinforcement learning-guided early exits for efficient and adaptive inference. Evaluations across MLP, LeNet, and AlexNet architectures demonstrated that the proposed Quantised Dynamic SNNs (QDSNN) consistently outperform conventional SNNs and QSNNs, achieving up to 5.15% higher accuracy over QSNNs, over 330 times lower system energy compared to baseline SNNs, and over 90 percent fewer synaptic operations across different datasets. These results validate SPARQ as a hardware-friendly, energy-efficient solution for real-time AI at the edge.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPARQ：面向节能边缘AI的脉冲早期退出神经网络
脉冲神经网络（SNN）凭借其事件驱动的计算模型具有天然的能效优势，在边缘AI部署中前景广阔。然而，深度架构的计算开销和缺乏输入自适应控制限制了其实际应用。本研究提出SPARQ框架，该框架整合了脉冲计算、量化感知训练和强化学习引导的早期退出机制，以实现高效自适应推理。在MLP、LeNet和AlexNet架构上的评估表明，所提出的量化动态SNN（QDSNN）始终优于传统SNN和量化SNN（QSNN）：相比QSNN精度提升最高达5.15%，系统能耗较基准SNN降低超330倍，在不同数据集上突触操作减少超90%。这些结果验证了SPARQ作为硬件友好、高能效的边缘实时AI解决方案的有效性。

Motivated by the need for energy-efficient and adaptive edge AI, this paper introduces SPARQ, a framework that combines spiking neural networks (SNNs) with quantization-aware training and reinforcement learning-guided early exits to reduce computational overhead. The method develops Quantised Dynamic SNNs (QDSNN) to enable input-adaptive inference, optimizing both accuracy and efficiency. Experimental results on MLP, LeNet, and AlexNet show that QDSNNs achieve up to 5.15% higher accuracy than quantized SNNs, reduce system energy by over 330 times compared to baseline SNNs, and cut synaptic operations by over 90%, demonstrating significant gains for edge deployment.

Continuous-time Risk-sensitive Reinforcement Learning via Quadratic Variation Penalty
Authors: Yanwei Jia
First: 2024-04-19T03:05:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T13:09:41+00:00
Comments: 54 pages, 2 figures, 1 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper studies continuous-time risk-sensitive reinforcement learning (RL) under the entropy-regularized, exploratory diffusion process formulation with the exponential-form objective. The risk-sensitive objective arises either as the agent's risk attitude or as a distributionally robust approach against the model uncertainty. Owing to the martingale perspective in Jia and Zhou (J Mach Learn Res 24(161): 1--61, 2023) the risk-sensitive RL problem is shown to be equivalent to ensuring the martingale property of a process involving both the value function and the q-function, augmented by an additional penalty term: the quadratic variation of the value process, capturing the variability of the value-to-go along the trajectory. This characterization allows for the straightforward adaptation of existing RL algorithms developed for non-risk-sensitive scenarios to incorporate risk sensitivity by adding the realized variance of the value process. Additionally, I highlight that the conventional policy gradient representation is inadequate for risk-sensitive problems due to the nonlinear nature of quadratic variation; however, q-learning offers a solution and extends to infinite horizon settings. Finally, I prove the convergence of the proposed algorithm for Merton's investment problem and quantify the impact of temperature parameter on the behavior of the learning procedure. I also conduct simulation experiments to demonstrate how risk-sensitive RL improves the finite-sample performance in the linear-quadratic control problem.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于二次变差惩罚的连续时间风险敏感强化学习
本文研究在熵正则化、探索性扩散过程框架及指数形式目标下的连续时间风险敏感强化学习（RL）。风险敏感目标既源于智能体的风险态度，也可作为应对模型不确定性的分布鲁棒方法。基于Jia与Zhou（J Mach Learn Res 24(161): 1–61, 2023）的鞅视角，风险敏感RL问题被证明等价于保证一个包含价值函数与q函数的过程的鞅性质，并附加一个惩罚项：价值过程的二次变差，用于捕捉轨迹中未来价值的变异性。这一特性使得现有非风险敏感RL算法能通过添加价值过程的实现方差直接扩展至风险敏感场景。此外，本文指出传统策略梯度方法因二次变差的非线性本质不适用于风险敏感问题，而q学习提供了解决方案并可推广至无限时域设定。最后，作者证明了所提算法在默顿投资问题中的收敛性，量化了温度参数对学习过程行为的影响，并通过仿真实验展示了风险敏感RL在线性二次控制问题中如何提升有限样本性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses continuous-time risk-sensitive reinforcement learning, motivated by the need to incorporate risk attitudes or model uncertainty robustness into RL, using an entropy-regularized exploratory diffusion process with an exponential objective. The method leverages a martingale perspective to show equivalence between the risk-sensitive problem and ensuring martingale properties of a combined value and q-function process, augmented by a quadratic variation penalty that captures trajectory variability, enabling adaptation of existing non-risk-sensitive RL algorithms by adding realized value variance. Experimental results include proving algorithm convergence for Merton's investment problem, quantifying the impact of a temperature parameter, and simulation experiments demonstrating improved finite-sample performance in linear-quadratic control problems.
本文研究连续时间风险敏感强化学习，其动机在于将风险态度或模型不确定性鲁棒性纳入强化学习，采用基于熵正则化的探索性扩散过程与指数形式目标。方法利用鞅视角，证明风险敏感问题等价于确保结合价值函数与q函数的过程的鞅性质，并增加捕获轨迹变异性的二次变差惩罚项，从而可通过添加已实现价值方差来适配现有非风险敏感强化学习算法。实验结果包括证明算法在默顿投资问题中的收敛性，量化温度参数对学习过程的影响，并通过仿真实验展示风险敏感强化学习在线性二次控制问题中提升有限样本性能。
AgroNVILA: Perception-Reasoning Decoupling for Multi-view Agricultural Multimodal Large Language Models
Authors: Jiarui Zhang, Junqi Hu, Zurong Mai, Yuhang Chen, Shuohong Lou, Henglian Huang, Lingyuan Zhao, Jianxi Huang, Yutong Lu, Haohuan Fu, Juepeng Zheng
First: 2026-03-15T12:24:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T12:24:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agricultural multimodal reasoning requires robust spatial understanding across varying scales, from ground-level close-ups to top-down UAV and satellite imagery. Existing Multi-modal Large Language Models (MLLMs) suffer from a significant "terrestrial-centric" bias, causing scale confusion and logic drift during complex agricultural planning. To address this, we introduce the first large-scale AgroOmni (288K), a multi-view training corpus designed to capture diverse spatial topologies and scales in modern precision agriculture. Built on this dataset, we propose AgroNVILA, an MLLM that utilizes a novel Perception-Reasoning Decoupling (PRD) architecture. On the perception side, we incorporate a View-Conditioned Meta-Net (VCMN), which injects macroscopic spatial context into visual tokens, resolving scale ambiguities with minimal computational overhead. On the reasoning side, Agriculture-aware Relative Policy Optimization (ARPO) leverages reinforcement learning to align the model's decision-making with expert agricultural logic, preventing statistical shortcuts. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AgroNVILA outperforms state-of-the-art MLLMs, achieving significant improvements (+15.18%) in multi-altitude agricultural reasoning, reflecting its robust capability for holistic agricultural spatial planning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AgroNVILA：面向多视角农业多模态大语言模型的感知-推理解耦架构
农业多模态推理需具备跨尺度的稳健空间理解能力，涵盖从地面特写至无人机与卫星的俯视影像。现有多模态大语言模型存在显著的'陆地中心'偏差，导致复杂农业规划中出现尺度混淆与逻辑漂移。为此，我们首次构建了大规模多视角训练语料库AgroOmni（288K），旨在捕捉现代精准农业中的多样化空间拓扑与尺度特征。基于此数据集，我们提出采用感知-推理解耦架构的AgroNVILA模型：感知端引入视图条件元网络，将宏观空间上下文注入视觉标记，以最小计算开销解决尺度歧义；推理端采用农业感知相对策略优化，通过强化学习使模型决策与专家农业逻辑对齐，避免统计捷径。大量实验表明，AgroNVILA在多海拔农业推理任务中显著优于现有最优模型（提升15.18%），展现出对整体农业空间规划的强健能力。

This architecture includes a View-Conditioned Meta-Net to inject spatial context for resolving scale ambiguities and Agriculture-aware Relative Policy Optimization to align decision-making with expert logic. Efficient Neural Combinatorial Optimization Solver for the Min-max Heterogeneous Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem
Authors: Xuan Wu, Di Wang, Chunguo Wu, Kaifang Qi, Chunyan Miao, Yubin Xiao, Jian Zhang, You Zhou
First: 2025-07-28T23:38:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T12:14:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Numerous Neural Combinatorial Optimization (NCO) solvers have been proposed to address Vehicle Routing Problems (VRPs). However, most of these solvers focus exclusively on single-vehicle VRP variants, overlooking the more realistic min-max Heterogeneous Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem (MMHCVRP), which involves multiple vehicles. Existing MMHCVRP solvers typically select a vehicle and its next node to visit at each decoding step, but often make myopic decoding decisions and overlook key properties of MMHCVRP, including local topological relationships, vehicle permutation invariance, and node symmetry, resulting in suboptimal performance. To better address these limitations, we propose ECHO, an efficient NCO solver. First, ECHO exploits the proposed dual-modality node encoder to capture local topological relationships among nodes. Subsequently, to mitigate myopic decisions, ECHO employs the proposed Parameter-Free Cross-Attention mechanism to prioritize the vehicle selected in the preceding decoding step. Finally, leveraging vehicle permutation invariance and node symmetry, we introduce a tailored data augment strategy for MMHCVRP to stabilize the Reinforcement Learning training process. To assess the performance of ECHO, we conduct extensive experiments. The experimental results demonstrate that ECHO outperforms state-of-the-art NCO solvers across varying numbers of vehicles and nodes, and exhibits well-performing generalization across both scales and distribution patterns. Finally, ablation studies validate the effectiveness of all proposed methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向最小-最大异构容量车辆路径问题的高效神经组合优化求解器
已有众多神经组合优化求解器被提出以应对车辆路径问题，但大多仅关注单车辆变体，忽略了更贴近实际的多车辆最小-最大异构容量车辆路径问题。现有求解器通常在解码步骤中依次选择车辆及访问节点，但往往做出短视决策，且忽视了该问题的关键特性——局部拓扑关系、车辆排列不变性与节点对称性，导致性能欠佳。为此，我们提出高效求解器ECHO：首先通过双模态节点编码器捕捉节点间局部拓扑关系；其次采用无参数交叉注意力机制优先处理前序解码步骤所选车辆，以缓解短视决策；最后利用车辆排列不变性与节点对称性，设计针对性数据增强策略以稳定强化学习训练。大量实验表明，ECHO在不同车辆与节点规模下均优于当前最优神经组合优化求解器，并在规模与分布模式上展现出良好泛化能力。消融实验验证了所提方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of existing Neural Combinatorial Optimization (NCO) solvers, which typically focus on single-vehicle routing problems and perform poorly on the more realistic min-max Heterogeneous Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem (MMHCVRP) due to myopic decoding decisions and overlooked problem properties. The proposed method, ECHO, introduces a dual-modality node encoder to capture local topological relationships, a Parameter-Free Cross-Attention mechanism to reduce myopic decisions by prioritizing the previously selected vehicle, and a tailored data augmentation strategy leveraging vehicle permutation invariance and node symmetry to stabilize Reinforcement Learning training. Experimental results show that ECHO outperforms state-of-the-art NCO solvers across different numbers of vehicles and nodes, with strong generalization in scale and distribution, and ablation studies confirm the effectiveness of each component.

Data-Driven Physics Embedded Dynamics with Predictive Control and Reinforcement Learning for Quadrupeds
Authors: Prakrut Kotecha, Aditya Shirwatkar, Shishir Kolathaya
First: 2026-03-15T11:52:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T11:52:14+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State of the art quadrupedal locomotion approaches integrate Model Predictive Control (MPC) with Reinforcement Learning (RL), enabling complex motion capabilities with planning and terrain adaptive behaviors. However, they often face compounding errors over long horizons and have limited interpretability due to the absence of physical inductive biases. We address these issues by integrating Lagrangian Neural Networks (LNNs) into an RL MPC framework, enabling physically consistent dynamics learning. At deployment, our inverse dynamics infinite horizon MPC scheme avoids costly matrix inversions, improving computational efficiency by up to 4x with minimal loss of task performance. We validate our framework through multiple ablations of the proposed LNN and its variants. We show improved sample efficiency, reduced long-horizon error, and faster real time planning compared to unstructured neural dynamics. Lastly, we also test our framework on the Unitree Go1 robot to show real world viability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：数据驱动物理嵌入动力学与预测控制及强化学习在四足机器人中的应用
当前最先进的四足机器人运动方法将模型预测控制（MPC）与强化学习（RL）相结合，实现了具备规划与地形适应能力的复杂运动能力。然而，这些方法在长时域中常面临误差累积问题，且因缺乏物理归纳偏置而可解释性有限。我们通过将拉格朗日神经网络（LNNs）集成到RL-MPC框架中来解决这些问题，实现了物理一致的动力学学习。在部署阶段，我们的逆动力学无限时域MPC方案避免了昂贵的矩阵求逆运算，将计算效率提升高达4倍，同时任务性能损失极小。我们通过对所提LNN及其变体的多项消融实验验证了该框架，结果表明：与非结构化神经动力学方法相比，我们的方法提升了样本效率、减少了长时域误差，并实现了更快的实时规划。最后，我们还在宇树Go1机器人上测试了该框架，证明了其实际应用的可行性。

This paper addresses the issues of compounding errors and limited interpretability in state-of-the-art quadrupedal locomotion, which combines Model Predictive Control (MPC) and Reinforcement Learning (RL), by integrating Lagrangian Neural Networks (LNNs) to learn physically consistent dynamics. The method employs an inverse dynamics infinite horizon MPC scheme that avoids costly matrix inversions, improving computational efficiency by up to 4x with minimal performance loss. Experimental results from ablations and real-world tests on a Unitree Go1 robot demonstrate improved sample efficiency, reduced long-horizon error, and faster real-time planning compared to unstructured neural dynamics, confirming the framework's viability.

Retrieval-augmented Decoding for Improving Truthfulness in Open-ended Generation
Authors: Manh Nguyen, Sunil Gupta, Hung Le
First: 2025-08-04T08:28:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T10:35:33+00:00
Comments: updated experiments and presentation
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Ensuring truthfulness in large language models (LLMs) remains a critical challenge for reliable text generation. While supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning with human feedback have shown promise, they require a substantial amount of annotated data and computational resources, limiting scalability. In contrast, decoding-time interventions offer lightweight alternatives without model retraining. However, existing decoding strategies often face issues like prompt sensitivity, limited generalization, or dependence on internal model states. We propose Retrieval-Augmented Decoding (RAD), a context-aware adaptive decoding method that leverages a compact reference grounding space built from as few as 10 annotated examples and comprising pairs of context embeddings and next-token logits from truthful responses, to enable retrieval-based logit shaping during inference. At each decoding step, RAD retrieves high-quality semantically similar contexts from this grounding space and aggregates their associated next token logits to modify the model's current logits. Across four open-ended generation benchmarks and four LLMs, our method consistently outperforms strong baselines and shows robust cross-task generalization, underscoring the promise of context-aware decoding for enhancing factual reliability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：检索增强解码：提升开放域生成的真实性
确保大语言模型（LLM）生成文本的真实性仍是可靠文本生成的关键挑战。尽管监督微调和基于人类反馈的强化学习展现出潜力，但它们需要大量标注数据和计算资源，限制了可扩展性。相比之下，解码时干预提供了无需模型重训练的轻量级替代方案。然而，现有解码策略常面临提示敏感性、泛化能力有限或依赖内部模型状态等问题。我们提出检索增强解码（RAD），一种上下文感知的自适应解码方法，利用仅需10个标注样本构建的紧凑参考基础空间（包含真实响应的上下文嵌入和下一词元对数概率对），在推理过程中实现基于检索的对数概率调整。在每个解码步骤中，RAD从该基础空间检索语义相似的高质量上下文，并聚合其关联的下一词元对数概率以修正模型当前对数概率。在四个开放域生成基准和四种LLM上的实验表明，本方法持续优于强基线，并展现出稳健的跨任务泛化能力，凸显了上下文感知解码在提升事实可靠性方面的潜力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of improving truthfulness in large language models for open-ended generation, motivated by the high costs of existing methods like supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning with human feedback. The authors propose Retrieval-Augmented Decoding (RAD), a lightweight decoding-time intervention that builds a compact reference grounding space from as few as 10 annotated examples, containing context embeddings and next-token logits from truthful responses, and uses it to retrieve and aggregate logits for adaptive logit shaping during inference. Experimental results across four benchmarks and four LLMs demonstrate that RAD consistently outperforms strong baselines and exhibits robust cross-task generalization, highlighting its effectiveness in enhancing factual reliability without model retraining.
本文针对开放域生成中大型语言模型真实性提升的挑战，其动机在于现有方法如监督微调和基于人类反馈的强化学习成本高昂。作者提出检索增强解码（RAD），这是一种轻量级的解码时干预方法，仅需10个标注示例构建一个紧凑的参考基础空间，包含真实响应的上下文嵌入和下一词元对数概率，并在推理时通过检索和聚合这些对数概率来自适应调整模型输出。在四个基准测试和四种大语言模型上的实验结果表明，RAD始终优于强基线方法，并展现出强大的跨任务泛化能力，凸显了其在无需模型重训练的情况下提升事实可靠性的潜力。
AMPED: Adaptive Multi-objective Projection for balancing Exploration and skill Diversification
Authors: Geonwoo Cho, Jaemoon Lee, Jaegyun Im, Subi Lee, Jihwan Lee, Sundong Kim
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-06T10:59:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T09:25:12+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Skill-based reinforcement learning (SBRL) enables rapid adaptation in environments with sparse rewards by pretraining a skill-conditioned policy. Effective skill learning requires jointly maximizing both exploration and skill diversity. However, existing methods often face challenges in simultaneously optimizing for these two conflicting objectives. In this work, we propose a new method, Adaptive Multi-objective Projection for balancing Exploration and skill Diversification (AMPED), which explicitly addresses both: during pre-training, a gradient-surgery projection balances the exploration and diversity gradients, and during fine-tuning, a skill selector exploits the learned diversity by choosing skills suited to downstream tasks. Our approach achieves performance that surpasses SBRL baselines across various benchmarks. Through an extensive ablation study, we identify the role of each component and demonstrate that each element in AMPED is contributing to performance. We further provide theoretical and empirical evidence that, with a greedy skill selector, greater skill diversity reduces fine-tuning sample complexity. These results highlight the importance of explicitly harmonizing exploration and diversity and demonstrate the effectiveness of AMPED in enabling robust and generalizable skill learning. Project Page: https://geonwoo.me/amped/
中文标题/摘要
标题：AMPED：自适应多目标投影平衡探索与技能多样化
基于技能的强化学习（SBRL）通过预训练技能条件策略，能够在奖励稀疏的环境中实现快速适应。有效的技能学习需要同时最大化探索性和技能多样性，但现有方法往往难以同时优化这两个相互冲突的目标。本文提出一种新方法——自适应多目标投影平衡探索与技能多样化（AMPED），其通过两阶段机制显式处理该问题：预训练阶段采用梯度手术投影平衡探索与多样性梯度；微调阶段通过技能选择器利用习得的多样性，选取适合下游任务的技能。该方法在多个基准测试中超越了SBRL基线性能。通过详尽的消融研究，我们明确了各组件的作用，并证明AMPED的每个要素都对性能提升有所贡献。进一步的理论与实验证据表明，在贪婪技能选择器条件下，更高的技能多样性可降低微调样本复杂度。这些结果凸显了显式协调探索与多样性的重要性，并证明了AMPED在实现鲁棒且可泛化技能学习方面的有效性。项目页面：https://geonwoo.me/amped/
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge in skill-based reinforcement learning of simultaneously optimizing the conflicting objectives of exploration and skill diversity during pre-training. The proposed method, AMPED, employs an adaptive multi-objective projection technique that balances the gradients for exploration and diversity via gradient surgery, and during fine-tuning, it uses a skill selector to leverage the learned diversity for downstream tasks. Experimental results show that AMPED outperforms existing baselines across multiple benchmarks, with ablation studies confirming the contribution of each component, and theoretical and empirical evidence indicates that greater skill diversity reduces fine-tuning sample complexity when using a greedy selector.
本文的动机源于技能强化学习中，在预训练阶段同时优化探索和技能多样性这两个冲突目标所面临的挑战。提出的AMPED方法采用自适应多目标投影技术，通过梯度手术平衡探索和多样性的梯度，并在微调阶段使用技能选择器利用学习到的多样性来适应下游任务。实验结果表明，AMPED在多个基准测试中超越了现有基线，消融研究证实了各组成部分的贡献，理论和实证证据表明，在使用贪婪选择器时，更高的技能多样性可以降低微调的样本复杂度。
TRACED: Transition-aware Regret Approximation with Co-learnability for Environment Design
Authors: Geonwoo Cho, Jaegyun Im, Jihwan Lee, Hojun Yi, Sejin Kim, Sundong Kim
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-24T20:29:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T09:16:57+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generalizing deep reinforcement learning agents to unseen environments remains a significant challenge. One promising solution is Unsupervised Environment Design (UED), a co-evolutionary framework in which a teacher adaptively generates tasks with high learning potential, while a student learns a robust policy from this evolving curriculum. Existing UED methods typically measure learning potential via regret, the gap between optimal and current performance, approximated solely by value-function loss. Building on these approaches, we introduce the transition-prediction error as an additional term in our regret approximation. To capture how training on one task affects performance on others, we further propose a lightweight metric called Co-Learnability. By combining these two measures, we present Transition-aware Regret Approximation with Co-learnability for Environment Design (TRACED). Empirical evaluations show that TRACED produces curricula that improve zero-shot generalization over strong baselines across multiple benchmarks. Ablation studies confirm that the transition-prediction error drives rapid complexity ramp-up and that Co-Learnability delivers additional gains when paired with the transition-prediction error. These results demonstrate how refined regret approximation and explicit modeling of task relationships can be leveraged for sample-efficient curriculum design in UED. Project Page: https://geonwoo.me/traced/
中文标题/摘要
标题：TRACED：面向环境设计的具备协同可学习性的转移感知遗憾近似方法
将深度强化学习智能体泛化至未见环境仍是一项重大挑战。无监督环境设计（UED）作为一种协同进化框架，通过教师自适应生成具有高学习潜力的任务，学生则从这一动态课程中学习鲁棒策略，为解决该问题提供了可行路径。现有UED方法通常通过遗憾（最优性能与当前表现的差距）来衡量学习潜力，且仅依赖价值函数损失进行近似。基于此，我们引入转移预测误差作为遗憾近似的新增项。为捕捉单任务训练对其他任务性能的影响，我们进一步提出轻量级指标“协同可学习性”。结合这两项度量，我们提出了面向环境设计的具备协同可学习性的转移感知遗憾近似方法（TRACED）。实证评估表明，TRACED生成的课程在多个基准测试中实现了优于强基线的零样本泛化能力。消融研究证实：转移预测误差能驱动复杂度快速提升，而协同可学习性与该误差结合可带来额外增益。这些结果证明，通过精化遗憾近似与显式建模任务关联，可在UED中实现样本高效的课程设计。项目页面：https://geonwoo.me/traced/
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of generalizing deep reinforcement learning agents to unseen environments, this paper introduces TRACED, a method for Unsupervised Environment Design (UED) that refines the approximation of regret—a measure of learning potential—by incorporating transition-prediction error alongside a novel lightweight metric called Co-Learnability to model how training on one task affects performance on others. The method combines these two measures to generate adaptive curricula. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that TRACED improves zero-shot generalization over strong baselines, with ablation studies confirming that the transition-prediction error drives rapid complexity increase and Co-Learnability provides additional gains when paired with it, highlighting the benefits of refined regret approximation and explicit task relationship modeling for sample-efficient curriculum design.
本文针对深度强化学习智能体在未见环境中泛化的挑战，提出了TRACED方法，用于无监督环境设计（UED）。该方法通过将转移预测误差与一种名为“共学习性”的轻量级度量相结合，改进了对遗憾（衡量学习潜力的指标）的近似，从而建模任务间训练效果的相互影响。实验结果表明，TRACED在多个基准测试中相比强基线提升了零样本泛化能力，消融研究证实转移预测误差能驱动任务复杂度快速上升，而共学习性与其结合可带来额外收益，这体现了精细的遗憾近似和显式任务关系建模对样本高效课程设计的价值。
DRL-Based Beam Positioning for LEO Satellite Constellations with Weighted Least Squares
Authors: Po-Heng Chou, Chiapin Wang, Kuan-Hao Chen, Wei-Chen Hsiao
First: 2025-11-12T00:14:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T08:43:29+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 3 figures, 1 table, accepted by 2026 IEEE ICC Workshops
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates a lightweight deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-assisted weighting framework for CSI-free multi-satellite positioning in LEO constellations, where each visible satellite provides one serving beam (one pilot response) per epoch. A discrete-action Deep Q-Network (DQN) learns satellite weights directly from received pilot measurements and geometric features, while an augmented weighted least squares (WLS) estimator provides physics-consistent localization and jointly estimates the receiver clock bias. The proposed hybrid design targets an accuracy-runtime trade-off rather than absolute supervised optimality. In a representative 2-D setting with 10 visible satellites, the proposed approach achieves sub-meter accuracy (0.395m RMSE) with low computational overhead, supporting practical deployment for resource-constrained LEO payloads.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的加权最小二乘低轨卫星星座波束定位
本文研究了一种轻量级深度强化学习辅助的加权框架，用于低轨星座中无需信道状态信息的多卫星定位，其中每颗可见卫星每周期提供一个服务波束（一个导频响应）。离散动作深度Q网络直接从接收的导频测量值和几何特征中学习卫星权重，而增强的加权最小二乘估计器提供物理一致的位置估计，并联合估计接收机时钟偏差。所提出的混合设计旨在权衡精度与运行时间，而非追求绝对监督最优性。在具有10颗可见卫星的代表性二维场景中，该方法以较低计算开销实现了亚米级精度（0.395米均方根误差），支持资源受限低轨载荷的实际部署。

This paper is motivated by the need for efficient and accurate beam positioning in LEO satellite constellations, particularly for resource-constrained payloads. Incentivizing Strong Reasoning from Weak Supervision
Authors: Yige Yuan, Teng Xiao, Shuchang Tao, Xue Wang, Jinyang Gao, Bolin Ding, Bingbing Xu
First: 2025-05-26T14:51:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T07:30:35+00:00
Comments: Accepted at EACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive performance on reasoning-intensive tasks, but enhancing their reasoning abilities typically relies on either reinforcement learning (RL) with verifiable signals or supervised fine-tuning (SFT) with high-quality long chain-of-thought (CoT) demonstrations, both of which are expensive. In this paper, we study a novel problem of incentivizing the reasoning capacity of LLMs without expensive high-quality demonstrations and reinforcement learning. We investigate whether the reasoning capabilities of LLMs can be effectively incentivized via supervision from significantly weaker models. We further analyze when and why such weak supervision succeeds in eliciting reasoning abilities in stronger models. Our findings show that supervision from significantly weaker reasoners can substantially improve student reasoning performance, recovering close to 94% of the gains of expensive RL at a fraction of the cost. Experiments across diverse benchmarks and model architectures demonstrate that weak reasoners can effectively incentivize reasoning in stronger student models, consistently improving performance across a wide range of reasoning tasks. Our results suggest that this simple weak-to-strong paradigm is a promising and generalizable alternative to costly methods for incentivizing strong reasoning capabilities at inference-time in LLMs. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/yuanyige/w2sr.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用弱监督激励强推理能力
大语言模型（LLMs）在推理密集型任务上展现出卓越性能，但提升其推理能力通常依赖于两种昂贵方法：一是基于可验证信号的强化学习（RL），二是使用高质量长链思维（CoT）演示的监督微调（SFT）。本文研究了一个新颖问题：如何在不依赖昂贵高质量演示和强化学习的情况下激励LLMs的推理能力。我们探讨了能否通过显著弱于目标模型的监督有效激励LLMs的推理能力，并进一步分析了这种弱监督何时及为何能激发更强模型的推理潜力。实验表明，来自显著较弱推理模型的监督能大幅提升学生模型的推理性能，以极低成本实现了昂贵强化学习约94%的收益增益。跨多种基准测试和模型架构的实验证明，弱推理模型能有效激励更强学生模型的推理能力，在广泛推理任务中持续提升性能。这些结果表明，这种简单的“弱到强”范式是一种具有前景且可泛化的替代方案，能以较低成本在推理阶段激励LLMs的强推理能力。代码已公开于https://github.com/yuanyige/w2sr。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of enhancing large language models' reasoning abilities without costly high-quality demonstrations or reinforcement learning, motivated by the expense of existing methods. The proposed method investigates whether supervision from significantly weaker models can effectively incentivize reasoning in stronger student models, analyzing the conditions for success. Experimental results across diverse benchmarks show that weak supervision recovers close to 94% of the gains from expensive reinforcement learning at a fraction of the cost, consistently improving performance on a wide range of reasoning tasks, suggesting this weak-to-strong paradigm is a promising and generalizable alternative.
本文旨在解决无需昂贵高质量演示或强化学习来增强大语言模型推理能力的挑战，动机在于现有方法成本高昂。所提出的方法研究来自显著较弱模型的监督是否能有效激励更强学生模型的推理，并分析其成功条件。实验结果表明，弱监督以极低成本恢复了昂贵强化学习约94%的收益，在多样化基准测试中持续提升广泛推理任务的性能，表明这种弱到强范式是一种有前景且可推广的替代方案。
Combining Tree-Search, Generative Models, and Nash Bargaining Concepts in Game-Theoretic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zun Li, Marc Lanctot, Kevin R. McKee, Luke Marris, Ian Gemp, Daniel Hennes, Paul Muller, Kate Larson, Yoram Bachrach, Michael P. Wellman
Venue: IJCAI
First: 2023-02-01T23:06:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T07:01:36+00:00
Comments: Accepted by IJCAI'25 main track
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Opponent modeling methods typically involve two crucial steps: building a belief distribution over opponents' strategies, and exploiting this opponent model by playing a best response. However, existing approaches typically require domain-specific heurstics to come up with such a model, and algorithms for approximating best responses are hard to scale in large, imperfect information domains. In this work, we introduce a scalable and generic multiagent training regime for opponent modeling using deep game-theoretic reinforcement learning. We first propose Generative Best Respoonse (GenBR), a best response algorithm based on Monte-Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) with a learned deep generative model that samples world states during planning. This new method scales to large imperfect information domains and can be plug and play in a variety of multiagent algorithms. We use this new method under the framework of Policy Space Response Oracles (PSRO), to automate the generation of an \emph{offline opponent model} via iterative game-theoretic reasoning and population-based training. We propose using solution concepts based on bargaining theory to build up an opponent mixture, which we find identifying profiles that are near the Pareto frontier. Then GenBR keeps updating an \emph{online opponent model} and reacts against it during gameplay. We conduct behavioral studies where human participants negotiate with our agents in Deal-or-No-Deal, a class of bilateral bargaining games. Search with generative modeling finds stronger policies during both training time and test time, enables online Bayesian co-player prediction, and can produce agents that achieve comparable social welfare and Nash bargaining score negotiating with humans as humans trading among themselves.
中文标题/摘要
标题：博弈论强化学习中结合树搜索、生成模型与纳什议价概念的研究
对手建模方法通常包含两个关键步骤：构建对手策略的信念分布，以及通过最优响应策略利用该对手模型。然而，现有方法通常需要领域特定的启发式规则来构建此类模型，且近似最优响应的算法在大型非完美信息领域中难以扩展。本研究提出一种基于深度博弈论强化学习的可扩展通用多智能体对手建模训练框架。我们首先提出生成式最优响应算法，这是一种基于蒙特卡洛树搜索的最优响应算法，通过学习的深度生成模型在规划过程中采样世界状态。这种新方法可扩展至大型非完美信息领域，并能即插即用于多种多智能体算法。我们将该方法应用于策略空间响应预言框架，通过迭代博弈论推理与基于种群的训练，实现离线对手模型的自动化生成。我们提出基于议价理论的解概念来构建对手混合策略，该策略能识别接近帕累托边界的策略剖面。随后，生成式最优响应算法持续更新在线对手模型并在博弈过程中实时应对。通过在双边议价游戏类别的'成交与否'游戏中开展人类与智能体谈判的行为实验，研究表明：结合生成模型的搜索方法在训练与测试阶段均能发现更强策略，支持在线贝叶斯协同玩家预测，且所构建的智能体与人类谈判时，可获得与人类间交易相当的社会福利与纳什议价分数。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses scalability and generalization issues in opponent modeling for multiagent systems, where existing methods rely on domain-specific heuristics and struggle in large imperfect-information games. The authors propose a novel approach combining Generative Best Response (GenBR), which integrates Monte-Carlo Tree Search with a deep generative model to sample world states during planning, and Policy Space Response Oracles (PSRO) for iterative opponent modeling, enhanced by Nash bargaining concepts to build opponent mixtures near the Pareto frontier. Experimental results in bilateral bargaining games, such as Deal-or-No-Deal with human participants, demonstrate that GenBR yields stronger policies during training and testing, enables effective online Bayesian co-player prediction, and achieves social welfare and Nash bargaining scores comparable to human-human negotiations.
本文针对多智能体系统中对手建模的可扩展性和泛化性问题，现有方法通常依赖领域特定启发式且难以应对大规模不完全信息博弈。作者提出了一种新方法，结合了生成式最佳响应（GenBR）——通过蒙特卡洛树搜索与深度生成模型在规划中采样世界状态，以及策略空间响应预言（PSRO）进行迭代对手建模，并引入纳什讨价还价概念以构建接近帕累托边界的对手混合策略。在双边讨价还价游戏（如“成交或不成交”与人类参与者）中的实验结果表明，GenBR在训练和测试期间能产生更强策略，实现有效的在线贝叶斯对手预测，且其智能体与人类谈判时获得的社会福利和纳什讨价还价分数与人类间谈判相当。
GoldenStart: Q-Guided Priors and Entropy Control for Distilling Flow Policies
Authors: He Zhang, Ying Sun, Hui Xiong
First: 2026-03-15T06:39:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T06:39:09+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 13 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Flow-matching policies hold great promise for reinforcement learning (RL) by capturing complex, multi-modal action distributions. However, their practical application is often hindered by prohibitive inference latency and ineffective online exploration. Although recent works have employed one-step distillation for fast inference, the structure of the initial noise distribution remains an overlooked factor that presents significant untapped potential. This overlooked factor, along with the challenge of controlling policy stochasticity, constitutes two critical areas for advancing distilled flow-matching policies. To overcome these limitations, we propose GoldenStart (GSFlow), a policy distillation method with Q-guided priors and explicit entropy control. Instead of initializing generation from uninformed noise, we introduce a Q-guided prior modeled by a conditional VAE. This state-conditioned prior repositions the starting points of the one-step generation process into high-Q regions, effectively providing a "golden start" that shortcuts the policy to promising actions. Furthermore, for effective online exploration, we enable our distilled actor to output a stochastic distribution instead of a deterministic point. This is governed by entropy regularization, allowing the policy to shift from pure exploitation to principled exploration. Our integrated framework demonstrates that by designing the generative startpoint and explicitly controlling policy entropy, it is possible to achieve efficient and exploratory policies, bridging the generative models and the practical actor-critic methods. We conduct extensive experiments on offline and online continuous control benchmarks, where our method significantly outperforms prior state-of-the-art approaches. Code will be available at https://github.com/ZhHe11/GSFlow-RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GoldenStart：基于Q引导先验与熵控制的流策略蒸馏方法
流匹配策略通过捕捉复杂多峰动作分布，为强化学习带来巨大潜力，但其实际应用常受限于高昂的推理延迟与低效的在线探索。尽管近期研究采用单步蒸馏实现快速推理，初始噪声分布的结构仍是未被充分挖掘的关键因素。该因素与策略随机性控制难题共同构成推进蒸馏流匹配策略发展的两大核心方向。为此，我们提出GoldenStart（GSFlow）——一种融合Q引导先验与显式熵控制的策略蒸馏方法。我们采用条件变分自编码器构建Q引导先验，替代传统无信息噪声初始化，将单步生成起点重新定位至高Q值区域，实现引导策略直达优质动作的“黄金起点”。同时，为提升在线探索效率，我们使蒸馏后的策略输出随机分布而非确定性点，通过熵正则化调控策略在利用与探索间的平衡。该集成框架表明：通过设计生成起点与显式控制策略熵，可实现高效且具备探索能力的策略，弥合生成模型与实用演员-评论员方法间的鸿沟。在离线与在线连续控制基准测试中，本方法显著超越现有最优方法。代码发布于https://github.com/ZhHe11/GSFlow-RL。

This work addresses the inference latency and exploration challenges of flow-matching policies in reinforcement learning by proposing GoldenStart (GSFlow), a distillation method incorporating Q-guided priors and entropy control. The method replaces standard noise initialization with a state-conditioned prior from a conditional VAE to start generation in high-value action regions, while entropy regularization enables stochastic outputs for exploration. Experimental results on continuous control benchmarks demonstrate that this integrated approach outperforms prior state-of-the-art methods in both offline and online settings.

Slow-Fast Policy Optimization: Reposition-Before-Update for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Ziyan Wang, Zheng Wang, Jie Fu, Xingwei Qu, Qi Cheng, Shengpu Tang, Minjia Zhang, Xiaoming Huo
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-05T07:22:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T05:57:00+00:00
Comments: Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become central to enhancing reasoning in large language models (LLMs). Yet on-policy algorithms such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) often suffer in early training: noisy gradients from low-quality rollouts lead to unstable updates and inefficient exploration. We introduce Slow-Fast Policy Optimization (SFPO), a simple yet efficient framework to address the above limitations via decomposing each step into three stages: a short fast trajectory of inner steps on the same batch, a reposition mechanism to control off-policy drift, and a final slow correction. This reposition-before-update design preserves the objective and rollout process unchanged, making SFPO plug-compatible with existing policy-gradient pipelines. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SFPO consistently improves stability, reduces number of rollouts, and accelerates convergence of reasoning RL training. Specifically, it outperforms GRPO by up to 2.80 points in average on math reasoning benchmarks. It also achieves up to 4.93\texttimes{} fewer rollouts and an up to 4.19\texttimes{} reduction in wall-clock time to match GRPO's best accuracy. Project website is available at https://slow-fast-po.github.io/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：慢快策略优化：面向大语言模型推理的“重定位-后更新”方法
强化学习已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的核心技术。然而，如组相对策略优化等在线策略算法在训练初期常面临挑战：低质量轨迹产生的噪声梯度导致更新不稳定与探索低效。本文提出慢快策略优化框架，通过将每步分解为三个阶段来应对上述局限：在同一批次内执行短时快速轨迹的内部步骤、控制离策略偏移的重定位机制、以及最终的慢速校正。这种“先重定位后更新”的设计保持目标函数与轨迹生成过程不变，使SFPO可直接兼容现有策略梯度流程。大量实验表明，SFPO能持续提升训练稳定性、减少轨迹采样次数并加速推理强化学习的收敛。具体而言，在数学推理基准测试中平均优于GRPO达2.80分；为达到GRPO最佳精度，所需轨迹采样次数最多减少4.93倍，实际训练时间最多缩短4.19倍。项目网站详见https://slow-fast-po.github.io/。

Eva-VLA: Evaluating Vision-Language-Action Models' Robustness Under Real-World Physical Variations
Authors: Hanqing Liu, Shouwei Ruan, Jiahuan Long, Junqi Wu, Jiacheng Hou, Huili Tang, Tingsong Jiang, Weien Zhou, Wen Yao
First: 2025-09-23T13:02:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T05:21:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have emerged as promising solutions for robotic manipulation, yet their robustness to real-world physical variations remains critically underexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose Eva-VLA, the first unified framework to systematically evaluate the robustness of VLA models by formulating uncontrollable physical variations as continuous optimization problems. Specifically, our framework addresses two fundamental challenges in VLA models' physical robustness evaluation: 1) how to systematically characterize diverse physical perturbations encountered in real-world deployment while maintaining reproducibility, and 2) how to efficiently discover worst-case scenarios without incurring prohibitive real-world data collection costs. To tackle the first challenge, we decouple real-world variations into three key dimensions: 3D object transformations that affect spatial reasoning, illumination changes that challenge visual perception, and adversarial regions that disrupt scene understanding. For the second challenge, we introduce a continuous black-box optimization mechanism that maps these perturbations into a continuous parameter space, enabling the systematic exploration of worst-case scenarios. Extensive experiments validate the effectiveness of our approach. Notably, OpenVLA exhibits an average failure rate of over 90% across three physical variations on the LIBERO-Long task, exposing critical systemic fragilities. Furthermore, applying the generated worst-case scenarios during adversarial training quantifiably increases model robustness, validating the effectiveness of this approach. Our evaluation exposes the gap between laboratory and real-world conditions, while the Eva-VLA framework can serve as an effective data augmentation method to enhance the resilience of robotic manipulation systems.

视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型已成为机器人操控领域有前景的解决方案，但其对真实世界物理变化的鲁棒性仍严重缺乏探索。为填补这一空白，我们提出Eva-VLA——首个通过将不可控物理变化建模为连续优化问题来系统评估VLA模型鲁棒性的统一框架。该框架重点解决VLA模型物理鲁棒性评估中的两大核心挑战：1）如何在保持可复现性的同时系统化表征真实部署中遇到的多样化物理扰动；2）如何在不产生高昂真实数据采集成本的前提下高效发现最坏情况场景。针对第一项挑战，我们将真实世界变化解耦为三个关键维度：影响空间推理的3D物体变换、挑战视觉感知的照明变化，以及破坏场景理解的对抗性区域。针对第二项挑战，我们引入连续黑盒优化机制，将这些扰动映射到连续参数空间，从而系统探索最坏情况场景。大量实验验证了本方法的有效性：在LIBERO-Long任务中，OpenVLA模型在三种物理变化下的平均故障率超过90%，暴露出关键的系统脆弱性。此外，在对抗训练中应用生成的最坏情况场景可量化提升模型鲁棒性。本评估揭示了实验室与真实环境间的差距，而Eva-VLA框架可作为增强机器人操控系统适应性的有效数据增强方法。
