Learning to Generate Unit Test via Adversarial Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dongjun Lee, Changho Hwang, Kimin Lee
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-08-28T14:32:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T04:29:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026. Code is available at: https://github.com/dgjun32/UTRL
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Unit testing is a core practice in programming, enabling systematic evaluation of programs produced by human developers or large language models (LLMs). Given the challenges in writing comprehensive unit tests, LLMs have been employed to automate test generation, yet methods for training LLMs to produce high-quality tests remain underexplored. In this work, we propose UTRL, a novel reinforcement learning framework that trains an LLM to generate high-quality unit tests given a programming instruction. Our key idea is to iteratively train two LLMs, the unit test generator and the code generator, in an adversarial manner via reinforcement learning. The unit test generator is trained to maximize a discrimination reward, which reflects its ability to produce tests that expose faults in the code generator's solutions, and the code generator is trained to maximize a code reward, which reflects its ability to produce solutions that pass the unit tests generated by the test generator. In our experiments, we demonstrate that unit tests generated by Qwen3-4B trained via UTRL show higher quality compared to unit tests generated by the same model trained via supervised fine-tuning on human-written ground-truth unit tests, yielding code evaluations that more closely align with those induced by the ground-truth tests. Moreover, Qwen3-4B trained with UTRL outperforms frontier models such as GPT-4.1 in generating high-quality unit tests, highlighting the effectiveness of UTRL in training LLMs for this task.

标题：通过对抗性强化学习生成单元测试
单元测试是编程中的核心实践，用于系统评估人类开发者或大语言模型（LLM）生成的程序。鉴于编写全面单元测试的挑战，已有研究利用LLM自动化测试生成，但训练LLM生成高质量测试的方法仍待深入探索。本研究提出UTRL——一种新颖的强化学习框架，用于训练LLM根据编程指令生成高质量单元测试。核心思想是通过强化学习以对抗方式迭代训练两个LLM：单元测试生成器和代码生成器。测试生成器的训练目标是最大化判别奖励（反映其生成能暴露代码生成器解决方案缺陷的测试的能力），代码生成器则最大化代码奖励（反映其生成能通过测试生成器所产测试的解决方案的能力）。实验表明，通过UTRL训练的Qwen3-4B生成的单元测试，相较于基于人工编写真实测试进行监督微调的同模型版本，展现出更高质量，其代码评估结果与真实测试的评估更接近。此外，经UTRL训练的Qwen3-4B在生成高质量单元测试方面优于GPT-4.1等前沿模型，凸显了UTRL在此任务中训练LLM的有效性。

Flow-Factory: A Unified Framework for Reinforcement Learning in Flow-Matching Models
Authors: Bowen Ping, Chengyou Jia, Minnan Luo, Hangwei Qian, Ivor Tsang
First: 2026-02-13T02:21:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T01:41:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has emerged as a promising paradigm for aligning diffusion and flow-matching models with human preferences, yet practitioners face fragmented codebases, model-specific implementations, and engineering complexity. We introduce Flow-Factory, a unified framework that decouples algorithms, models, and rewards through through a modular, registry-based architecture. This design enables seamless integration of new algorithms and architectures, as demonstrated by our support for GRPO, DiffusionNFT, and AWM across Flux, Qwen-Image, and WAN video models. By minimizing implementation overhead, Flow-Factory empowers researchers to rapidly prototype and scale future innovations with ease. Flow-Factory provides production-ready memory optimization, flexible multi-reward training, and seamless distributed training support. The codebase is available at https://github.com/X-GenGroup/Flow-Factory.
中文标题/摘要

Diffusion Reinforcement Learning via Centered Reward Distillation
Authors: Yuanzhi Zhu, Xi Wang, Stéphane Lathuilière, Vicky Kalogeiton
First: 2026-03-14T21:29:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T21:29:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion and flow models achieve State-Of-The-Art (SOTA) generative performance, yet many practically important behaviors such as fine-grained prompt fidelity, compositional correctness, and text rendering are weakly specified by score or flow matching pretraining objectives. Reinforcement Learning (RL) fine-tuning with external, black-box rewards is a natural remedy, but diffusion RL is often brittle. Trajectory-based methods incur high memory cost and high-variance gradient estimates; forward-process approaches converge faster but can suffer from distribution drift, and hence reward hacking. In this work, we present \textbf{Centered Reward Distillation (CRD)}, a diffusion RL framework derived from KL-regularized reward maximization built on forward-process-based fine-tuning. The key insight is that the intractable normalizing constant cancels under \emph{within-prompt centering}, yielding a well-posed reward-matching objective. To enable reliable text-to-image fine-tuning, we introduce techniques that explicitly control distribution drift: (\textit{i}) decoupling the sampler from the moving reference to prevent ratio-signal collapse, (\textit{ii}) KL anchoring to a CFG-guided pretrained model to control long-run drift and align with the inference-time semantics of the pre-trained model, and (\textit{iii}) reward-adaptive KL strength to accelerate early learning under large KL regularization while reducing late-stage exploitation of reward-model loopholes. Experiments on text-to-image post-training with \texttt{GenEval} and \texttt{OCR} rewards show that CRD achieves competitive SOTA reward optimization results with fast convergence and reduced reward hacking, as validated on unseen preference metrics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于中心化奖励蒸馏的扩散强化学习
扩散与流模型虽已实现最先进的生成性能，但许多实际关键行为（如细粒度提示保真度、组合正确性和文本渲染）在基于分数或流匹配的预训练目标中约束较弱。采用外部黑盒奖励的强化学习微调是自然的解决方案，但扩散强化学习常表现出脆弱性：基于轨迹的方法内存成本高且梯度估计方差大；基于前向过程的方法收敛更快，但可能受分布漂移影响而导致奖励漏洞利用。本文提出**中心化奖励蒸馏（CRD）**，这是一种基于前向过程微调、从KL正则化奖励最大化推导的扩散强化学习框架。其核心洞见在于：在**提示内中心化**条件下，难解的正则化常数可被抵消，从而得到良定义的奖励匹配目标。为实现可靠的文本到图像微调，我们引入显式控制分布漂移的技术：（i）将采样器与动态参考解耦以防止比率信号坍缩；（ii）通过KL锚定至CFG引导的预训练模型来控制长期漂移，并与预训练模型的推理时语义对齐；（iii）采用奖励自适应的KL强度，以在强KL正则化下加速早期学习，同时减少后期对奖励模型漏洞的利用。基于\texttt{GenEval}和\texttt{OCR}奖励的文本到图像后训练实验表明，CRD能以快速收敛和更低奖励漏洞利用实现具有竞争力的最先进奖励优化效果，该结论在未见偏好指标上得到验证。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the brittleness of reinforcement learning (RL) fine-tuning for diffusion models, which often suffers from distribution drift and reward hacking when optimizing for weakly specified behaviors like prompt fidelity. The authors propose Centered Reward Distillation (CRD), a diffusion RL framework derived from KL-regularized reward maximization that uses within-prompt centering to yield a well-posed reward-matching objective, and introduce techniques to control drift, including decoupling the sampler from the moving reference, KL anchoring to a pretrained model, and reward-adaptive KL strength. Experimental results on text-to-image post-training with GenEval and OCR rewards demonstrate that CRD achieves state-of-the-art reward optimization with fast convergence and reduced reward hacking, as validated on unseen preference metrics.
本文针对扩散模型强化学习微调的脆弱性问题，在优化如提示保真度等弱指定行为时，常出现分布漂移和奖励黑客攻击。作者提出了中心化奖励蒸馏（CRD），这是一个基于KL正则化奖励最大化的扩散RL框架，通过提示内中心化得到一个适定的奖励匹配目标，并引入了控制漂移的技术，包括将采样器与移动参考解耦、对预训练模型进行KL锚定以及奖励自适应的KL强度。在基于GenEval和OCR奖励的文本到图像后训练实验中，CRD实现了最先进的奖励优化效果，具有快速收敛和减少奖励黑客攻击的特点，并在未见过的偏好指标上得到了验证。
